**Method of Focused Visualization**

Whenever one wishes to recite the *Wenchang Great Cavern Scripture*, one should rise at dawn before worldly affairs intrude, bathe in fragrant waters, don fresh garments, observe purification rites, and enter the chamber. Lighting twenty candles and holding incense, face north and stand in reverent order. Recite the purifying incantation, offer fragrant smoke to the sages, state one’s intent, and perform the ritual invitation. Present nine portions of tea and fruits as offerings—if tea is unavailable, nine cups of pure water will suffice. The essential matter is utmost sincerity; rigid adherence is unnecessary.

Then, facing east, sit in repose. Draw in the vital qi of life, still the breath, and settle the mind, allowing no stray or reckless thoughts. With both eyes, inwardly behold the Yellow Court, emptying even the emptiness, until stillness is achieved. After a time, visualize the green qi within the liver transforming into a Bluegreen Dragon, standing to the left; the white qi within the lungs becoming a White Tiger, standing to the right; the red qi within the heart becoming a Vermilion Bird, standing before; and the black qi within the kidneys becoming a Dark Warrior, standing behind. One’s own body sits upon a nine-colored lotus throne, above and below which ride nine-headed lions. The Three Primordials Generals and Four Sage Marshals stand in attendance.

Next, visualize the Three Treasures of Heaven’s Center and the Nine Heavens’ Life-Generating Lord above the head, emitting nine beams of radiant light that penetrate the nine palaces of the head and the nine apertures of the body. Then, envision the thirty-two Celestial Emperors and the sixty celestial stems and earthly branches of one’s natal star officials, their light descending to illuminate the five viscera, six bowels, thirty-six palaces within the body, and extending downward to the Earth Sovereigns of the thirty-six lands, from the Bubbling Spring to the Muddy Pellet, uniting heaven and earth in luminous clarity, each detail distinct.

Next, visualize the green qi of the liver transforming into Wu Ying, the white qi of the lungs into Bai Yuan, the red qi of the heart into the Controller of Fate, the black qi of the kidneys into Tao Kang, and the Great One residing in the head—these five spirits are the ancestors of all spirits and are thus first to be visualized. If a Daoist is performing the Morning Audience, their cap and robes should correspond to the colors of the respective directions, standing in attendance to the left, right, front, and rear.

Then, visualize the ten thousand qi and ten thousand spirits, each in accordance with the method, reciting the incantations. Command the spirits with the mind while reciting with the mouth. Upon completion, begin reciting the scripture in a soft voice, without coarse breath or loud shouting, but with precise and concentrated visualization. This is the ancient immortal’s method for reciting the Three Caverns scriptures, wherein the Five Emperors’ Jade Lads and Jade Maidens attend as protectors, and the majestic spirits guard in accordance with the scripture—this must not be treated lightly.

The recorded experiences and verifications are exhaustive and may be studied and pondered in private. At times, celestial perfected beings may descend, earthly deities may witness the rite, or the spirits within one’s own body may manifest, as when Xiao Weiyi saw the Four Beasts take form—all results of meticulous visualization. Those who cherish the Dao should each adhere to these practices.

---

**Preface to the Wenchang Great Cavern Immortal Scripture**
**Preface and Mystic Concordance by the Nine Heavens’ Transformative Sovereign, the True and Luminous Treasure Radiance Heavenly Worthy**

Born in the vast kalpa, I lived as a humble laborer. One day, while tilling the soil, I unearthed a golden statue. The village elders identified it as the likeness of the Primordial Heavenly Venerable, cast in metal by the Great Yu during his flood-taming labors to pacify the sacred peaks. I honored it with incense and offerings, never once neglecting my devotion. When a sea storm surged beyond human strength to resist, I, on behalf of the people, cast the golden statue into the raging waves. Thereupon, the winds and tides receded, and the entire region was spared.

After long reflection, one night upon the sandy shoals, a light stretched across the sky. Digging, I recovered the same statue and returned it to build a temple for its veneration, where the villagers and I worshipped together. Over the years, the numinous responses were too numerous to record.

My parents, alas, perished in an epidemic. After mourning and burying them, I kept vigil at their graves, tending the mounds until they were well established. One day, three divine beings—clad in hempen headscarves, feathered robes, and straw sandals—visited me and bestowed a volume of the *Great Cavern Immortal Scripture*, saying: “Recite it morning and evening, and you will surely attain good fruits. Among the Three Powers, above, it may aid in serving your parents and ancestors, liberating their souls from dark suffering; in the middle, it may eradicate sins, dispel calamities, prolong life, and increase destiny; below, it may protect your clan and save others, ensuring collective preservation. You may offer gold and silk to us three, and we will transmit this on your behalf.”

That very day, I followed their instructions, preparing a vegetarian feast and presenting gold and silk to receive the teaching. Thereafter, I recited the scripture morning and evening without fail, repeatedly experiencing numinous responses. Once, during a sweltering summer, a great flood submerged my parents’ graves. I reverently presented the golden statue and recited the *Great Cavern Scripture*, vowing to complete a thousand recitations to ensure their safety. The following autumn, incessant rains caused the nearby streams to swell and merge. Fearing the worst, I waited for the waters to recede and saw that the valley before the graves had transformed into a broad, firm ridge over a mile wide. From then on, the pines and catalpas remained unharmed.

I often reflected on my parents’ deaths from pestilence, hating the plague demons with a bone-deep enmity. Though the paths of the living and the dead diverge, and I lacked the power to exact vengeance, I diligently recited the *Great Cavern Immortal Scripture* morning and night, praying fervently to the golden statue, beseeching it to grant me the power to subdue the plague demons.

Three years later, I suddenly dreamed that the golden statue spoke to me: “You have mastered the *Great Cavern Immortal Scripture*, but you have not yet seen the *Great Cavern Register of Methods*. Today, I shall bestow it upon you to subdue evil demons. Not only will this fulfill your original vow, but it will also aid heaven’s transformative work and assist the nation in saving the people.” From its sleeve, it produced two books, which I received with bows. One was titled *Great Cavern Register*, the other *Great Cavern Methods*. Upon waking, the two books lay before my pillow. I prepared a vegetarian feast and placed them in a repository for safekeeping.

Choosing an auspicious day, I took them out to read. Upon reaching the passage, “One myriad of the Heavenly Couriers’ armored soldiers descend,” suddenly, wind and thunder darkened the day, and countless figures in golden armor and crimson sashes arrayed themselves before me, bowing to receive my command. One holding a red banner stepped forward and said, “We await your orders.” Startled, I unconsciously raised my voice and commanded: “I require you to subdue the plague demons. The household of Prefect Zhang in this village is stricken—go and drive them out!” The banner-bearer led over a hundred soldiers into the house. In an instant, they emerged, capturing five demons: one clad in tiger skin, one crowned with a rooster, one with a human face, one with a crow’s head, and one with a donkey’s head. They wielded implements of water, fire, feathers, sickles, axes, and chisels. Enraged, I rebuked them, about to annihilate their forms.

Then they offered their defense, saying: "We, the Yuanbo and our kind, arise from the yearly cyclical movements and are formed by the annual *qi*. Our travels follow fixed directions, and our afflictions target specific people. Those who suffer grave yin retribution bear its calamity; those whose heavenly mandate is severed meet their death—this is not something we, the Yuanbo, dare claim as our own doing. It begins with the Three Officials and Five Peaks submitting a memorial to the Jade Emperor, presenting the transgressions of mortals. Thereupon, the Emperor commands the Three Officials and Five Peaks to spread disease. The Year King, according to the register, issues writs and dispatches us, the Yuanbo, to act strictly in accordance with the records. If the True Officer grants us leniency, we shall henceforth abide by your constraints. Whenever we encounter the plague, we will not dare approach wherever your talismans and scriptures reside."

Thereupon, I instructed them in accordance with the scriptural methods and sent them away. For those in the village afflicted by plague, I provided talismans and rituals, and all were preserved and revived. By means of these scriptures and talismans, I have saved countless from illness and suffering. My name spread far and wide, and scholars, commoners, officials, and clerks flocked to my door seeking cures—innumerable in number. My accumulation of profound merit and wondrous deeds all stem from upholding the *Great Cavern Scripture of the Immortals*, through which I obtained the *Great Cavern Talismans*. Thus, I fully harnessed divine efficacy, instantly rectifying and expelling evil, delivering the living, transcending the dead, dispelling misfortune, and prolonging life.

Later, in the unseen realms, mighty spirits and deities from temple altars came to beseech me to recite scriptures for their benefit, expressing gratitude: "By the power of the True Officer’s scriptures, our might and virtue have been augmented, and our names inscribed in the registers of the virtuous. Some were lingering souls and stagnant spirits unable to be reborn; they came in dreams or through possession to beg for my recitation of scriptures to aid their deliverance. All gave thanks, saying: 'By the power of the True Officer’s scriptures, we have escaped suffering and attained rebirth.'"

When seasonal epidemics spread unchecked, one need only recite this scripture and employ the talismans within its methods—*Talismans for Dispatching Plague, Severing Plague, and Halting Plague*—to command the celestial couriers and armored soldiers above, as well as the *Officers Who Seize Plague and Devour Plague, Officers Who Seize Poison and Devour Poison, Officers Who Seize Evil and Devour Evil, Officers Who Seize Qi and Devour Qi, Officers Who Seize Ghosts and Devour Ghosts, Officers Who Seize Calamity and Devour Calamity, Officers Who Seize Essences and Devour Essences, Divine Healers, Officers Who Destroy Talismans and Demolish Temples*—the Nine Ranks of the Mighty Generals of the Orthodox Unity, each leading their armored troops, along with the Five Hundred Million Black Riders of the Northern Celestial Officials, the Venerable Cang Lao, the Maiden Magu, the Vajra Warriors, and others, to capture them.

First, a writ is sent to the Year King, then a petition is submitted to Mount Tai. The City Gods and Earth Gods are delegated to dispatch the Plague Envoys. If, upon hearing the scriptures, they defy the covenant and refuse to withdraw, they are then memorialized and annihilated.

The Great Dao cherishes compassion; the Supreme Clarity is ever benevolent. The August Emperor favors life and extends mercy to halt killing. Those who practice the scriptural methods and talismans must not act with private malice or cruelty, lest they incur heavenly retribution. One should dispatch them with propriety, honor them with scriptures, awe them with talismans, and exhort them with virtuous deeds—this is the swiftest path of expedient cultivation.

Those who practice these scriptures and talismans should deliberate carefully to establish profound merit. This scripture can resolve karmic entanglements, halt retributive trials, dissolve oral curses, absolve offenses, pacify graves and dwellings, stabilize military and government offices, quell warfare, halt epidemics, pray for wind and rain, summon auspicious omens, ensure silkworm and grain harvests, protect life and body, shield clans and kin, rescue villages and communities, secure borders, restrain insects and tigers, end droughts and floods, eradicate demons and monsters, suppress collective misfortunes, repel malevolent stars and dark portents, honor ancestral sacrifices and temple deities, aid the deliverance of ancestral souls, relieve destitute spirits and stagnant souls—these constitute the twenty-four supreme merits of Wenchang, corresponding to the twenty-four *qi* of the year, for which one may hold fasts, recite scriptures, and perform rituals to avert and give thanks.

For other ailments and the eradication of poisons, there is the *Divine Prescription of the Purple Court Celestial Physician*, a remnant grace of the Golden Queen of Yu the Great, extending to all generations, sparing people from untimely deaths and freeing them from the scourge of epidemics. Those who receive these teachings should seek out and study them to attain profound merit.

I have attained the fruit of the *Most High Unassuming and Joyous Nurturing Heavenly Emperor, the Clarified and True Contemplation Treasure Radiance Compassionate Response Life-Prolonging Heavenly Worthy*, truly through diligent recitation of scriptures, thereby ascending to the nobility of the Supreme Clarity. Those who receive and recite these scriptures should strive to practice them, wishing to join all within the Wenchang assembly in ascending to wondrous deeds.

Respectfully recorded.

---

**Imperial Decree of Yuan Dynasty:**
By the Mandate of Heaven, the Sacred Edict of the Emperor:
In the manifest realm, there are rites and music; in the hidden realm, there are spirits and deities. The subtle and the evident are one in essence. In heaven, they become stars and constellations; on earth, rivers and mountains. Their forms and functions operate between the two realms, yet how could they remain concealed within the great Way? They must be honored with solemn ceremonies.

The Emperor of Wenchang of the Seven Curves Mountain’s Zhang-Dong Palace, whose light emanates from the Zhang constellation and whose friendship is praised in the *Book of Songs*, has aided our prosperous reign with loyalty and filial piety, guiding the people. He has illuminated our civil virtues with scholarly success, selecting and cultivating many talents. Whenever he has rescued us from disasters, his responsive manifestations of reward and punishment have been evident. The decrees on imperial examinations have been reissued, and the records of assessments have been predetermined. Though adorned with splendor, his fame has not yet fully satisfied our heart.

Alas! We desire an abundance of literary talent—may you brilliantly manifest the spirit of the Jiang and Han rivers. We desire civil governance—may you dredge and display the treasury of the Kui and Bi constellations. To bestow a fitting title in response to your illustrious light, you shall be additionally enfeoffed as *Imperial Lord Wenchang, Assistant Originator of Transformation, Bestower of Emoluments, and Vastly Benevolent Emperor*.

Let the relevant officials carry this out.

Issued on a day in the seventh month of the third year of the Yanyou era.

---

**Sacred Titles of the Seven Curves Mountain:**
*Celestial Master of the Golden Portal of the Vast Heaven, Inner Assistant to the Three Pure Ones and Prime Minister of the Great Supervisory Office, Commander-in-Chief of the Three Realms’ Yin Soldiers with Discretionary Powers, Overseer of the Prisons of Heaven, Earth, and Water, Holder of the Tiger Tallies and Dragon Credentials of the True Forms of the Five Peaks and Four Waterways, Director of All Celestial Stars and Constellations, Adjudicator of the Registers of Cassia and Emoluments, Supreme Immortal and Primordial Sovereign, Lord of the Five Qi of the Heavenly Terrace Elder, True Lord of Emoluments and Imperial Examinations, Compiler of the Flying Immortals’ Registers, Master of the Transformations of the Primordial Chaos and the Vast Heaven, Deliverer from Suffering Heavenly Worthy.*

His brush records no matter unaddressed; his emanations save no being unsaved. The brilliance of his ninety-five transformations is resplendent.

The Sun and Moon, saviors of the common folk through billions of myriad kalpas,
Preserve the great bonds of loyalty and filial piety, demonstrating the eternal models for ministers and children.
Radiant with autonomous majesty, embodying the Dao of non-action and virtue,
True King of Longevity of the Southern Culmen,
Sovereign of the Nine Heavens who Stabilizes the Primordial, Protects Life, Upholds the Teachings, Enlightens, and Delivers All Beings,
Perfectly Compassionate Honored One of the Ten Titles of Eternal Joy and Everlasting Blessing,
Overseer of the Affairs of Fortune and Misfortune in the Three Realms,
King Bodhisattva of Realized Fruition and Settled Wisdom,
Tathāgata of the True Form of Śakra, Brahmā, and the Thus-Come One,
Supreme Emperor of the Heaven of Unarrogant Joy and Nurturing Cultivation,
Pure Dao True One of the Inner Realm of Jade Clarity,
Manifesting in the Purple Tenuity Grotto, wielding the Ruyi Scepter,
Universally delivering from all suffering, governing the myriad spirits,
Commander-in-Chief of the Vast Heaven,
True Lord of the Myriad Heavens who Receives Sincere Devotion and Teaches All,
Heavenly Worthy of Compassionate Response to All Wishes,
Great Sage, Great Compassion, Great Benevolence, Great Filial Piety,
Boundless, Immeasurable, Most Wondrous, Most Mysterious,

Lord of Literature and Emoluments, Magnanimous Emperor of Vast Benevolence,
Ancestral Master, Heavenly Worthy of Limpid Truth and Radiant Contemplation.

Heavenly seals and favors bestowed,
The Primordial ascends the true numen.
With three hundred characters complete,
Its merit rivals the Three Caverns’ scriptures.
Immortals and transcendents transmit and chant it,
The Yin Talismans establish it as capital.
Should one hold and recite it,
Generation after generation shall enjoy prosperity and honor.

**Eulogy of the Great Cavern Scripture by the True Person Zheng Yuansou**

**Eulogizing the Treasured Scripture**
1.
The Great Cavern True Scripture is the Great Vehicle,
Profound and abstruse, reaching the ultimate mystery.
The immortals and sages of the ten directions and three times,
Through cultivation and accomplishment, attain the Primordial Azure.

**Proclaiming the Mysterious and Wondrous**
2.
The Three Caverns and Three Vehicles are not easily fathomed,
The August Emperor’s wondrous words are flawless.
All scriptures and myriad dharmas return to the ancestral origin,
Through understanding and awakening, one ascends the kalpic abode.

**Exhorting the Present Age**
3.
Emperors, ministers, and nobles,
Prefects, officials, and common folk:
Wealth, honor, glory, and splendor are no other matters,
Than to investigate the profound principles of the Great Cavern in its entirety.

**Admonishing the Three Teachings**
4.
Though the black-robed and yellow-robed teachings differ in path,
Those who hear rites and hear poetry are gentlemen scholars.
All may recite and uphold the True Great Cavern,
Which is prior to Heaven and Earth, the One of Primordial Emptiness.

**Inducing and Exhorting**
5.
All kings and people who study the Complete Truth and cultivate the Dao,
Waste their minds on the myriad methods and thousand gates.
Should one recite the Immortal Scripture of the Great Cavern ten thousand times,
The August Emperor and Venerable Master Lao will naturally become one’s confidants.

**Devout Men and Women**
6.
The civil and military officials of the world,
Prostitutes, commoners, and all their peers:
All may wholeheartedly uphold the Great Cavern,
Severing the roots of sin and roaming with the spirits.

**Determined Realization of Fruition**
7.
The true essence of the Great Cavern differs from other scriptures,
Ascending as immortals and entering as sages to meet the Mysterious True.
Though one may recite eighty thousand scriptures through kalpas as numerous as dust motes,
Only by perfect realization does one become the Supreme Person of the August Emperor.

**Lamenting the Ignorant Multitude**
8.
Alas! The dull and unenlightened multitude,
How could they recognize the pearl of the floating millet?
The Great Cavern delivers all as one body,
Easily ascending to the Mysterious Capital from the common ground.

**Expedient Exhortation**
9.
Should one wish to cultivate and attain the Supreme Vehicle,
How could anything compare to the few chapters of the Great Cavern?
Exhausting the mind and nature in the method of cultivating the body,
One awakens to ascend the Great Possession’s court.

**Karmic Conditions and Encounters**
10.
I, on account of all disciples, have this scripture engraved,
Composing eulogies to praise this scripture.
Its merit is towering, its treasury inexhaustible,
The wondrous Dao of the August Emperor is originally formless.

**Eulogy of the Great Cavern Scripture of the August Emperor of the Primordial Heaven**

**Origins and Causes**
Year Star:
Beginning with the resonant sound of Cang Hu Tan Chi,
Cloud scripts were formed to deliver heaven and humanity.
The Father of the Great Dao of the Supreme Mystery sought and received it,
And only then was the Great Cavern Scripture heard in the world below.

**Cultivating the True and Studying the Dao**
Beginning of Spring:
The common folk of the great earth study to awaken to the true,
The path to the immortal source is distant and truly hard to find.
Should one wish to know a shortcut without error,
Recite with the mouth and hold in the heart the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Praying for Emoluments, Official Position, and Offspring**
Rain Water:
The good deeds of ancestors in past lives were slight,
In this life, emoluments and offspring are quite arduous.
Should one pray to attain one’s desires,
How could anything compare to diligently studying the Great Cavern Scripture?

**Dispelling Calamities and Anomalies**
Awakening of Insects:
The sun and moon lose their light, suffering from eclipses,
The stars and constellations err in their courses, disordering the celestial patterns.
To eliminate heavenly calamities and pacify the common folk,
The lofty scholars together proclaim the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Praying for Wind, Rain, Silkworms, and Grain**
Spring Equinox:
Drought demons bring disaster, rain falls like metal,
Locusts and floods leave no harvest of grain.
To pray for wind and rain, for silkworms and grain,
Recite the Great Cavern Scripture with utmost sincerity.

**Ensuring Abundant Harvests and No Famine**
For universal bounty without hunger or want,
All prayers rely on the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Guiding and Transforming the Common Folk**
*Qingming*
Artisans, merchants, farmers, and the four classes of people,
Greedily seek without realizing their karma follows them.
Amidst busyness, set aside time and effort,
To study and recite the Wenchang Great Cavern Scripture.

**Pacifying Military Prefectures and Ceasing Warfare**
*Grain Rain*
Government storehouses overflow with wealth and resources,
Weapons of war forever stilled in joyous peace.
The people sing of the Dao’s governance, envisioning long stability,
To repay the nation, diligently study the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Honoring and Offering Sacrifices to Ghosts and Spirits**
*Start of Summer*
The deities of the earth altars, temples, and the hundred spirits,
Seek promotion yet find no means.
To ascend the register of good names and augment their power,
Morning and evening, they must heed the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Aiding and Recommending the Souls of Ancestors**
*Lesser Fullness*
The souls of kin, ancestors, parents, and relatives,
Long linger in the underworld, unable to ascend.
Should one wish to deliver them but lack the means,
With fasting and devotion, study the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Ending Tomb Litigation and Halting Summons**
*Grain in Ear*
Tomb litigation and summons burden descendants,
With reproaches and accusations lodged in the heavenly court.
Generation after generation, misfortunes are bequeathed,
To resolve and cease them, study the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Resolving Offenses and Pacifying Tombs and Dwellings**
*Summer Solstice*
Whether renovating or constructing tombs,
Breaking ground offends the baleful spirits.
Causing dwellings to suffer calamities,
To resolve and pacify, hold fast to the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Dispelling Pestilence**
*Lesser Heat*
The Year King of Epidemics commands the Five Pestilences,
Spreading through provinces and villages, harming the people.
To protect and preserve neighbors from contagion,
With utmost purity, together study the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Healing Illness**
*Greater Heat*
The misfortunes of monthly and yearly afflictions linger in the body,
Seeking physicians, divination, and prayers to the gods.
Yet no relief is found, no refuge to turn to,
Entrust life to the Dao and take refuge in the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Rescuing and Delivering Impoverished Souls and Stagnant Spirits**
*Start of Autumn*
The six kinds of karmic relations—male and female souls,
Dim and obscure, dwell in the nether darkness.
To universally guide them through refinement to the heavenly realms,
Frequently study the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Resolving Karmic Entanglements**
*Limit of Heat*
The six paths of karmic foes are deeply entwined,
Vengeance upon vengeance—when will it end?
Should one wish each to rejoice and be glad,
Nothing compares to hearing the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Reciting the Eastern Incantation**
*White Dew*
Whether over wealth or wrath,
In a moment of fury, one invokes the gods.
Binding oneself in ghostly litigation—when will it end?
To resolve and absolve, nothing but the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Quelling Multitudes of Malevolence**
*Autumn Equinox*
Illness, death, and loss never leave one’s side,
Official calamities and bandits cruelly encroach.
Wealth dissipates, possessions scatter like ice and snow,
For protection, hold fast to the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Eradicating Demonic Beings**
*Cold Dew*
Foxes, monkeys, and dog spirits from wood and stone,
Hurl bricks, set fires, and appear in human form.
Wielding power, seeking lewd sacrifices,
To exterminate them, study the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Restraining Tigers and Insects**
*Frost Descent*
Dwelling in mountains and forests or traveling alone,
Snakes, tigers, and wolves often harm people.
At the sound of recitation, they retreat, leaving no venom,
Sit or stand, keep the Great Cavern Scripture in mind.

**Opening the Mind and Awakening Wisdom**
*Start of Winter*
Scholars and students with minds like overgrown thatch,
Even child prodigies lack quick wit in response.
To wield the brush as if divinely aided,
First, cherish and hold fast to the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Preserving Form and Spirit**
*Lesser Snow*
This body is like illusion, like a bubble,
Within qi and spirit, cultivate the true.
To preserve form and life, enduring with heaven,
Familiarize yourself with the Wenchang Great Cavern Scripture.

**Admonishing Wealthy Families**
*Greater Snow*
Do not rely on vast wealth and hoarded gold,
Heaven’s decrees strip emoluments, easily toppling one.
At times, it is fitting to cultivate merit and virtue,
Sacrificing one’s own to publish and propagate the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Relating Ancient Verifications**
*Winter Solstice*
With a heart of sincerity reaching the Supreme Clarity,
One’s resonance is received, and the Three Spirits bestow it.
This body attains the fruition of Heavenly Worthies,
All because of diligently studying the Great Cavern Scripture.

**Universally Exhorting the Faithful**
*Lesser Cold*
Hear my repeated words on the Great Cavern Scripture,
Its profound and mysterious text is truly ineffable.
Boundless merit and virtue defy contemplation,
I universally exhort the common folk not to take it lightly.

**Reaping Karmic Fruits**
*Greater Cold*
The Primordial Heavenly King expounded the Great Vehicle,
Only those with affinity encounter this revered scripture.
Should one diligently recite it from beginning to end,
Together, they shall become companions of Wenchang.

**Hymn of Reverent Invocation**
I reverently invoke the boundless realms of the Three Clarities, the Supreme Three Realms’ Worthies,
The Primordial Beginning, Great Dharma King, Most Compassionate True Teaching Master,
The Jade Emperor, Great Dao Sovereign,
The Supreme Mystery, True Dao Father.
I bow to the Lord of the Supreme Mystery Heaven, the boundless Primordial Vault,
I reverently invoke the attendants of the Three Clarities’ realms, the host of Perfected Ones.
The *Great Cavern Scripture*, woven from the precious pearls of the myriad azure heavens,
Its wondrous Dao defies contemplation, its jade verses give birth to the ten thousand spirits.
The Greatly Compassionate Primordial Beginning Worthy,
Emerges from the earth’s gate in golden radiance,
Manifesting as three divine persons,
Clad in kudzu garments, bestowing golden treasures.
In dreams, they tuck two books into sleeves,
Registers and methods are conferred together.
Transforming and appearing as Wenchang,
Responding to wishes, divinely efficacious.

Now, I purify my three karmas,
Forever severing the roots of blood and corpse.
I present the talisman and enter the Jade Capital,
Bowing my head at the Golden Gate.
With wholehearted reverence, I prostrate,
Before the Primordial Beginning, Great Dharma King.
I only pray for great compassion,
To receive and grant my supplications.

May my silent contemplation,
Align with the talisman before the Emperor of Unity.
Transcending the Yellow Court of Immortals,
Together ascending beyond the Great Vastness.
May my seven ancestors sever their dark entanglements,
Receiving office in the assembly of the August King.

When I recite,
May the hundred spirits gather,
My voice penetrating the ten thousand heavens,
Its resonance reaching the nine earths.
May all my wishes be fulfilled,
As the scripture proclaims.
From this, gradually advance in cultivation,
Attaining the Dao and serving the sages.

**Hymn of Reverent Invitation**
All filial friends at the scripture’s feast,
Like gold and stone, pledge their original resolve.
With each bow and each invocation of the name,
Take refuge in the Lord of the Seven Curves.
Visualize the Primordial Azure Heaven,
The Primordial Eternal Life Mother.
Visualize the Purple Cloud Crag,
The true land of Wenchang.
The later-heavenly compassionate parents,
Manifesting in the Osmanthus Fragrance Palace.
Filial sons and compassionate grandsons,
Arrayed to attend their compassionate countenance.
Wishing to receive the true faith’s rites,
They emit great wish-fulfilling light,
Responding to minds and dreams,
Ensuring posterity and amassing blessings.

May I attend my compassionate parents,
Lifelong, their crane-hair flourishing in glory.
May I encounter the sagely age,
Step by step, basking in profound favor.
May I dwell in the realm of life,
Abounding in wealth and treasures.
As wish-fulfilling light follows thought,
In every direction, I ascend to the realm of longevity.
May my karmic conditions ripen,
That I may learn the Dao and attain immortality.
May my karmic defilements dissolve,
So that my mind alone is the Pure Land.
Universally, with all beings of heaven and earth,
I emerge from the gates of all suffering.
Gradually advancing, gradually cultivating,
According to conditions, I realize the fruits.
With a heart steadfast as gold and stone,
My true heart returns to the Lord of the Seven Curves.
All Buddhas and Heavenly Worthies,
With heart-incense, together offer praise and blessing.
May I, with all scripture students,
With one heart, prostrate in reverent homage.

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Jade Pure Sacred Realm,
The Celestial Palace of Qingwei Heaven.
Amidst the Yu Luo Xiao Terrace,
Above the Sen Luo Pure Abyss.
Manifesting the form of active creation,
Possessing the divine power of the boundless.
Expounding the true and mysterious,
Dispelling the hindrances of being, non-being, form, and emptiness;
Delivering all destinies,
Eradicating distinctions of wisdom and folly, high and low.
Its wondrous workings are unfathomable,
Its numinous mechanism beyond measure.
Great Compassion, Great Vow, Great Sage, Great Mercy,
Immeasurable Savior of Beings,
Original Celestial Worthy of Primordial Beginning.

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Northern Realm, within the station of the Dark Warrior.
From the Golden Portal, transforming the body,
To aiding the Jade Emperor in severing evil.
Cultivating truth and learning the Dao,
Achieving perfection in forty-two years.
Delivering the world and saving beings,
Blessings extending through kalpas innumerable.
All prayers answered,
No wishes unfulfilled.
Might and virtue resounding through heaven and earth,
Vows profound as seas and mountains.
Deeds and transgressions surely observed,
Rewards and punishments impartially bestowed.
Great Compassion, Great Vow, Great Sage, Great Mercy,
Dark Warrior, Assisting and Compliant, Numinous and Responsive True Lord;
Jade Void Preceptor, Mysterious Heavenly Primordial Sage, Benevolent and Majestic Emperor;
Heavenly Worthy of Salvation from the Final Kalpa.

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Primordial Life Mother of the First Epoch, transformed at the dawn of the Upper Command in the Azure Heaven.
Before the qi had dispersed,
She contained the essence of the Seven Curves’ true origin.
At the inception of the Nine Heavens,
She embraced the completeness of the Three Luminaries’ radiant body.
Her phoenix-like mechanism without trace,
Yet her signs may be named.
Her crane-like nature gazing upward to purity,
Lofty beyond all discourse.
The compassionate mother before heaven and earth,
The graceful countenance beyond ancient and modern.
At the return of yang on the fifth day of the tenth month,
She teaches the ancestral principles of the Three Bonds and Five Constants.
Her longevity stretches boundlessly,
Her form bestowed beyond form.
Perusing the preface to the *Collected Scriptures of Original Conduct*,
The attainment of the Dao in the Azure Heaven remains unfathomable.
Great Compassion, Great Vow, Great Sage, Great Mercy,
Primordial Eternal Life Mother of the Seven Curves’ First Epoch, Form-Bestowing Before Heaven,
Supreme Ultimate Primordial Sovereign,
Born on the fifth day of the tenth month.

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Upper Palace of Wenchang in the Osmanthus Fragrance Inner Hall.

The Dao-body is undifferentiated and complete,
Encompassing the ninety-five cycles of transformation.
The true primordial remains unrevealed,
Storing the thirty-six thousand essences of purity.
It unfolds the *Phoenix Script* of agelessness in the later heaven,
Originating from the unfathomable *Bear Dream* of the Azure Empyrean.
The greatly compassionate father of the divine father,
The supremely good person above all perfected beings.
The pulse of longevity is the root of the Three Bonds and Five Constants,
The heart embraces the essence of a hundred practices and ten thousand virtues.
Devotion knows no end,
Praise can never be forgotten.

**Revered as Long-Progenitor, born on the eleventh day of the second month.**

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Upper Palace of Wenchang in the Osmanthus Fragrance Inner Hall.

Her virtuous nature harmonizes with spring,
Embodying the pure qi of the Great True.
Her clear radiance mirrors autumn’s depth,
Nurturing the luminous essence of the Seventh Night.
She enfolds the dragon and elephant before their full manifestation,
Conceals the phoenix mechanism in its unrevealed state.
The greatly compassionate mother of the Sword Spring,
The supremely good person of Penglai.
She gives birth to the bonds and constants of ten thousand generations,
Engenders the teachings of fame and principle across the nine heavens.
Devotion knows no end,
Praise can never be forgotten.

**Great Compassion, Great Vow, Great Sage, Great Mercy,**

**Fruit-Attaining Preserving Radiance Bodhisattva, Successive Blessing Treasured Auspicious Primordial Sovereign,**
**Lady Qi, born on the seventh day of the seventh month.**

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Upper Palace of Wenchang in the Osmanthus Fragrance Inner Hall.

Ninety-five cycles of return, planting virtuous fruits in the garden of poetry and books;
A hundred thousand myriad transformations, cultivating osmanthus roots in the field of hidden merit.
From the thunder-shuttle’s luminous radiance upon Phoenix Mountain,
To the nurturing of auspicious omens within Turtle Peak’s grottoes,
Opening the human heart must be rooted in filial piety toward one’s kin,
Prolonging the nation’s pulse must first arise from loyalty to one’s sovereign.
Responding to dreams to preserve life,
Extending compassion and relieving suffering.

**Great Benevolence, Great Filial Piety, Great Sage, Great Mercy,**
**Divine Civil and Sacred Martial Filial Virtue Loyal Benevolence King,**
**Newly Enfeoffed Auxiliary Primordial Opening Transformation Wenchang Controller of Emoluments Vast Benevolence Emperor Lord,**
**Limpid Truth Correct Vision Treasured Radiance Compassionate Relief Heavenly Worthy, named Ya,**
**born on the third day of the second month.**

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Osmanthus Fragrance Inner Hall’s Wenchang Inner Palace.

Her virtuous demeanor is pure as ice,
Scooping the clear moon from the nine heavens;
Her benevolent heart is rich as spring,
Fanning the family winds of the Seven Curves.
Her graceful bearing serves in the chambers of her kin,
Her kindness and purity fulfill the Way of motherhood.
Harmonious qi fills the hall above and below,
A spring terrace for all ages past and present.
Responding to dreams to nurture auspicious omens,
Evolving transformations from the heart’s sincerity.

**Great Benevolence, Great Filial Piety, Great Sage, Great Mercy,**
**Reverent Compliant Gentle Responsive Virtue Radiant August Empress,**
**Fruit-Attaining Fixed Response Bodhisattva, Primordial Harmony Penetrating Mystery Primordial Sovereign,**
**former Zhong clan, named Zhi Zheng,**
**born on the third day of the fifth month,**
**later Princess Xing Tang of the Li clan.**

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Osmanthus Fragrance Inner Hall’s Wenchang Auxiliary Palace.

Her sagely virtue and compassionate kindness, in a single thought, perpetuate the family’s illustrious legacy;
Her divine works resplendent, the Nine Heavens ease the Emperor-Father’s heart.
Amidst cloud-kissed crags, she enacts the rites of formless, soundless music;
In the moon’s cavern, she transmits the enduring patterns of the ancestral heritage.
Bestowing the Five Blessings upon generations of benevolent and filial households,
She displays the Three Primacies before the flourishing descendants of poetry and letters.
Teaching arises from the heart’s sincerity,
Responding to dreams to nurture auspicious omens.

**Utmost Benevolence, Utmost Filial Piety, Utmost Sage, Utmost Mercy,**
**Sacred Eldest Son, Heir of Virtue and Treader of Filial Piety, Prince,**
**Wenchang Extender of Blessings Perfected Lord, named Ran Ming,**
**born on the second day of the third month of the Stone [Year].**

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Osmanthus Fragrance Inner Hall’s Wenchang Auxiliary Palace.

Her gentle nature, soft as spring, refines her bearing in attendance;
Her chaste heart, pure as jade, embodies the lofty purity of her noble model.
Together they uphold the family’s long-standing reputation,
Silently mastering the inner chambers’ harmonious principles.
Her teachings spread kindness and fraternal love,
Her transformative influence suffuses tranquil harmony.
Responding to dreams to nurture auspicious omens,
From the heart’s sincerity, she bestows blessings.

**Utmost Benevolence, Utmost Filial Piety, Utmost Sage, Utmost Mercy,**
**Sacred Eldest Daughter-in-Law, Virtuous Assistant, Manifestly August and Compliant Filial Lady,**
**Wenchang Tranquil Responder Heavenly Lord of the Wei clan,**
**born on the first day of the eighth month.**

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Osmanthus Fragrance Inner Hall’s Wenchang Auxiliary Palace.

Father and son, one household, fully embody the Way of filial piety and compassion;
Ruler and minister, through a thousand ages, fulfill the hearts of perfect benevolence and reverence.
Models of human culture arise from the warp and weft of constant norms to establish teachings;
Plumb lines for the world’s path root in the *Odes* and *Rites* learned at court.
Rectifying decay in the heavens of hidden merit,
Fortune humbles itself in the garden of cultivated arts.
Evolving transformations from the heart’s sincerity,
Responding to dreams to nurture auspicious omens.

**Utmost Benevolence, Utmost Filial Piety, Utmost Sage, Utmost Mercy,**
**Sacred Second Son, Establisher of Virtue and Filial Piety, Prince,**
**Wenchang Controller of Emoluments Perfected Lord, named Mao Yang,**
**born on the first day of the first month.**

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Osmanthus Fragrance Inner Hall’s Wenchang Auxiliary Palace.

Filial virtue gentle and yielding, endowed with the pure essence of the primordial unity;
Chaste heart compliant as earth, graceful in the sevenfold chambers’ decorum.
Before the Five Wives’ Ridge, she raised the splendor of inquiring after well-being;
Upon the Three Tides’ waters, she flowed the clear source of accumulated blessings.
Responding to dreams to nurture auspicious omens,
Evolving transformations from the heart’s sincerity.

**Utmost Benevolence, Utmost Filial Piety, Utmost Sage, Utmost Mercy,**
**Sacred Second Consort, Assistant of Compliance and Kindness, Perfect in Filial Piety, Lady of Virtue,**
**Wenchang Heir of Blessings Heavenly Lord, née Wei,**
**born on the eighteenth day of the second month.**

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Osmanthus Fragrance Inner Hall’s Wenchang Inner Palace.

The toad’s luminous essence congeals in auspiciousness, rooted in the father’s celestial kindness;
The phoenix’s heart gathers fortune, molded by the mother’s harmonious virtue.
Her frosty bearing and snowy nature remain pure, untouched by worldly things;
Her embrace of spring winds and autumn moons is as heaven’s own heaven.
Inwardly observing the emptiness of ten thousand realms,
She attains the Dao of the Nine Heavens—
Her heart’s clarity defies discussion,
Her gentle virtue eludes description.

**Utmost Benevolence, Utmost Filial Piety, Utmost Sage, Utmost Mercy,**
**Refined and True, Wondrous and Serene, Filial Princess,**
**Wenchang Myriad Longevities Heavenly Lord,**
**born on the sixteenth day of the fourth month.**

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Osmanthus Fragrance Inner Hall’s Wenchang Inner Palace.

Her celestial bearing stern and majestic, the Dao’s measure purifies the family’s legacy;
Her noble integrity unyielding, her benevolent renown renews the forge of transformation.
Thunder’s inquiry bursts forth in spring’s harmony, awakening all to enlightenment;
Rain and dew spread universally across heaven’s expanse, giving life to all things.
Responding to thoughts to nurture auspicious omens,
Her numinous efficacy answers dreams.

**Utmost Benevolence, Utmost Filial Piety, Utmost Sage, Utmost Mercy,**
**Sacred Eldest Grandson, Inheritor of Manifest Numinosity, Perfect in Filial Piety, Marquis,**
**Wenchang Accumulator of Blessings Perfected One, named He,**
**born on the third day of the seventh month.**

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Osmanthus Fragrance Inner Hall’s Wenchang Inner Palace.

Her sacred essence born of heaven’s grace, pure as the spring breeze’s embrace;
Her immortal bearing and Dao’s measure carve clarity from autumn’s moon.
Four generations gathered in one hall, her chamber’s decorum refined and solemn;
A hundred deeds and myriad virtues, her family’s blessings precise and profound.
Her numinous efficacy answers dreams, unfolding transformations in response to circumstance.

**Utmost Benevolence, Utmost Filial Piety, Utmost Sage, Utmost Mercy,**
**Sacred Eldest Grandson’s Wife, Cultivator of Virtue and Inheritor of Filial Piety, Lady of Manifest Response,**
**Wenchang Accumulator of Blessings Perfected One, née Li,**
**born on the eighteenth day of the fifth month.**

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Osmanthus Fragrance Inner Hall’s Wenchang Inner Palace.

Her laughter like spring’s breeze, each word nurturing virtue’s growth;
Her demeanor harmonious, every utterance transmitting the family’s legacy.
The son inherits the sacred son’s heart, his roots nourished by hidden merit;
The grandson embodies the divine grandson’s form, his fruits proving true immortality.
Auspicious omens answer dreams, her teachings founded in the heart’s sincerity.

**Utmost Benevolence, Utmost Filial Piety, Utmost Sage, Utmost Mercy,**
**Sacred Second Grandson, Inheritor of Manifest Numinosity and Obedient Filial Piety, Marquis,**
**Wenchang Successor of Blessings Perfected One, named Huai,**
**born on the thirteenth day of the tenth month.**

**Reverent Homage with Utmost Sincerity**
To the Osmanthus Fragrance Inner Hall’s Wenchang Inner Palace.

Jade essence and golden bearing—
the soil where parents’ careful nurture took root;
Graceful radiance like the transforming sun—
the heaven where descendants’ lineage endures.
Born to honor the roots of hidden merit,
inwardly endowed with mutual vigilance;
Destined to continue the ancestral mandate,
gently emerging to fulfill mutual success.
Auspicious omens answer dreams,
evolving in accord with opportunity.

**Utmost Benevolence, Utmost Filial Piety, Utmost Sage, Utmost Mercy,**
**Sacred Second Grandson’s Wife, Wisdom-Responsive Embodiment of Filial Piety, Lady of Manifest Virtue,**
**Wenchang Successor of Blessings Perfected, Heavenly Lord Guo,**
**born on the twenty-third day of the seventh month.**

The rites of reverence now complete,
we turn to the light for repentance:

**True Master of the Sevenfold Compassionate Teachings,**
**Compassionate Father, Compassionate Mother, born with me.**
**Sons born as sacred sons all practice filial piety and kindness;**
**Grandchildren inheriting divine grandsons all embody kindness and filial piety.**
**A family’s harmonious qi knows no end to spring;**
**Ten thousand generations’ spring terrace shines with moonlight.**
**Compassionate light illumines all heavenly beings,**
**infusing the tiniest dust to fill heaven and earth.**
**My life shares the body of heaven and earth,**
**just as Wenchang was at the beginning of kalpas.**
**The sacred is not sacred of itself, nor the ordinary merely ordinary—**
**wandering to this day, only now do I awaken.**
**May I encounter the teachings of the Sevenfold Compassionate Master,**
**devoted to loyalty, to filial piety, to a compassionate heart.**
**Let me not use speech to slight gods or mortals,**
**nor use my body to burden my parents.**
**Let me not use my mind to deceive heaven and earth,**
**nor use my heart to bring calamity upon my descendants.**
**May I cultivate filial conduct and hidden merit,**
**practicing every expedient with diligence.**
**I repent and atone for the sins of many lives,**
**taking refuge in the Primordial Emperor’s great compassionate light.**
**Seeking heirs, seeking emolument, seeking the way of life—**
**I seek not from others but from myself.**
**Only our Wenchang’s Sevenfold Master,**
**through kalpas awaiting beings, preserves the law of forbearance.**
**May you release a single wish-fulfilling light,**
**moved by the true repentance of all sentient beings.**

The repentance now complete,
we proceed to make vows:

**May my parents together attain the fruit of longevity,**
**tortoise years and crane hair illumined by compassionate light.**
**May I myself bow to great good fortune,**
**serving above and nurturing below without sorrow.**
**May my children and grandchildren inhale the osmanthus of Cloud Cliff,**
**flourishing together with me in shared prosperity.**
**Father’s kindness, son’s filial piety—one family’s spring;**
**brilliant light unbetraying the Compassionate Master’s teachings.**
**May I be personally received and guided by the Sevenfold One,**
**led to ascend to truth and enter the Buddha-gate.**
**Abandoning life after life, rightly perceiving all,**
**may all future kalpas be perfectly fulfilled.**

The vows now complete,
we proceed to praise:

**Lord of Benevolence and Filial Piety in the Osmanthus Fragrance Hall,**
**your teachings rain everywhere, washing away karmic roots.**
**Karmic roots transformed into osmanthus fragrance,**
**good roots cultivated into the fruit of longevity.**
**One family’s flesh and blood free from affliction,**
**Sevenfold descendants together protected.**
**May all in this life and the next,**
**before the Purple Cloud Cliff, forever attain the Dao.**
**Step by step, heart by heart, at the Emperor’s side;**
**life after life, the heavens ordain.**
**Though bones may turn to dust and hearts to ash,**
**one point of true heart remains like metal and stone.**

**With faith and reverence, we bow to the Radiant Treasure of Clear Truth and Right Contemplation, Heavenly Worthy.**
**Great Cavern Sutra Assembly of Wenchang.**

**Seated Praise**
**Sung in Sanskrit tones,**
**we bow our heads before the Heavenly Worthy of the Void Sovereign.**
**To recite the Cavern Scripture,**
**all who wish to intone must first purify the Three Karmas.**

**Purification Mantra for the Karma of the Body**
*Sprinkle the crown with purified water, wash the hands, left hand in the Jade Seal, right hand in the Sword Seal.*
Within this bodily realm,
thirty-six thousand spirits reside.
In motion, stillness, walking, or repose,
through kalpas past and future,
may this body remain ever pure,
abiding always within the Three Treasures.
When the kalpa dissolves in ruin,
may this body never perish.
*Hasten, hasten, in accordance with the law’s decree!*

**Purification Mantra for the Karma of the Mind**
*Pass the incense burner, inhale the fragrant smoke once, left hand in the Departure Seal.*
The Great Dao descends with true qi,
exhaling and inhaling to refine the Five Spirits.
May it gather all demons,
the karma of the mind ever pure.
Sever the ten thousand obstructions,
dispel all misfortunes,
subdue all sentient beings,
and with each thought return to the Right Dao.
*Hasten, hasten, in accordance with the law’s decree!*

**Purification Mantra for the Karma of Speech**
*Each drinks a mouthful of water, left hand in the Kan Seal.*
The mouth is the Palace of Supreme Harmony,
exhaling and inhaling to receive true qi.
At all times recite the precious scripture,
daily feasting on the flavor of the Dharma.
Let no evil words arise,
nor impure thoughts of lust.
May the roots of sin and suffering be extinguished,
and the discourse of true and right meaning ever flow.
*Hasten, hasten, in accordance with the law’s decree!*

**Purification Mantra for Heaven and Earth**
*Sprinkle water within and without the scripture assembly, left hand in the Fourfold Upright Seal.*
Essence of the Great One,
flower of the Eastern Well,
flowing to irrigate the whole,
scouring filth and dispelling evil.
Pure as a luminous pearl,
spotless as the lotus blossom,
transform into a body of golden light,
treading upon cloud-brocade and rosy mist.
Ascend the Seven Treasures Hall,
to become a true immortal family.
*Hasten, hasten, in accordance with the law’s decree!*

**Mantra to Pacify the Earth Deity**

**Mantra to Pacify the Earth Deity**
*Left hand in the Tiger Seal.*
Primal Beginning establishes and pacifies,
proclaiming universally to the ten thousand spirits.
True officials of the mountains and rivers,
spirits of the land and altars,
left the She-ji, right the grain sacrifices—
let none disturb without cause.
Turn toward the right Dao,
within and without made limpid and clear.
Each abides in its proper place,
prepared to guard the imperial court.
The Most High issues the command:
search out and seize the deviant essences.
Dharma-protecting divine kings,
safeguard the recitation of scriptures.
Take refuge in the Great Dao,
*origin, prosperity, harmony, and constancy.*
*Hasten, hasten, in accordance with the law’s decree!*

**Mantra of the Profound Mystery of Opening the Scripture**
The qi of the Mysterious Origin divides,
the three qi of the Mysterious Origin first part.
Luminous purity opens the cavern spirits.
Radiant clarity and literary splendor awaken the great cavern’s honored spirits.
Spiritual wind returns the Great Harmony,
divine wind stirs the qi of the Great Harmony.
Jade tones gather the flowing essences,
resonant tones of jade and gold.
Supreme is the root of spontaneity,
supreme is the Dao, not forced or contrived.
Who discerns this hidden script?
Who can recognize the obscure and concealed text?
Firm and resolute, awakened to unity,
one who is courageous and avoids the lesser and middling vehicles.
In an instant, transcend the three vehicles.
In a fleeting moment, swiftly ascend the most wondrous supreme vehicle.
Still and silent, without root in form,
tranquil and empty, unattached to void or form.
Through endless kalpas, how could one drift or sink?
Through eons unobscured, how could one wander or stray?
How could one diligently cultivate and uphold,
why not advance with precision to accomplish this Dao?
Ultimately ascend to the Jade Clarity,
or in another version, *your body attains eternal endurance.*
Jade Clarity, Boundless, and Supreme Truth—
*Wenchang’s Great Cavern Scripture of the Immortals, Scroll the Second*
● 『□』: This character is indistinct in the original text.

*Jade Clarity, Boundless, and Supreme Truth—*
*Wenchang’s Great Cavern Scripture of the Immortals, Annotated, Scroll the Third*
Annotated by Yangzi of Mount Penglai in Eastern Shu, Wei Qi

The Dao speaks: In the primordial beginning of the Dragon-Han kalpa, the Celestial King of Primordial Beginning revealed *The Jade Scripture of the Great Cavern* within the Supreme Great Possession Jade Clarity Palace.

The Dao speaks—this is the discourse of the Jade Emperor Dao Lord.
"In the past" refers to the distant antiquity of bygone ages.
"Dragon-Han" denotes the moment when the singular qi gestated within the empty vastness, at the inception of the Great Void, where above there was no further form, below no further abyss—chaotic and boundless, an expanse of surging currents. For over seven thousand kalpas, this qi circulated ceaselessly, traversing ninety-nine thousand nine hundred and ninety li in a single year. Its transformations, like a dragon’s, were unfathomable, hence the name Dragon-Han. When the reckoning of its cycles reached its zenith, the Three Luminaries dawned, ushering in the Red Clarity. The Brahma-qi suffused the cosmos, the myriad patterns unfolded, the primordial net flowed and evolved, giving birth to heaven and earth, awakening the numinous spirits—this is called the Three Kalpas of the Kaihuang, when all became distinct.

According to *The Golden Book of Great Possession*, the Heavenly Treasure Lord was born in the first year of the Dragon-Han kalpa and revealed his scripture that same year. The Numinous Treasure Lord was born at the Dragon-Han’s unfolding of the cosmic chart, and after one kalpa, in the first year of Red Clarity, he revealed his scripture. The Divine Treasure Lord was born in the first year of Red Clarity, and after two kalpas, in the first year of the Supreme August, he revealed his scripture. Only then did the Three Treasures acquire their fixed names.

Yet the Divine Kings memorialized: When the reckoning ended in the jia-shen year, the great currents scoured away the filth. From the era of Red Clarity to the first year of the Supreme August, twenty-four myriad beings received deliverance. After the Kaihuang, when the count reached jia-shen, the heavens selected and ranked the immortals, but the offices of the immortals were left vacant. Thus, from the three generations, ten myriad were chosen to fill their ranks, and another twelve myriad were raised as reserve officials. From among the departed souls with meritorious deeds, thirty-two myriad were selected to join them. After the jia-shen purgation, the people of the Great Possession were inaugurated.

The Confucian classics state: Yao ascended the throne in the jia-chen year, and by the jia-shen year, forty years had passed before the calamity of the great flood arose. By this reckoning, *The Scripture of Spirit Generation* must have emerged before the time of Tang Yao, while *The Great Cavern Scripture* was first revealed in the first year of the Dragon-Han kalpa, when the Primordial Beginning was born and issued the scripture. Thus, it is called the primordial beginning of the Dragon-Han kalpa. By the first year of the Supreme August, when the Most High revealed his scripture, the Three Treasures had each attained their fixed positions. The Numinous Treasure was transmitted once more, then bestowed upon the Supreme Mystery while seated. Hence, the subsequent scripture states: "This treasure is revealed anew."

*The Scripture of the True Warrior* records that in the first year of the Dragon-Han kalpa, the teaching was expounded, recounting events from the first year of the Kaihuang. Yet since the Kaihuang precedes the Dragon-Han, this must be an error in the transmission of the scriptures by the various perfected ones. One should follow *The Golden Book of Great Possession*, thoroughly examining the kalpas in which the Three Treasures were born and the times when they revealed their scriptures to deliver beings—other accounts cannot be entirely trusted.

It is also said: The beginning of heaven and earth comprises five kalpas—the kalpa of inception, the kalpa of formation, the kalpa of dwelling, the kalpa of dissolution, and the kalpa of emptiness. These five kalpas cycle endlessly, and heaven and earth complete their beginning and end through them. The same applies to humans and all things.

The East is called Dragon-Han, the South Red Clarity, the West Extended Peace, the North Kaihuang, and the Center Supreme August. Starting from *zi*, every three characters denote a kalpa, reaching *xu* and *hai* as Extended Peace. In terms of the sun, this is night; in terms of humans, this is death. Beyond the six directions, we shall provisionally set aside discussion.

Since the separation of heaven and earth, as recorded in the Six Classics, the *Book of Changes* speaks of the Supreme Ultimate, which generates the Two Modes. The Two Modes generate the Four Images, and the Four Images generate the Eight Trigrams. The Two Modes are heaven and earth; the Four Images are the four seasons. Yin is quiescent, yang is dynamic—hence transformation arises. Movement and stillness have their constancy, hardness and softness are determined—thus the four seasons alternate and transform. Since transformation is ceaseless, there are kalpas and reckonings, as in the *River Chart* and *Luo Scripture*. The ascent and descent of the two qi, the interweaving of the five phases—none escape the workings of number. Greatly, there are kalpas; minutely, there are epochs, all arising from years, months, days, and hours. Hours comprise quarters, days have their markers, months have their crescents, full moons, waning, and conjunctions; years have spring, summer, autumn, and winter. Thus, quarters accumulate into hours, hours into days, days into months, months into years, years into epochs, and epochs into kalpas.

Since the Supreme Ultimate divided, who can reckon how many kalpas and epochs have passed? In the first year of the Dragon-Han kalpa, the Heavenly Treasure Lord was transformed and born, and when he revealed his scripture, the palace was named the Supreme Great Possession Jade Clarity Palace. This was the capital of the Celestial King of Primordial Beginning, the inception of the perfected deities’ exposition of *The Great Cavern Scripture of the Immortals*. Thus, it is the ancestor of all scriptures, the sovereign of all teachings.

All scriptures refer to the Celestial Venerable of Primordial Beginning, yet *The Great Cavern Scripture* alone calls him the Celestial King of Primordial Beginning—this is the utmost reverence. There are also the Supreme Thearch of Primordial Beginning and the Celestial Thearch of Primordial Beginning, names given according to what is perceived, for in truth, there is no fixed name. It is the various perfected ones who have forcibly named him.

The scripture states: The Great Dao is nameless, but because it engenders heaven, earth, and the myriad things, it acquires a name. Expounding the Way of the Supreme Mystery, the Double Mystery, and the Mystery of Unity, it is named *The Great Cavern Scripture of the Immortals*. "Mystery" (*xuan*) is black with a tinge of red, for the northern direction’s yang stirs and generates water. The yang qi is red, the water’s color is black—hence the term *xuan*. The Supreme Mystery, the Double Mystery, and the Mystery of Unity denote the flourishing of the water qi, which is the root of heaven and earth. *Xuan* also signifies profundity and boundless vastness. Thus, the various scriptures speak of "mystery upon mystery," following this principle.

The Supreme Mystery refers to the prior existence of the mysterious qi and the primordial qi, after which the initial qi sequentially generates and grows. Thus, the unfolding of the Supreme Mystery’s qi is called the Way of the Double Mystery and the Mystery of Unity, named *The Great Cavern Scripture of the Immortals*. Within its treasury are the Three Clarities’ *Great Cavern Scripture* in one hundred twenty scrolls, and the *Jade Scripture* of Mount Mao and Mount Longhu in thirty-nine chapters.

The Primordial Heavenly King of the Origin first emitted the sound of the Supreme Mystery of Unity, its resonance flowing through the Jade Clarity. For the One is the root of all transformations, the origin of all virtues, and there is no affair that does not arise from the heart. Laozi’s attainment of the One, Confucius’s thread of unity, and Master Shao’s saying—"Heaven divides creation within the One"—how could this not be so? The Way of Heaven is simply the One. The Supreme Mystery is the true qi of the north; the Two Modes established their positions, with the north as the *zi* [first] phase. The "sound of unity" refers to Heaven’s One generating water, and water corresponding to the *yu* tone. When heaven and earth first arose, they began with the number One in the north, where the initial yang stirred and gave birth to water—red in its yang qi. This is like human birth, where the yang essence coalesces to form the embryo. When yang stirs, it transforms, hence it is called "flowing resonance." It is not proclaimed by a golden mouth but is the vibration of the numinous wind, which naturally forms the Cavern Chapters.

The Vast Emperor’s Way of Singular Truth expounds the precious scripture of the Great Cavern. That which governs is called the Emperor—this is the human heart. For a state, there are the Nine Classics, yet the principle by which they are practiced is one. The One is sincerity; without delusion, it is called true reality. Thus, it is named the *Vast Emperor’s Way of Singular Truth*. Therefore, we know the *Great Cavern Scripture* is the Confucian *Doctrine of the Mean*. The "Emperor One" is the title of the Great Cavern’s Imperial Honored One. There are the Emperor One, the Male One, and the Female One—together called the Way of the Three Ones, which is the origin of the Great Cavern.

"Vast" means to unfold and to magnify, to greatly propagate this Way. Expounding the precious scripture of the Great Cavern aims to enable people to attain the One, whereby all affairs are completed. If one can focus on the One without distraction, this Way is accomplished. It is also called the "Non-Dual Dharma Gate." This is named the *Wenchang Great Cavern Scripture of the Immortals*. Additionally, there are the *Great Cavern’s Marrow*, the *Great Cavern’s Exegesis*, and the *Great Cavern’s Mysterious Covenant*. According to the commentaries in various scriptures, I dare not presume authority.

It reveals the methods of the Nine Governances and transmits the talismans of the Nine Radiances. The Primordial, Mysterious, and Originative Three Qi each generate nine qi, forming the Nine Emperors of the Divine Empyrean. Thus, it reveals the methods of the Nine Governances to unite with the Emperors and transmits the talismans of the Nine Radiances to gather the spirits. The Way of the Great Cavern begins with the One Qi, which generates the Three Qi; the Three Qi generate the Nine Qi; the Nine Qi generate the Ten Thousand Qi, which coalesce into the Ten Thousand Heavens. It speaks only of the Nine Qi, not the Ten Thousand Qi, to highlight the essential framework.

Within humans, the Ten Thousand Qi are complete, giving rise to the Ten Thousand Spirits. Heaven and earth are established through the Ten Thousand Qi, and the human body is born through the Ten Thousand Qi. If the spirits depart and the qi scatter, the human Way nearly ceases. This Way of the Emperor One flourishes here. Using the Nine to represent the Nine has already been expounded in the *Luo River Writing*. The Nine Heavens generate the four nines—thirty-six heavens; the Nine Earths generate the four nines—thirty-six earths. Each has its annotations below.

When a devoted scholar recites this, enters seclusion, and cultivates practice, the Ten Thousand Spirits rejoice and celebrate, the Ten Thousand Numina protect and uphold, the Ten Thousand Sages respond and connect, and the Ten Thousand Immortals gather and descend. "Seclusion" means alignment, signifying the purification and alignment of the heart’s ground, the settling of thoughts in stillness, and the prevention of disorder. The ancients practiced three days of seclusion and seven days of abstinence, or "alignment and abstinence with bathing," which is fitting for sacrificing to the Supreme Emperor. Seclusion levels the heart, while abstinence guards and stills it. If one attains the heart-seclusion of Yanzi’s "sitting in forgetfulness," this is the *Great Cavern Scripture*.

This means that when a devoted scholar practices the *Great Cavern Scripture of the Immortals*, they should enter seclusion with purity, remove defilements, cease thoughts, and guard the One in stillness. Internally, the Ten Thousand Spirits rejoice and celebrate; externally, the hundred numina protect and uphold; above, the Ten Thousand Sages respond and connect; below, the Ten Thousand Immortals gather and descend. The *Chapter on Generating the Spirit* says: "When the One is intoned, the Ten Thousand Perfected harmonize; when the Nine are recited, all heavens pay homage." Such is the case.

The scripture states: "If a person can constantly abide in clarity and stillness, heaven and earth all return to them." Heaven and earth, ghosts and spirits, never aid the tyrannical in cruelty. One can transcend the Three Calamities, Four Slaughters, Five Demons, Six Harms, Seven Injuries, Eight Difficulties, Nine Tribulations, and Ten Evils. The *Dipper Scripture* records these in great detail; I will not repeat them here.

While living in the world, one encounters various demonic obstacles. Without single-minded devotion to the Supreme Way, how can one escape afflictions? The ancestral gate has a saying: "The grinding stone and whetstone harm oneself to benefit others"—this is self-restraint and serving others. Ascending as an immortal and entering sagehood, the spirit is born in the Purple Tenuity, naturally and without contrivance. The *Book of Changes* says: "Without thought, without action," which perfectly accords with the Great Cavern’s Way of naturalness. One version reads: "Ascending as an immortal and entering sagehood, awakened." One’s original spirit stands shoulder to shoulder with the Emperors of the various heavens, enjoying the bliss and freedom of heaven—how could there be contrivance? It is all the principle of naturalness.

Formerly, Yang Taiming of the Tang, having risen through Confucianism to a prominent official post and served as magistrate of Chang’an under Guo Ziyi’s command, later abandoned his position and built a thatched hut on Mount Lu. One day, while seeking the True Lord, he was visited by a descent, who said: "The Three Primordial Lords of the Grand Simplicity have commanded me to transmit to you the *Scripture of the Supreme Perfected Way of the Nine Heavens*." Upon inspection, it was the *Supreme Great Cavern Scripture*. Taiming recited it without ceasing, and in the eighth year of Emperor Xianzong’s *Yuanhe* reign, on the first day of the first month, he ascended lightly as an immortal. Was this not the "ascending as an immortal and entering sagehood" spoken of in the scripture?

It is not bound by yin and yang, the Five Phases, or the Six Qi. The Six Qi are cold, heat, wind, rain, darkness, and brightness. Heaven has the Six Qi, which descend to generate the Five Flavors, manifest as the Five Colors, and manifest as the Five Tones. Excess gives rise to the Six Illnesses. According to medical texts, yin and yang, the Five Phases, the Five Movements, and the Six Qi intertwine between heaven and earth. When harmonious, they bring auspiciousness; when in opposition, they bring misfortune. Auspiciousness brings forth sages, heaven bestows sweet dew, earth produces numinous mushrooms, the Five Grains flourish, and the people live in peace. Misfortune causes heaven and earth to close, the worthy to hide, celestial portents and disasters to appear, mountains to collapse, seas to dry up, and people to perish—all constrained by the Five and Six.

Cultivators should shed the shell of the Five Phases and depart from the mechanisms of the Eight Trigrams. The Eight Trigrams belong to earth; those who focus on the Supreme Way transcend them. The Way of Earth models itself on the Way of Heaven, and thus yin and yang cannot constrain them.

Each thought grows and deepens, advancing into the Great Vehicle. When its vastness knows no bounds, the myriad heavens gaze below, the Jade Emperor descends to witness, and flying immortals come to escort. This very thought is the Golden Elixir. Its mechanism must ceaselessly revolve, continuously and subtly present. If one’s thought remains unshaken, each thought following the last, growing in succession, one progresses to awaken to the Great Vehicle, and further to the Supreme Vehicle. In spreading this Dao, the heavenly emperors and kings observe from above, the Supreme Emperor bestows his gaze, and flying immortals and demon kings protect and elevate one’s being.

In former times, Gao Yunju recited the *Great Cavern Scripture*. One day, celestial emissaries descended to observe and spoke with him in kindness. Later, Yunju ascended as an immortal—was this not the gaze of the myriad heavens? Countless ancestors across ten thousand kalpas, wandering souls and stagnant spirits, all attain rebirth. Before one has crossed over oneself, one first delivers one’s ancestors. How much more so for the innumerable ancestors from a thousand myriad kalpas past—wandering luminous souls and sunken spirits—all ascend to higher realms.

In the Jin dynasty, Xu Jingyang and Wu, the Immortal Elder of Ge, both ascended as immortals through offering rites and refining solitary souls and spirits. For these solitary souls are also ancestors from a thousand lives and ten thousand kalpas. Noble lineages connect with immortals, and their descendants become perpetual nobles. Generations of descendants, of illustrious lineage, continue in communion with immortals, enduring in the world as exalted beings—like Zhang Zifang and the hereditary Celestial Masters, whose succession stretches unbroken.

When merit is complete and the Dao perfected, flesh and bone ascend together. When merit is fulfilled and conduct perfected, virtue and power fill to abundance, and an entire family—flesh and bone—ascends as one, as when Xu Jingyang and his forty-two kin lifted their dwelling in broad daylight. Riding dragons and driving clouds, they ascend to pay homage in the Jade Purity. Transforming one’s own yin and yang qi into dragon and cloud, one mounts them to soar through the heavens, ascending to the sacred realm of Jade Purity to attend the Primordial Sovereign of the Three Purities as a minister.

The Primordial Heavenly King chants the Supreme Mystery, concentrating spirit in profound contemplation to utter the Cavern Chapters. The Primordial One intones the qi of the Supreme Mystery into sound, gathering spirit and qi in deep and distant thought, refining spirit and qi to precision, and only then speaks the precious chapters of the Great Cavern. It is as if one must ponder before attaining—uttering the Cavern Chapters is not mere oral recitation, but the coalescence of spirit and qi, illuminating the void to form sound.

The Supreme Cavern Primordial—this chapter names the Most High Lord of the Void, the August Sovereign of the Great Cavern, who presides over the entire scripture. The characters within the chapter are divided into sections for their meanings, so it is briefly summarized here.

The Primordial One was born before the Great Non-Being and the beginningless beginning, before the first signs of the Five Ultimates. A single qi transformed within the void, formless and nameless, without qi or image, without color or light—what Master Zhou called the Limitless. With one movement and one stillness, one yin and one yang, yang transforms and yin unites, giving rise to the Five Phases: Supreme Change, Supreme Beginning, Supreme Origin, Supreme Simplicity, and Supreme Ultimate. Today’s Great Cavern is the *Book of Changes*’ Supreme Ultimate.

The Most High is exalted beyond all naming—it is the Limitless. The Primal Chaos and Great Non-Being is the primordial qi of the Primordial One, born within the undivided void, at the beginning of the Great Non-Being. *Yuan* means beginning, hence the name Primordial One. Some call it Primal Chaos, which is also fitting. The present text lacks the character *yuan*; it should be added. Thus, the Primordial One is called the Most High Primal Chaos of the Great Non-Being, the Numinous Treasure calls it the Red Primal Chaos of the Great Non-Being, and the Lord Lao calls it the Dark and Tranquil Mystery-Pervading Origin. Together, they are called the Three Origins—not the Three Origins of heaven, earth, and water, but the ancestral qi that gives birth to heaven and establishes earth.

The Heavenly Treasure is the title of the Primordial One as the Heavenly Treasure Venerable Lord. The Jade Emperor is not the common Jade Emperor; jade symbolizes virtue, for its nature is warm and moist yet firm and hard. *Huang* means great. The Primordial One, with his own qi of utmost greatness and hardness, established heaven and earth, bringing forth things and accomplishing affairs—what Mencius called the vast and flowing qi that fills heaven and earth.

The Origin gives birth to the Nine Heavens. The Origin is the foremost of virtues, for it is the ancestor of all transformations. Here, *yuan* refers to the Three Origins. The Three Qi generate the Nine Qi, which are the Nine Heavens of spirit generation. Heaven, earth, and the myriad things could not be born without the nurturing of the Three Origins and the guidance of the Nine Qi. Thus, the Three Qi are the honor of heaven and earth, and the Nine Qi are the root of the myriad things. Those who cultivate them unite their virtue with the Three Qi and align with the Nine Qi. From this point onward, the Dao of ceaseless generation becomes manifest. Thus, the *Book of Changes* says: "The great virtue of heaven and earth is called generation."

Other versions read "Supreme Cavern Mystery," which is surely an error.

The Qi Ancestor is the Great Non-Being. The Three Qi of the Mysterious Origin were born before the Great Non-Being, coalescing from the void to generate qi. Qi is born from emptiness, emptiness from beginning, beginning from origin, and origin from mystery. Thus, it is called the Qi Ancestor of the Great Non-Being—this is the source of the Great Dao, where being arises from non-being.

The Multitude of Winds begets the Mysterious. One version reads "Ancestral Wind," which is incorrect. *Feng* means qi. *Zhong* means not one. The qi of the Primal Chaos and Great Non-Being Origin comprises ninety-nine billion, nine hundred ninety-nine million, nine hundred ninety thousand qi. The qi of the Red Primal Chaos of the Great Non-Being Origin comprises ninety-nine billion, nine hundred ninety-nine million, nine hundred ninety-nine thousand qi. The qi of the Dark and Tranquil Mystery-Pervading Origin comprises ninety-nine billion, nine hundred ninety-nine million, nine hundred ninety thousand qi. For the myriad qi root in the Nine Qi, the Nine Qi begin with the Three Qi, and the Three Qi return to the One Qi. Thus, it is called the Multitude of Winds begetting the Mysterious. *Yin* means succession, continuation, and lineage. The root and lineage emerge from the mysterious qi—this is called the Returning Wind’s Primal Union.

Once scattered kin are reunited. One version reads "governed and scattered," which is mistaken. If there were governance, there would be constraint—how could there be scattering? When one cultivates this Cavern, the three generations of ancestors, nine lineages, five clans, and six relations each attain transformation, free from the illness of karmic roots and stagnant obstructions.

The Four Pures pacify the tranquil. The Four Pures are the four qi illuminating clarity. When Heaven and Earth divided, the four directions expanded—this illustrates how one’s ancestors and stagnant perceptions all attain transformation, free from calamitous entanglements. Thus, the four directions are fully guarded, and one dwells in effortless serenity, ascending to Heaven, where joy and freedom abide.

The Supreme One of the Upper Radiance gathers the multitudes and seizes the mists. The Great Cavern’s Imperial Honored One is named the Supreme One. Riding the dragon chariot of the mysterious radiance, he summons spirits and captures winds to deliver suffering souls, akin to the gathering of numinous winds and mists. A long covenant aligns with a single destiny; seven generations find repose. Through enduring harmony with auspicious fortune—akin to the assembly of kindred spirits in propitious times—seven generations of ancestors all attain rest, and all dispersed gatherings are delivered to transcendence.

Entrusting the numinous and binding fate, the blossom returns to spontaneity. Every spark of numinous light finds its lodging, and the original destiny of one’s life has its proper affiliation. Restored to radiant splendor without loss or deficit, free from toil or expenditure—hence it is called spontaneous.

Vast and boundless, luminous brilliance flows; the Six Luminaries sink and shift. *Vast and boundless* describes the far-reaching, while *luminous brilliance* signifies the flowing radiance suffusing the entire body.
