The Six Luminaries govern the registers of life under the Southern Dipper. When the six palaces congeal and stabilize, no further change or shift occurs.

Ascending the Brahma and steering the radiance, the Western Florescence manifests peace. The Jade Emperor’s name is Feng Lingfan, styled Lü Changling, also called the Divine Elder White Emperor, named Zhang An, styled Xihua—representing the harmony of the human lung and viscera. Together inscribed in the imperial records, all roots are untangled. The Western Florescence Jade Numinous Jasper Palace compiles the azure jade registers to present to the Jade Emperor. Through cultivation, the roots of evil, earthly bonds, demonic registers, and ghostly ledgers are all dissolved.

The womb-field’s profound path gives rise to jade orchids through the ages. The upper field is the Muddy Pellet, the middle field the Crimson Palace, and the lower field the Sea of Qi—where embryonic breathing resides. The path is deep and secluded. The Yellow Court revolves, embracing the purple and enveloping the yellow to enter the cinnabar field. Generation after generation, jade-like orchids flourish, as in the *Chapter on Generating the Divine*: "Radiant jade blossoms" conveys the same meaning. If one can nurture the lower field, the essence pervades the body like jade steps adorned with orchids. *Orchid* signifies purity and fragrance, as the *Yellow Court* states: "The body generates luminous splendor, its fragrant qi like orchids." Below, *Qiu Lan* and *Su Lan* share this meaning.

The numinous light’s eightfold radiance blends to generate the myriad spirits. One’s own spark of numinous light illuminates the eight chambers—what is called the eight windows, exquisitely open. If a person’s desire for life lacks the full complement of the myriad qi, the myriad spirits will not be complete, and life will not come to be.

The above jade passage in celestial script comprises eighty-eight characters, serving as the preface to the thirty-six chapters. The thirty-six celestial and terrestrial deities all encompass this chapter. The *Mysterious Covenant* states: "When one cultivates the Great Cavern’s Supreme Mystery Imperial One’s Cavern Chapter and recites it once, all sins are dissolved. The body’s spirits and six roots all attain cavernous purity. The Six Heavens descend in submission, the host of demons bind their heads, and the myriad qi align in rectitude, gaining the Gate of Unobstructedness."

The Primordial Celestial Sovereign said: "The first jade passage of the Great Cavern of Wenchang generates the embryo in a month, and the golden elixir returns once. *Ding-chou, Wu-yin, Yu, Sui.*" The inception flourishes in the primordial qi, its color azure, forming the Nine Yangs’ Wood Qi of the East. It congeals into celestial realms, named the Boundless Heaven of Yudan, with the kalpa called Dragon Han. This heaven’s essence and soul open the Yang Qi, governing the Muddy Pellet Palace. The imperial true womb-life’s original unity arises from the Yellow Evolution Qi, generating the embryo’s origin.

The Highest Feasts in the Purple Clarity. The *Wenchang Scripture* formerly placed this chapter first. Verified against the *Mysterious Covenant* and the scripture’s character count, they align—hence this arrangement is followed. One version of the *Supreme Clarity Great Cavern* begins with *Eastern Florescence Initiates Embryonic Radiance*. Moreover, the ten chapters of the middle volume in various editions have been interchanged. Here, the six roots are ordered sequentially, and the upper volume’s *Chapter on the Body Generating the Divine* is arranged according to the reception of womb and embryonic qi, offering readers a coherent progression.

Yet this treasured passage is not solely for those receiving life. For the practitioner refining the inner golden elixir, it must also be followed month by month in sequence, like a woman with child or a hen brooding eggs—devoted, cherishing, and unwavering in mindfulness. From the initial commencement to the tenth month, the sacred embryo completes, and the yang spirit suddenly appears. Both paths share the same track.

The generation of the human embryonic origin: the *Book of Changes* states, "When male and female unite their essences, the myriad things transform and generate." Father’s essence and mother’s blood, through empty resonance, form the Supreme Mystery’s qi born of the Supreme Nonbeing. Heaven One generates Water as its root. First arises the Ren Water of the northwest, uniting with the Ding Fire of the southwest—termed the Water-Fire mutual completion. Yin and yang resonate, meeting in the primordial palace, suspended and attached to the spleen. The spleen belongs to Earth, so all things naturally transform and generate through Earth, thereby forming the embryo. Thus, Water and Earth share the embryo in *Ji*. *Ji* is the domain of six pure yangs, belonging to Qian and Xun—this is where the Returning Wind’s Primal Union occurs. Males revolve left for ten months to *Yin*, where the Three Yangs intersect in harmony, hence males are born. Females revolve right for ten months to *Shen*, where the Three Yins fully attain closure, hence females are born.

The *Highest Feasts in the Purple Clarity*: the Highest Supreme’s Great Existence Jade Clarity Palace, where the Primordial Commencement resides, lies in the Purple Clarity Heaven. The Primordial Commencement roams and feasts above it. The Qian’s inception qi generates the human Muddy Pellet Palace in sequence. At birth, the nose forms first, hence ears form later—hence the ancient saying, "Nose ancestors, ear descendants," marking the beginning and end of human generation. The nose connects to the forehead, so the inception qi first generates the Muddy Pellet. Next, the mysterious and original two qi generate the middle and lower regions. Human life arises from yin and yang’s two flourishings and the Five Phases. Those receiving clear and luminous qi become sages and worthies; those receiving heavy and turbid qi become common folk; those receiving mixed qi become the myriad things. Thus, below it states *Five Elders Assist the Jade Root*, referring to the division of qi, as in the Nine Qi of the East.

The assistance of the Jade Root and the planting of the Jade Root within the Five Viscera both involve the scattering of crimson blossoms and the flight of jade pairs, all through the descent of true qi from the Five Directions, thereby forming the formless spirits of humanity.

The Five Elders assist the Jade Root.
The so-called *Four Mysteries Receive the Original Prohibition* ensures the long preservation of the Five Emperors’ City. The Five Viscera serve as the root of the body, guarded by the Five Spirits—hence the assistance of the Jade Root. The Five Sons return to the root: from *renzi* Wood to *gengshen*, nine in number, constituting the Nine Qi of the East; from *wuzi* Fire to *gengyin*, three in number, the Three Qi of the South; from *jiazi* Metal to *gengwu*, seven in number, the Seven Qi of the West; from *bingzi* Water to *gengchen*, five in number, the Five Qi of the North. *Gengzi* Earth resides at the Center, forming the One Qi.

The Azure Numinous Beginning Elder, Lord of the Nine Qi of the East;
The Cinnabar Numinous True Elder, Lord of the Three Qi of the South;
The Radiant Numinous August Elder, Lord of the Seven Qi of the West;
The Dark Numinous Mystic Elder, Lord of the Five Qi of the North;
The Primordial Numinous Primordial Elder, Lord of the One Qi of the Center—
all assist the Jade Root, signifying the return of the qi of the Five Viscera to their root to restore destiny. The essence, spirit, ethereal soul, corporeal soul, and intention are the roots of the heart, liver, spleen, lungs, and kidneys.

The Supreme Simplicity brushes past the distant radiance.
The Supreme Simplicity is the Mother of the Three Simplicities, whose spirit sweeps beyond the farthest light. *Miao* means small or complete, as seen in the infusion of the Three Floral Qi. The Supreme Simplicity is the wondrous fruit attained according to one’s rank, bearing the title *Supreme Simplicity Pure Void Perfected*.

Align the tally before the Imperial Unity.
The Noble Scion Without Peer, named *He Fu*, presents the tally he holds to align it before the Imperial Unity. Once the tally’s tokens match, rebirth is assured. *He Fu* is also called *Mysterious Origin Uncle*, who guards the gate of the liver.

The White Emperor’s luminous radiance shines.
The Venerable White Prime Spirit, whose luminous radiance shines, governs the lung qi of the West. Also named *White Prime Cavern Yang Lord*, his numinous banner bears the style *Mysterious Yi Absolute*. With the Seven Yang Metal Qi of the West, he presides over *shen* and *you*, ruling the *Dui* Palace below to guard the lungs.

Return to the Great Auroral Realm of Metal.
As the lung qi pertains to Metal, the revolving winds merge into the Great Auroral Realm. Above lies the Great White Metal Star and the Seven Mansions of the West, weaving the celestial patterns; below, it governs the Western Marchmount, its terrestrial correspondences linking to the human lung and viscera to infuse true qi.

Cross my gate of death and seal it.
Having traversed the gate of life, one must block the gate of death. The human body contains thirty-six gates of life and thirty-six gates of death. Auspicious clouds open the gates of life, while propitious mists seal the gates of death—propitious mists being true qi.

Draw forth the beam across the Three Paths.
To escape the bitter sea of the Three Paths, one must erect the bridge of the Mystic Ford. To pass the Three Passes, one must build the Magpie Bridge. As the ancients said: "Above the Magpie Bridge, below the Magpie Bridge, heaven responds to the heart, earth to the tide"—distinct from the Flying Mystic Beam.

The Ten Penetrations arise from this.
The Six Perfections and Ten Penetrations perfect the myriad practices, thereby attaining the Dao of longevity and enduring vision. Human gestation completes in ten months, with all spirits embodied before birth. Only when this fetal root is firm does one achieve the Ten Penetrations.

Wondrous practices flourish from this.
The Three Thousand Wondrous Practices thus flourish, perfectly fulfilled. Once the human spirit and qi are distributed, at an auspicious hour and propitious moment, the Dao of Golden Elixir arises. Cultivating the Ten Great Cavern Wondrous Practices, one may realize the Ten Great Wondrous Fruits.

Within the luminous radiance of the Cavern’s clarity,
In the realm of the Solar Dao, the radiance is extraordinary. Only when one’s substance is bathed in the Great Yang does one perceive the luminous realm. Floral radiance and luminous radiance are one. The ancient immortals said: "The gentle lead crucible’s light pierces the curtains"—this is the clarity of luminous radiance within the Cavern.

The Imperial Unity is truly mysterious and profound.
The Imperial Unity is the name of the Great Cavern’s Imperial Honored One. Those who refine the Golden Elixir also realize this fruit—how could it not be mysterious in the extreme? The scriptures speak of the Imperial Unity, the Male Unity, and the Female Unity, known as the *Scripture of the Three Unities*. The Imperial Unity pertains to the Water number of the North, while *xuan* (mysterious) is the color-symbol of the North. Thus, the true essence of the Male and Female Imperial Unity reaches the utmost profundity.

Of old, Master Liu Gen traveled through the four directions in official service, governing with virtue. He constantly cultivated the Dao of the Great Cavern’s Imperial Unity and thereby attained mysterious transformation into immortality.

In general, the Dao of Heaven flows and nurtures the myriad things. That which enables creation and transformation is none other than yin and yang and the Five Phases. Nothing exists without first possessing this principle, and only then does it possess this qi. When generating beings, it must rely on the gathering of this qi before there can be form. Thus, the birth of humans and things must first obtain this principle, and only then do they possess the natures of strength and compliance, benevolence, righteousness, propriety, and wisdom. They must obtain this qi before they can have souls, spirits, the Five Viscera, and the hundred bones. As Master Zhou said: "The true of the Non-Ultimate and the essence of the Two and Five wondrously unite and congeal." Humans receive qi in the first month, forming the embryo, and by the tenth month, the spirit is distributed and the qi is complete before birth. The Dao of refining the Golden Elixir follows this pattern precisely. After three hundred merits are perfected, the sacred embryo is firmly established.

The above Jade Chapter in celestial seal script comprises sixty characters. Above, it governs the Supreme August Yellow-Perfected Heaven; below, it rules the First Layer of the Lustrous Earth, the Earth Sovereign Lord.

The *Mysterious Contract* states: "When the disciple recites the *Wenchang Great Cavern Scripture of the Immortals* and cultivates the true Dao of the Imperial Unity, the wondrous practices are fully accomplished, and one first realizes the sacred merit of the Ten Penetrations. Initially, one accumulates profound and abstruse mysterious principles. Reciting it a hundred times naturally unites the qi; reciting it a thousand times without cease unites the spirit and the numinous."

The Orthodox Unity teachings include the self-designation *Minor Disciple Perfected, Your Subject So-and-So*. Thus, in the *Mysterious Contract*, whenever *disciple* is mentioned, it refers to the self-designation of the Perfected.

The Celestial Venerable of Primordial Beginning said: "The second Jade Chapter of the *Wenchang Great Cavern*, the second month of gestation, the second return of the Golden Elixir. *Jimao*, *Gengchen*, *Gu*, *Lin*."

The primordial qi generates the Cavern qi, its color crimson, forming the Three Yangs’ fire-qi of the southern direction. Condensing into celestial realms, it is named the Supreme Meditation Virtue Immeasurable Longevity Heaven, its kalpa called Crimson Clarity. This heaven’s essence-spirit is the yang luminosity of qi, governing the Hall of Light Bureau. The Imperial Perfected’s embryonic destiny arises from the Cavern of Luminous Primordiality, where the Purple Portal’s qi engenders the root of gestation.

The Jade Void accords with the mysterious return—this is the sign of gestation in the second month. First, the Supreme Unity’s essence-spirit, named Mysterious Return, styled Flourishing Prosperity, presides over matters of birth and nurture. The Jade Void is the Jade Thearch’s bureau. The human head possesses nine palaces—this is one among them. In the fifth chapter, the Thearch descends to ascend the Jade Void, thus revealing it as the Jade Thearch’s bureau. It is also called the Supreme Jade Void Luminous August Heavenly Worthy. The immortals’ traditions record the Jade Void Venerable Master attending the assembly of the Southern Qi Lady and Anqi Sheng, hence the Jade Void is named according to the fruition of attainment. Now, the Jade Void is the abode of the Supreme Essence-Spirit.

Celestial Morn wanders the Golden Empyrean.
Celestial Morn is the sun.

The Golden Empyrean is the Yellow Path, also called the Cloud Han. When the Jade Thearch ascends his throne, the qi of the Great Yang revolves through the void, as when the Jade Thearch rides the Vermilion Empyrean—like human yang essence suddenly congealing in the midst of emptiness.

Brightly shines the Thearch’s radiance,
As the celestial sun roams,
The Empyrean and Han gleam resplendent,
Giving birth to the Thearch’s Mysterious Radiance.
The Dragon Chariot is yet another divine name,
For when essence is ninefold,
Entering luminous brilliance,
It seeks to generate the brain’s palaces—
Thus it is said: “Mounting the radiance, it soars beyond the Empyrean.”

Reverently, you ride the Jade Isle.
The joyous one, named Everlasting Life, styled Swiftly Arising,
Surnamed Cypress Completion,
Rides the sun’s light-chariot to wander the Jade Isle—
That is, the Mysterious Isle—
To serve as the Controller of the Nine Heavens’ Embryonic Origin.
Without the descent of the life-bestowing writ,
Birth shall never come to pass.
“Swiftly” means in an instant.

On the left, the Primordial Youth is summoned.
This is the qi of the Wood Sovereign,
Hence the Azure Numinous Primordial Elder Azure Youth Lord of the East,
Also called the Lesser Youth of the Grand Tenuity,
Who, in the human body, presides on the left,
Summoning azure qi to govern the liver’s three hun-souls.
The Primordial Youth is the newly born youth.

On the right, the Everlasting Talisman is commanded.
The Everlasting Talisman is the name of the Thearch’s ministerial aide.
In the West resides the White Thearch Lord,
Whose office, in the human body, lies on the right,
Issuing commands to white qi to generate the lung’s seven po-souls.
The two spirits of yin and yang stand attendant on left and right,
Conveying and assisting the divine qi.

The Luminous Perfected shines upon the Nine Empyreans.
The Heart-Mysterious Ninefold Thearch Honorable Divine Lord,
Named Luminous Perfected,
Like the sun’s wheel blazing bright above the Nine Empyreans.
When sun and moon conjoin, it is called “illumination”;
Yin and yang unite within the midst of emptiness.
The *Elixir Canon* speaks of the meeting of the two qi upon the Yellow Path.

Three days illumine the Mysterious Array.
The Mysterious Array is the Mysterious Garden,
Located on the Kunlun Mountains in the northwest,
Also called the Northern Culmen.
The “three days” are the three qi of the South,
Where the Great Yang Thearch Lord,
With true fire,
Illumines the Mysterious Garden of the North—
Is this not the Way of Already Achieved?
As the ancients said:
“Accumulate fractions to make an inch,
Accumulate inches to make a foot,
Without cease in foot and inch,
One makes a bolt of cloth.”
When a person awakens in a single moment,
Advancing with courage and vigor,
Even to one day, two days,
Or three days,
Then the mysterious qi flows unimpeded.
As the *Tang Scripture* says:
“If daily renewed, daily renewed again,
And renewed yet again,”
Gradually washing away impurities to become a person of good fortune.

The Dry Radiance arises in tender solicitude.
(One text says “Thousand Radiance,” but this is surely an error.)
The Lesser Youth of the Grand Tenuity is named Dry Radiance Essence,
Styled Meeting the Origin Master,
Also named Tender Regard.
When water and fire achieve harmony,
Yin and yang intermingle,
And the signs of birth appear,
Thus they arise together in tender solicitude and cherishing love.

Within lies the Profound and Boundless.
The Supreme Thearch Sovereign’s essence-spirit,
Named Profound and Boundless,
Is the Supreme Unity.
This spirit governs transformation
And the essence of the embryonic sac.
The perfected person who attains this
May make it the root of the sagely embryo;
In golden elixir, it serves as the medicinal substance.

Grant me long years,
For it enables one to attain longevity and enduring vision.

The Master of Emptiness and Stillness says: The Dao is not distant—it lies within the body. All things are empty, yet the nature is not empty. If the nature is not empty, the spirit and qi abide. When qi returns to the primordial sea, longevity is boundless—this is called enduring years.

A thousand kalpas make but one cycle. Only after a thousand kalpas does a single cycle complete, revolving endlessly. In heaven, there are the years of the Brushing Stone, yet for those who suffer in hell, time is no less. The *Scripture of Salvation* forbids transmission for eighty thousand kalpas; the *Scripture of the Jade Emperor*, for forty thousand kalpas. The *Chapter on the Generation of Spirit* does not emerge unless at the opening of heaven and earth—yet when will those who suffer there find liberation? Only then will they awaken to the true cause. Upon seeing this scripture, one should awaken early to attain the joy of a thousand kalpas’ enduring years. This scripture is not to be transmitted recklessly; the responsibility of transmission is shared by all.

The Yellow Register preserves the kalpa’s measure. (The character *rèn* is commonly written as *chū*, meaning "beginning." A depth of seven feet is called a *rèn*. The *Book of Documents* says, "To build a mountain nine *rèn* high"; Mencius says, "To dig a well nine *rèn* deep.") The Radiant Yellow Register can preserve and restrain the kalpa’s destiny. Once a person receives life, their name is inscribed in the Yellow Register above. The scripture says: "The Yellow Register and white tablets erase death and promote life." The true lords of heaven and earth rejoice upon hearing of a person’s birth, for the Yellow Register records their name as an auspicious sign. Yet how lamentable that people willingly abandon life to enter the realm of death! *Rèn* means "high," "pointed," or "utmost"—when the kalpa’s reckoning nears its end, the Yellow Register preserves it.

Don the brocade and enter the Spirit Mound. *Qiū* means "hollow," "great," or "gathering." It lies southeast of Kunlun, high on all four sides and low in the center, hence called Kun Mound. In humans, it is called the Spirit Mound, the Celestial Valley, or sometimes the Jade Pillow. It speaks of the Profound and Boundless donning brocade robes to enter the imperial court—this is the qi of yin and yang ascending to the brain’s gate. The *Lower Alley* says: "Grand Unity, *Chóu Qiū*, and *Lán* share the same meaning." *Jǐn* refers to the intermingling of five colors—here, the qi of the five viscera steams and dyes the pattern, called brocade robes, or embroidered robes. These are the garments worn by the Perfected Lords of Execution, who wield axes and halberds to carry out punishments.

The Grand Unity governs the root of life. This chapter is titled "The Chapter of the Grand Unity, the Venerable Spirit." The Grand Unity is the essence-qi of primordial water. Before heaven and earth took form, Heavenly One generated water—this spirit presides over it. The spirit is the master of long life. Within the human body, it resembles an infant, unclothed, four inches in length. It is the spirit of the Great Cavern’s returned embryo, the first form—named *Wùyóu* and styled *Guī Huìchāng*. It constantly guards beneath the Jade Pillow. At the moment of a person’s birth, it holds the tally and unites the hundred spirits, solely governing the root of life. Below, the term "Grand Unity" appears ten times; the details are explained in the middle fascicle’s annotations.

The Noble Scion summons and unites the tally. On the left is the Peerless Noble Scion, named *Xuán Yuánshū* and styled *Héfúzi*. The Grand Unity summons him, and when their tally tokens align, it is called true qi, which can generate life. If they do not align, it is called deviant qi and must be rejected.

Ten cycles refine the initial resolve. This refers to the *Scripture of Salvation*’s ten revolutions—ten cycles to save beings. "Initial resolve" denotes the moment of hesitation, between belief and doubt, existence and nonexistence. Thus, ten cycles complete the count, reaching the stage of non-retreat. The *Tradition* says: "If others can do it once, I will do it a hundred times; if others can do it a hundred times, I will do it a thousand." If one truly pursues this Dao, though soft, they may overcome the strong. If one tests the initial resolve with ten cycles, this Dao will be achieved. It urges people to exert utmost effort, advancing without retreat. Those who wish to turn their minds toward the supreme Dao should face the lofty Perfected and exalted Sages, making great vows and firming their initial resolve.

Attain entry into the root of great faith. Through the *Great Cavern Scripture of the Immortals*’ guidance and transformation, one may enter the great stability of faith—the root of truth without delusion, the meaning of "faith" as non-opposition to things. Faith pertains to earth, and earth’s completion number is ten—also the number of the *River Chart*. This fascicle’s ten chapters include ten cycles, ten virtues, ten directions, ten flowers, ten powers, ten immortals, ten Perfected, and ten penetrations, all spoken of in full measure. Lacking even one, the Dao of generation and transformation cannot be complete. Ten is the number of earth, illustrating earth’s power to nurture and transform. Faith is simply sincerity—thus, sincerity and faith are the root.

The above jade script of celestial seal comprises ninety characters. Above, it governs the Grand Clarity Jade Perfection Heaven; below, it commands the First Rampart’s Primordial Virtue Lord. The *Mysterious Contract* says: "Reciting it twice, one enters the root of nature. Good causes do not cease; the immortal register records the name. The ten thousand qi harmonize, and one attains the gate of settled contemplation."

The Primordial Heavenly King says: "The third jade script of the Great Cavern’s *Luminous Writ* corresponds to the third month’s animating soul, three returns to one reversal." *Xīnsì*, *rénwǔ*, *guān*, *shìkè*.

The Cavern qi generates the vast qi—its color is white, belonging to the seven yang metal qi of the west. It congeals into the celestial realm, called the Brahma Canopy Prolonged Extension Heaven, with the kalpa named Prolonged Prosperity. This heaven’s essence-spirit is the qi of incipient yang, governing the upper cinnabar field palace. The imperial spirit’s animating soul and life’s primordial long numinous luminous immortal qi generate the three souls.

The Jade Emperor’s Mystic Upper Banner. (One text says: "The Jade Emperor has a Mystic Upper Banner to command the nine heavens’ steps." The phrase "many" is likely an interpolation. Generally, spirit writings and jade scripts often condense meaning into one or two or three characters per line. For example, the four characters *dǎn lǒu ā huì* convey vast meaning, just as the phrase *gāo shàng dòng yuán* encapsulates several characters’ worth. The chapters are composed in five-character lines—how could three extra characters be added? This must be a transmission error.) The Grand Tenuity Jade Emperor possesses the Yellow Return Banner and the Numinous Banner as instruments of summoning, to return the yang soul to the body.

The banners command the nine heavens’ steps. These banners, issuing commands from the nine heavens’ steps, cannot ascend by mere staging—hence their summons is made by banner, so exalted is their dignity. The "heavenly steps" denote rank and order, forbidding reckless advancement.

The Seven Awakenings ride the wondrous Dao.
The Awakened is the Buddha’s perfect awakened wondrous mind. In heaven, it is the seven stars; it spreads qi among humans, called the heart. Descending spirit into its midst, it is named the numen. It oversees the office of the Seven Awakening Spirit Kings. The Seven Awakenings are the heart of human innate ability and innate knowledge. The heart has seven apertures, hence the Seven Awakenings. It is said to ride the power of the Great Dao, striking names from the ledgers of death and inscribing them in the registers of life. The Seven Awakenings appear thrice: "Together they fly as the Seven Awakening Primes," "The Supreme Harmony conveys the Seven Awakenings," for when humans awaken, they do good; when unawakened, they become instruments of misfortune. (The Seven Awakenings are also recorded elsewhere.)

Joyous radiance returns the numinous wind.
"Joy" is felicity, "radiance" is brightness. When the qi within the human body is in supreme harmony and concord, the numinous luminosity naturally arrives. One says "numinous wind," another "spirit wind"—both are the primordial spirit’s return, blending with the wind.

The whirlwind blazes, halting in the north’s splendor.
"Whirlwind" is commonly written as *biāo*; a scorching gale arrives violently. It is also called *jùyàn fúyáo*, the cyclone, or the solar soul named "halting." "Halting" refers to pavilions and towers; originally the character *tíng* (pavilion), later written as *tíng* (to halt, to gather).

The Purple Essence sings at the eastern bend.
The long numinous luminous immortal qi generates the three souls, like a good sprout growing. The Purple Essence flourishes in the eastern land of benevolent virtue. The blazing whirlwind and Purple Essence—these two spirits chant the precious chapters of the Great Cavern, their songs ascending to the nine heavens.

Jade harmony resounds beyond the nine skies.
The Left Immortal of the Orthodox Unity is named Jade Harmony, like jade chimes ringing, their sound piercing beyond the nine skies. As the *Analects* says: "Heaven will use the Master as a wooden clapper." Between heaven and humanity, harmonious qi brings auspiciousness, and all desire the overflowing of virtuous governance.

The jade tally summons the Grand Tenuity.
The Jade Emperor summons the Grand Tenuity’s youth named Dry Radiance, commanding him to stand at his side. He orders him to wield the Yellow Return Banner, while the Non-Male commands the Numinous Banner to summon the hidden souls. The *Chapter on Generating Spirit* says: "The Grand Tenuity’s Yellow Return Banner."

The Three Pures generate the Mud Pill Palace.
"Pure" means unadulterated. The Three Pures are purity without end. The Mud Pill Palace: the head has nine palaces. Between the brows, one *cun* inward, is the Hall of Light Palace, where the Grand One resides. To the left is the Purple Chamber, to the right the Vermilion Door. One *cun* further inward is the Cavern Chamber Palace, where three perfected ones dwell: to the left, the Non-Male; to the right, the White Prime; and in the center, the Yellow Cloud. Three *cun* inward is the Mud Pill Palace, the place of ingress and egress for the ten thousand spirits. The Three Pure Lords, named Han Zhang, preside over this palace. Four *cun* inward is the Flowing Pearl Palace, five *cun* the Jade Emperor Palace. One *cun* above the Hall of Light is the Heavenly Court Palace; one *cun* above the Cavern Chamber is the Ultimate Perfection Palace; one *cun* above the Cinnabar Field is the Mystic Cinnabar Palace; one *cun* above the Flowing Pearl is the Heavenly Sovereign Palace. Together, these are called the nine palaces of the head. The Three Radiant Lords of the Imperial Elder generate spirit in the Mud Pill Palace, also called the qi of the three fields: blue, yellow, and white. The *Yellow Court* says: "The Mud Pill has nodes, all with spirits." The Three Pures are also a name for cinnabar. Formerly, Master Wang refined the Three Pures Elixir and was summoned to the Central Marchmount, where he attained the Dao. Also, Duke Wu of Zhou, Lady Hui of Zhou, cultivated the Dao of the Three Pures. They encountered the Western Numinous Sage Mother, who transmitted the scriptures. Hundreds of men and women admired them. They said, "The world is in chaos; I shall depart. After a hundred years, I will return," and then transformed and departed.

The effulgence of the Golden Numen shines.
The Three Pures emit golden efflorescence, their numinous radiance illuminating above and below. Like a person whose wisdom-eye is opened, seeing all without obstruction. The eye is the canopy of the five viscera, manifesting the brightness of sun and moon. The Yellow Court’s eye spirit is the Luminous Effulgent Mystic Lord.

The Elder Lord and Han Zhang ascend.
Han Zhang is the personal name of the Three Pure Lords, the spirits who generate the Mud Pill Palace. When a person is born, qi descends from heaven, then receives the essence and blood of father and mother. At the inception of form, it begins from the Mud Pill, sequentially growing into a complete form.

Guard and defend the mechanism of death’s node.
Reciting this thrice, the three souls naturally generate. The Three Pure Lords must guard and seal the mechanism of death’s qi node, ensuring reception of life. The Lower Lane says: "Guard and seal the death qi, unfolding sameness." Han Zhang’s name means "spirit generates the Dao," his divine office.

The Ten Virtues generate within the Mystic.
The goodness of human nature can all become like Yao and Shun. There is no one who is not good, yet people themselves flow into the realm of misfortune and evil, inviting calamity and disaster.

The doctrine of karmic retribution for good and evil is sometimes dismissed as fantastical by Confucians. Yet it is also said that Wang Wei painted ghosts and spirits to frighten those who would not otherwise understand. The texts state: "Doing good brings a hundred blessings; doing evil brings a hundred calamities." The *Book of Yu* declares: "Following the Dao brings fortune; defying it brings misfortune—like shadow and echo." It also says: "Pride invites loss; humility brings gain—this is the Way of Heaven." The *Book of Changes* states: "A family that accumulates goodness will have abundant fortune; a family that accumulates evil will have abundant misfortune." Such are the earnest teachings of the sages, and the principle of karmic retribution is as clear as day. Why would the sages not speak of it? It is only that you have not yet had the leisure to study and clarify it.

When a person cultivates the Ten Virtues, they are born within the Mystic qi. Yanzi, upon attaining a single virtue, held it fast in reverence. Yu bowed upon hearing a virtuous word. For one who abides in the perfection of goodness—whether as a ruler in benevolence, a minister in respect, a child in filial piety, a parent in kindness, or in dealings with others in sincerity—every action and retreat becomes the utmost good. Thus, one naturally transcends calamity. Passing through the trials of calamity, one attains effortless spontaneity.

The scripture states: "Soaring beyond the Three Disasters and Four Destructions, one reaches the state of natural non-action, unbound by yin and yang, the Five Phases, or the six qi." This is the profound meaning of the earnest chapter.

The above Jade Chapter in celestial script comprises seventy characters. Above, it governs the Qingming River Lad of Heaven; below, it empowers the First Rampart’s Yuande Lord. The *Mystic Contract* says: "Reciting it thrice grants sovereign wisdom, transcends all calamities, enters the Upper Pass of the Mystic, and with all qi purified, enters the Gate of the Inaudible and Invisible."

*Jade Pure Ultimate Supreme Perfected Wenchang Great Cavern Scripture*, Scroll Three
● "Water Red" (*shui chi*) is likely an error for "Water’s" (*shui zhe*).
● "Kema" (*ke ma*) is likely an error for "Sima" (*si ma*).
● "Knife" (*dao*) is likely an error for "Thus" (*nai*).

*Jade Pure Ultimate Supreme Perfected Wenchang Great Cavern Scripture*, Scroll Four
Annotated by Zhongyangzi Wei Qi of Mount Penglai in Eastern Shu

The Primordial Heavenly King said: The Great Flourishing Great Cavern Jade Chapter, Fourth, generates the soul in the fourth month, cycling four returns and two reversions. *Guiwei*, *Jiashen*, *Bi*, *Bo*. The primordial qi generates the *Min* qi, its color profound black, forming the Five Yang Waters qi of the north. It congeals into a celestial realm named the Silent and Secluded *Doushu* Heaven, with its kalpa called *Kaihuang*. This heaven’s essence is the qi of the soul and the Great Yang, governing the Cavern Chamber Palace. The Emperor Perfected’s po-soul commands the primordial *Yangshi Mingyan* qi, from which the seven po-souls arise. The Supreme Perfected governs the nine qi.

The Supreme Perfected is the Great Profound One, that is, the primordial qi of the Profound and Primordial Two. ● It generates the nine qi—alternatively called the Great Profound Nine Qi. The upper and lower scrolls’ nine chapters state: "The Supreme Perfected’s Ninefold Radiant Wheel," where radiance is qi, governing the nine qi to generate the myriad spirits.

The Cavern’s luminous scene lodges numinous communion. The Cavern Yang’s abode is where perfected immortals refine the hun-souls. The Crimson Palace’s radiant scene is the dwelling where the divine luminaries lodge their traces. Those who attain communion enter and exit without constancy—Confucius grasped this: when he wielded it, it remained; when he set it aside, it vanished. They come and go without fixed time, their abode unknown.

The Jade Emperor rides the Vermilion Empyrean. The Jade Emperor Lord rides the chariot of the Vermilion Empyrean to govern and command the myriad numina. The Vermilion Empyrean, also called the Cinnabar Empyrean or Crimson Empyrean, is the name of the Upper Field’s *Niwan* [mud-pill palace]. There lies the Jade Emperor’s palace, which governs the myriad spirits of the human body and presides over the lord of the myriad qi.

Verdant radiance illumines the golden ramparts. *Yong* refers to earthen walls built of piled bricks to form a small city, or the north wall within a hall. It speaks of the Jade Emperor entering the city with majestic bearing, clad in a verdant rosy dawn sash, resplendent within the golden walls. The fifth stanza of the Central Lane states: "Adorned with vermilion kerchief and verdant radiance," conveying the same meaning.

The upper abode holds the cloud-pearl within. When [qi] ascends from the two kidneys, passing through the spine’s double gates to enter *Niwan*, only a single luminous pearl remains.

The *cloud-pearl* is the pearl of the five clouds, and the five clouds are the qi transformed from the five viscera. The cloud-pearl is thus the *Mysterious Pearl Palace*. Above, it connects to the *Peak Without Blade*. At the summit of the Jade Capital Mountain, the void is without sharp edges—this describes how the crown of the human head likewise meets the boundless, blade-less expanse of emptiness. The northwest’s Kunlun Mountain has its golden city and jade towers; the human head is the same.

Below lies the *Spirit Pass of the Great Wilderness*. The *Spirit Pass* refers to the three barriers, namely the upper, middle, and lower fields. In the profound obscurity of the vast and mysterious depths—where above there is no longer color, and below no longer abyss—this is the realm of the northern *Yin* of Fengdu, the domain of hidden darkness, situated between the two kidneys.

Misty vapors surge into the empty void. The true qi steams upward, filling the hollow expanse, speaking of the human’s utmost and most unyielding qi, which pervades beyond heaven and earth, in the boundless and infinite. *Misty vapors* refer to auspicious mists and propitious clouds; *surging* means harmony.

The obscure transformation blends *Kan* and *Li*. What humans cannot see is called the *dark and hidden*. Thus, when the qi of *Kan* (Water) and *Li* (Fire) unite, it is termed *obscure darkness*. *Transformation* refers to the merging of water and fire. The *Elixir Canon* states: *"Take the solid center from the Kan position, and direct it to the Yin within the Li palace."* Thus, water and fire are the true essence of the Dao. Fu Xi’s *precelestial* water and fire are King Wen’s *postcelestial* sun and moon—their names differ, but their reality is the same. The immortals say: *"This aperture is no ordinary aperture; it is formed by the union of Qian and Kun. It is called the Cavern of Spirit and Qi, wherein reside the essences of Kan and Li."*

The hexagram names are but a summary, for *Kan* and *Li* are the mother of the myriad things. The other hexagrams follow by extension and are all complete. For those who recite this, the six positions ascend, the body transforms into pure Yang, and refined gold is transmuted, ascending into the *Golden Gate*. The *six positions* are the six lines; when *Kun* transforms into *Qian* up to the sixth, it becomes a body of pure Yang. *Kan* and *Li* are the essentials of *Wenchang*.

The *Mysterious Mysterious* is *Fire King Shu*. The *Upper Prime’s Mysterious Father* has the hidden name *Fire King Shu* and the style *Left Revolving Light*. *Mysterious Father* is the *Father of the Dao*. Some texts say *Fire Born Shu*, but according to Chapter Fourteen of the lower scroll, it is *Fire King Shu*; the present text follows this. The character *King* comes from the *Shangqing Jade Canon*.

The *Jade Tranquility* is *High Same-Born*. The *Upper Prime’s Mysterious Mother* has the hidden name *High Same-Born* and the style *Right Revolving Light*. *Mysterious Mother* is the *Mother of the Dao*. *Jade Tranquility* is the *Gate of the Female*. Some texts say *High Same King*, but since the previous line uses *King*, this should be *Born*, guarding the *Mysterious Female Gate*.

The *Limitless* protects the *Valley Youth*. The *Spirit-Soul Lord of the Central Knot* is named *Valley Youth*. *Limitless* means *inexhaustible*; *protects* means *nurtures*. He is also called the *Yellow Tranquility Youth*. He resides in the central palace of the spleen, above the *Xu* and *Si* positions, governing the spirit that digests water and grain. Clad in yellow robes, he stands in the *Yellow Court*.

The *Round Path* knows no stagnation. One version reads *without obstruction*, but *no stagnation* is more refined. The *Round Path* is the aperture within the true. *No stagnation* means the three palaces ascend and descend, circulating without cease. When the Dao’s path is open, round brilliance arises.

The *Silken Union* has nine layers. The true qi intertwines like the patterns of silk brocade, its forces interwoven and blended, its radiance as thick as nine layers. When true immortals pay homage to the Emperor, they see only golden light ablaze, not the pure countenance. When humans cultivate the true, ghosts and spirits see only red light.

To the *south*, uproot the roots of the seven ancestors. *Uproot* may also be read as *unfurl*. *Southern seven* is fire. *Unfurl* means to brush away the dust of the seven ancestors’ roots, ensuring purity so that the nine souls may be born. The nine immortals and seven ancestors all reside within the body. When one is purified, they naturally transform and arise.

To the *west*, dissolve the misfortunes of kalpas past. The west belongs to Yin, governed by the lung’s *po*. The *po* draws human emotions and desires, leading to calamity. Without the *Great Cavern’s* dissolution, even after ten thousand kalpas of dust, there would be no liberation. Thus, one restrains the seven *po* and commands the lung’s qi.

The body is vigorous, the myriad essences wave. *Vigorous* describes strength; the body is robust, and the essence-qi is lustrous. *Vigorous* is the *jiao* of *strong and unyielding*. The *myriad essence-waves* are the true water of the north, transformed into true Yang qi, rising from the kidneys to the *Mud-Pill Palace* and dripping down to the heart.

The *Spirit King* gathers the ten directions. The *Spirit King of the Ten Directions’ Flying Heavens* is the qi of wind and life. One version says *spirit born*, which is incorrect. The *Scripture of Spirit Generation* states: *"The office of the Spirit King is no small matter, and the Jade Canon commands the Five Elders to defer to the Spirit King’s judgment—this is the office of the Jade Assistant’s High Minister."*

The *Great Return* reverts to the *Womb Chariot*. Having returned to the womb and been reborn, one’s great return follows the chariot’s tracks—no longer drifting as a floating soul. The *chariot* is named for its ceaseless circulation of true qi. *Return* means reverting to the root and source; the *womb* is the *Sacred Embryo*.

The *Threefold Union* mounts the *Celestial Dragon*. With the three transformations aligned and the three unions complete, form and spirit are perfected, and one ascends riding the dragon. The term *Celestial Dragon* has five variants: *Dragon Mountain*, *Dragon Terrace*, *Dragon Radiance*, *Dragon Gem*—all share the same meaning. The *Celestial Dragon* is the dragon ridden by the Heavenly Emperor.

The above is a jade stanza of celestial script, totaling one hundred characters. Above, it governs the *Mysterious Womb’s Peaceful Nurturing Heaven*; below, it commands the *First Rampart’s Primordial Virtue Lord*. The *Mysterious Contract* states: *"Recite it four times, and the roots of dust gradually dissolve; the net of karma unravels on its own. One no longer follows the kalpas but returns, and the myriad qi converge, attaining the gate of freedom."*

The *Primordial Heavenly King* said: *"The fifth jade stanza of the Great Cavern of Wenchang corresponds to the fifth month, which generates the five viscera and the five returns with three reversions."*

*Yiyou*, *Bingxu*, *Fu*, *Wuwang*—the *Min Qi* generates the *Jing Qi*. Its color is yellow, the central single Yang’s ascending qi, congealing into the celestial realm called *Paranirmita-vaśavartin*, the *Heaven of Unsurpassed Joy*. Its kalpa is named *Upper August*. This heaven’s essence is the *Upper Yang Qi of the Spirit-Soul*, governing the *Crimson Palace’s* true viscera and the life’s origin, the *Central Spirit Qi* among the five immortals that generates the five viscera.

The *Palace of the Supreme Subtlety Heavenly Emperor* resides within the *Great Ultimate*, and within the *Supreme Subtlety* are the Twenty-Four Perfected Ones, who specialize in descending spirits, deploying qi, and nurturing life. Those who suffer miscarriage or infertility do so because the *qi of the Supreme Subtlety* fails to connect, making sustenance difficult.

The *Eight Floating* enter the *Cloud Encampment*. The *eight consciousnesses* soar and drift, entering the encampment of the *Five Clouds*—the *Five Clouds* being the five viscera, each with its golden chambers and jade halls, hence called an "encampment." The scripture states: *"Flowing echoes in the cloud encampment,"* speaking of the qi circulating through the five viscera, forming a symphony of music.

The *Spiritual Ancestor* governs the *Numinous Lapel*. The *Central Elder*, named *Spiritual Ancestor*, is the ruler of the heart, meaning the spirit’s ancestral lord orders the numinous terrace of the breast. The five spirits take the heart-spirit as their master, while the other four spirits descend in sequence to generate the five viscera and deploy the five spirits.

*Dragon Mountain* flourishes in the *Jade Capital*. The *Dragon*, wood, resides on the left as the liver. Its spirit is called the *Lord of No-Florescence* or the *Dragon’s Yang Essence*, unfathomable in transformation. It speaks of the human head taking form, where the Yang qi flourishes brilliantly, and the complexion becomes joyful, reaching upward to meet the *Peak Without Blade*.

The *Golden Chamber* is dense with radiant rosy clouds. The *Golden Chamber* is the lung viscera, where the spirit *White Prime Honored Spirit* resides, governed by the *Western Great Flower Prime Elder* of the Metal Flower. The Metal qi transforms into thick, luminous clouds of rosy brilliance, signifying the lung qi’s majestic power, steaming with lush and verdant splendor.

The *Nine Gates* gleam with lofty jade. The heart has seven apertures corresponding to the seven stars, and below are the two mysterious female orifices corresponding to the *Auxiliary* and *Assistant*, thus forming the *Nine Gates* of jade, luminous and lofty. It is also said that the head has seven orifices, with the lower region’s water and fire orifices completing the nine.

The *Yellow Court* traverses the *Northern Origin*. The *Central Spleen Palace*, as the *Yellow Court* states: *"The spleen’s palace belongs to Wu and Ji,"* hence called the *Yellow Court*. *"Traversing the Northern Origin"* refers to its upward connection with the heart’s orifices, possessing both inner and outer scenes of the *Yellow Court*, spanning above, below, and the four directions to attain the center.

The *Primal Father* turns left in brightness. The *Three Primes* and *Three Perfected*’s *Upper Primal Father Lord*, styled *Left-Turning Brightness*, guards the *Mysterious Female*. The *Primal Father* appears thrice: in the eighth chapter as *"The Primal Father knits the immortal embryo,"* and in the middle scroll’s tenth chapter as *"The Primal Father, Left-Turning Brightness"* (see prior annotations).

The *Vermilion Crystal* awakens the *Radiant Master*. *Vermilion Crystal* is the original name of the spirit guarding the heart’s right, the *White Prime Cavern-Yang Emperor Lord*, named *Vermilion Crystal*. It opens the light of the sun, moon, and *Three Primes*. The *Radiant Master* is also called the *White Prime Lord* or *Yang Essence*, each having two appellations.

The *Profound Solitude* ascends to the *Upper Clarity*. The *Great One* is named *Profound Solitude*. When the human kidney’s water ascends to congeal with the heart’s fire, the *Upper Field* becomes *Jade Clarity*, the *Middle Field* *Upper Clarity*, and the *Lower Field* *Great Clarity*. It is also said: *"The Emperor Sovereign Great One dwells in the profound void,"* styled *Profound Solitude*.

The *Four Mysteries* uphold the *Primal Prohibitions*. The *Four Numinous Beings*—*Azure Dragon*, *White Tiger*, *Vermilion Bird*, and *Dark Warrior*—grasp the prohibitions of the *Primal Conduct*. The *Four Heavenly Gate Kings* guard the celestial gates, preventing demons and ghosts from daring to intrude. In Daoist fasts and offerings, at dawn, there are commands to expel demons and avert misfortune, welcoming the descent of perfected ones and sages. When a person’s five viscera are complete, the *Four Numinous Beings* guard them. The *Three Unions*, *Four Mysteries*, *Five Emperors*, *Six Luminaries*, *Seven Awakenings*, *Eight Scenes*, *Nine Lights*, and *Ten Perfected* all pertain to the way of the sacred embryo’s firmness in the tenth month, the method of *leaving the furnace and changing the cauldron*—for the liver is the *Azure Dragon*, the lung the *White Tiger*, the heart the *Vermilion Bird*, and the kidney the *Dark Warrior*.

Eternally protect the *Five Emperor Cities*. The heart, liver, spleen, lung, and kidney are the *Five Emperor Cities*. The *Five Emperors* are: the *Azure Emperor* styled *Carved Beam’s Edge*, the *Vermilion Emperor* styled *Ever-Coming Awareness*, the *White Emperor* styled *Manifest Peace and Fortune*, the *Black Emperor* styled *Preserving Completion and Prosperity*, and the *Yellow Emperor* styled *Containing Radiance and Subtlety*.

The above jade stanza in celestial script totals sixty characters, governing above the *Primordial Luminous Writ* of the *Wenju Heaven* and commanding below the *Second Rampart’s* *Stalwart Colored Earth-Soil Sovereign*.

The *Primordial Heavenly King* said: *"The sixth jade stanza of the Great Cavern of Wenchang corresponds to the sixth month, which generates the six bowels and the six returns with four reversions."*

*Dinghai*, *Wuzi*, *Great Accumulation*, *Providence*—the *Scenic Qi* generates the *Reclusive Qi*. Its color is azure, congealing into the northeastern celestial realm called the *Heaven of Cavernous Primordial Resonance*, where the kalpa’s essence is the *Primal Yang Qi of the Spirit-Soul*, governing the *Central Cinnabar Field Palace*, the *Imperial Perfected’s* numinous mansion, and the life’s origin of the *Lofty Perfected’s* harmonious and flowing qi that generates the six bowels.

The *Purple Essence* resides in the *Great Void’s* center. The *Purple Essence Heaven* lies within the *Great Void’s* empty cavern, the colorless celestial realm where the *Three Clarities* reside. In humans, this corresponds to the *Heavenly Valley*, the gathering place of the myriad spirits, also called the *Great Void*—formless and imageless.

The *Three Origins* ascend the *Upper Scenic Way*. The *Three Origins* are the *Chaotic Great Void Origin*, the *Vermilion Chaotic Great Void Origin*, and the *Profound Stillness Mysterious Penetration Origin*. The three qi ascend the *Upper Scenic Way*, speaking of the human qi circulating endlessly through the upper, middle, and lower fields, returning to the *Mud-Pill Palace*.

The *Great Treasure* shines with luminous brilliance. The *Great Treasure* is the *Jade Emperor’s* throne, pure and radiant. It speaks of the human *Mysterious Pearl’s* resplendence, the *Azure Fox’s* millet-grain pearl, all called the *Great Treasure*. The *Heavenly Perfected* are noble and weighty, possessing radiant brilliance, hence called the *Great Treasure*.

The *Luminous* fans the *Emperor’s* spread. One version says *"Vast and distant,"* while *"Luminous"* means manifest. *"Fanning"* refers to the *Jade Emperor* ascending the *Great Treasure*, where his pure light and majestic flames fan forth, just as in inner alchemy, where flames burst forth from the central palace.

The *Elder Scribe* awakens the *Three Primes*. The *Yellow Court’s* *Primal King of the Life Gate*, named *Elder Scribe*, is originally the *Three-One Spirit*—the *Upper One* the *Red Child*, the *Middle One* the *Primal Emperor*, and the *Lower One* the *Primal King*, also named *Original Essence* styled *Primal Yang*, or *Infant*. The *Embryo* awakens the *Three Prime Lords*.

The Emperor ascends to the Jade Void.
"Emperor" denotes the sovereign; without the myriad qi, the human body cannot nurture the myriad spirits. Yet at the center of the myriad spirits resides the Emperor-King—where the heart directs, the myriad spirits obey. "Ascending the Jade Void" refers to the upper Mud-Pill Palace, the Gate of the Brain.

Auspicious qi nurtures the Five Clouds.
Five-colored auspicious clouds and propitious mists surround and uphold the Jade Emperor. East with three, South with two together make five; North with one, West with four share in them. Five is the generative number of wu-ji, where the Three Families meet to form the Embryo-Brother. The Five Clouds are also called the Five Spirits.

The Deity of Destiny commands the luminous inception.
The Deity of Destiny governs the Palace of the Heart, named *Li Mingchu*. The heart-palace is the abode of luminous spirits; "inception" signifies the first shaping, referring to the heart-viscus. From its emptiness arises awareness, and upon it depends the span of human life—hence it is called the Deity of Destiny.

The Ten Radiant Flowers perfect the immortal’s wondrous practice.
The ten directions’ radiant splendor, their wondrous practice perfected, attest to the attainment of immortality. The Ten Radiant Flowers are: Azure Flower, Cinnabar Flower, Plain Flower, Mysterious Flower, Yellow Flower, Jade Flower, Golden Flower, Green Flower, Jasper Flower, and Jadeite Flower—together comprising the wondrous practice of the Ten Flowers.

Subduing demons gives rise to the Six Luminances.
The Six Luminances are the six roots. In humans, they first generate the five viscera, then the six bowels. The free flow between viscera and bowels becomes the mansion of the Six Luminances. The six bowels are: gallbladder, stomach, bladder, large intestine, small intestine, and navel—collectively termed the Six Bowels.

The above Jade Stanza in celestial script comprises fifty characters, governing above the *Upper Radiance* of the *Seven Luminaries* and *Māyā Heaven*, and ruling below the *Second Rampart* of the *August Virtue Lord*.
The *Mysterious Concord* states: Reciting it six times severs forever the demonic blades of the Six Heavens, purifies the six roots with vast clarity, and engenders the myriad qi to shine in unison—whereupon one transcends the world and enters the Gate of Immortality.

The Primordial Heavenly King declares: The *Great Cavern Jade Stanza, Seventh Chapter*, opens the seven apertures of the heart in the seventh month, achieving the Seven Returns and Five Reversions.
*Ji-chou*, *Great Exceedance*, *Kǎn*.
*Kǎn* and *lí* bear no branches or stems.
Mysterious qi generates harmonious qi, its color black, congealing to form the northwestern celestial realm, named *Linghua Brahmā-Assistant Heaven*. This heaven’s essence-spirit is the qi of true yang, presiding over the *Primal Valley Palace*. The *Imperial Perfected* of the *Primal Mansion* and the *High Immortals* of the *Cavern-Script* open the seven apertures of the heart.

The True Yang Emperor receives the Elder Guest.
The *Rites* state: The Son of Heaven bares his arm to carve the sacrificial beast, kneeling to present the spoon.

Awaiting the Rites of the Three Elders—what is called "nurturing the aged and entreating their counsel." Now the True Yang serves as the Jade Emperor’s Elder Guest, also named the Left Immortal of the *Zhengyi*, whose personal name is *Binlao*, and who is further styled *Zhongchengzi*. He receives his duties in the assembly of the Jade Sovereign. Each gathering convenes at the *Jade Void*, where he receives the Jade Emperor’s affairs, just as the True Yang makes its audience at the *Muddy Pellet of Nine*—this is called the "silent audience before the Supreme Emperor." The method employs the *Purple River Chariot*, transporting it from the *Weilü* into the brain; after twelve years, one attains immortality.

It extinguishes demons and purges the foul corpse,
subduing the demon kings and vanquishing their treachery,
eradicating the heads of malevolent spirits,
and expelling the impure qi of corpses and blood.
Once yang qi arises, yin qi naturally dissipates—such is the principle.

Demons are the trials by which the Emperor-Kings of all heavens test whether the human heart is steadfast. The hundred bureaus proceed to the *Crimson Palace*. The human *Dantian Palace* is called the *Crimson Palace*, which is the heart’s residence. The spirits of the hundred meridians constantly attend this palace to receive commands, for the heart is the lord of the myriad spirits. All spirits pay audience to their sovereign, and the principles of the myriad affairs and things reside therein.

The *Leisurely Abode* lies within the *Cinnabar Mystery*,
the dwelling of ease within the *Dantian*,
one inch above which is the *Mystery-Cinnabar Palace* in the head.
There, the primordial spirit gathers and congeals the myriad qi,
ascending to return to the *Leisurely Abode* of the *Mystery-Cinnabar Palace*,
the gate for refining and practicing the yang spirit’s ingress and egress.

The five qi bind the ten directions:
the qi of the five directions—
nine qi in the east,
three qi in the south,
seven qi in the west,
five qi in the north,
and one qi in the center—
flow like the qi of the five viscera,
circulating throughout the body’s interior and exterior, reaching everywhere without exception.

The *Seven Revolutions* summon the *Controller of Destiny*;
when the *Seven Returns and Nine Reversions* are complete, the Dao of the elixir is achieved.
The arrival of the *Controller of Destiny* signifies the perfection of the Way of longevity and enduring vision.
The *Controller of Destiny* is the spirit of the heart, also called the *Seven Revolutions Summoning the Controller of Destiny*.
The *Seven Revolutions* occur when the seven yang metal qi encounter fire to form the elixir.

The *Three Returns* summon the *Immortal Duke*.
The *Three Harmonies* form the sound that summons the *Immortal Duke*,
one of the five ranks of immortals—*Duke, Marquis, Earl, Viscount, and Baron*—
such as the *Supreme Ultimate Immortal Duke*.
Now, the *Immortal Duke* is the *Eastern Florescence Wood Palace*, overseer of the liver.

The *Lord of Mount Tai* governs ghosts,
the *Lord of Mount Tai* presides over the affairs of ghosts and spirits—
this is the *Sacred Emperor of the Eastern Peak*.
*Tai* is *Great*; the mountain lies in Yanzhou,
foremost of the Five Marchmounts, thus called *Daizong*,
belonging to the east’s wood, the realm of generation and transformation.

Hasten to audit the records of the Three Officials’ midst.
The Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water audit the registers of life and death, sin and fortune in their palaces.
"Hasten" means swiftness without haste.
The Three Primordial Officials’ bureaus number one hundred twenty,
convening thrice yearly—on the first, seventh, and tenth months—to conduct their impeccable audits.

The ten virtues lay the initial foundation.
The *Ten Virtues* correspond to the central earth’s number, governing the spleen and stomach’s grain qi to generate fluids.
The *Ten Virtues* form the foundation of perfect fortune:
the rooster possesses five virtues, humans ten, and all things at least one.
Human luminous virtue is bestowed by heaven,
endowed in all beings without deficit or excess.
Yet the passions and desires obscure it, leading to benightedness.
Thus, the *Primordial Beginning* desires that humans cultivate this Way,
rooting the perfection of virtue—this is called "knowing the origin lies in illuminating luminous virtue."
The *Ten Virtues* are recorded in the eighth chapter of the *Mystery Contract* in the *Lower Lane*; here, they are not reiterated.

Together, they ascend with the *Seven Awakening Primes*.
Awakening leads to perfect enlightenment; failure to awaken leaves one a common mortal.
The *Seven Awakenings* are the heart,
whose spirit ascends to communicate through the seven apertures—eyes, ears, nose, and mouth.
Thus, the seven apertures open to keen perception,
the seven stars shine brightly,
and the adept ascends with them into the *Seven Primes* of the Dipper.

The *Seven Awakenings* are the *Conscious Spirit*:
first, innate knowledge;
second, knowledge enabling perception;
third, perception enabling compliance;
fourth, compliance enabling practice;
fifth, practice enabling steadfastness;
sixth, steadfastness enabling accomplishment;
seventh, accomplishment without attachment—
these are the *Seven Awakenings*.
One who can practice them advances to sublime conduct and attains the rank of flying immortal.

These jade-script celestial seal characters, sixty in number, govern above the Void Transcending Heng Heaven and command below the Second Rampart of the August Virtue Lord.

The *Mysterious Contract* states: Recite them seven times, and the Seven Prime Dipper Consorts descend to erase the adept’s name from the ledgers of death, transferring it to the Southern Palace. The ten thousand qi ascend in unison, and one enters the Gate of Flying Immortals.

The Celestial Venerable of Primordial Beginning declares: This is the Eighth Jade Chapter of the Great Cavern of Wenchang. In the eighth month, the Eight Radiant Spirits generate the divine, and the human returns through six reversions. Gengyin, Li, Xian. Fused qi generates flaming qi, its color cinnabar, congealing into the southeastern celestial realm called High Void Luminous Heaven. This heaven’s essence-spirit communicates the yang qi, presiding over the Palace of Ultimate Yin. The Imperial Perfected of the Hua Mansion commands the primordial numinous-transformative qi to generate the Three Divisions and Eight Radiant Spirits.

The Three Primes of Primordial Simplicity—these Three Primes are the Three Divisions. Each division has eight nodes, also called the Three Primes, namely the spirit, qi, and essence. The Three Simplicities of the Primordial Mother are the feminine unity’s spirit, gathering in the Lower Prime at midnight, the Middle Prime at noon, and the Upper Prime at dusk, ascending and descending through the Three Palaces.

At dawn, ascend the Hall of Vast Spirit. The Hall of Vast Spirit is the heart’s mansion. At the first cock’s crow, ascend to the Crimson Palace, for the yang qi is newly born. The Three Simplicities of the Primordial Mother are also the spirits who impeach and report sins and blessings, presenting the worldly person’s transgressions. Thus, recite the scripture at early dawn to repel them.

The Jade Capital manifests the mysterious register. The Jade Capital Mountain is where the registers of all immortals reside. Those who cultivate the Dao should, at the midnight hour when the first yang stirs, sit in stillness to calm the heart, pay homage to the ten thousand qi, and avoid the recording of human transgressions and blessings before the Jade Emperor by the spirits who submit reports.

Guard the life-gate and preserve the Dao’s well-being. The Peach Well Lord guards the life-gate at the navel. Wang Shuhe identified the right kidney as the life-gate, for human life and death reside in the kidneys; when the kidneys fail, the life pulse ceases. One version mistakenly writes "child" for "kernel." Moreover, the peach kernel harmonizes with the flourishing radiance of life.

The revolving wind disperses the ten thousand demons. At midnight, yin and yang merge to perfect the Dao of the Imperial One. Thus, one can dispel the ten thousand demons, for yang arises as yin recedes. This is the time when the noble’s Dao grows while the petty’s Dao wanes—the Dao of revolving wind and fusion.

The golden talisman summons the Vast Realm. With the golden talisman, summon the Vast Wilderness, the realm of ultimate yin, so that the ethereal souls may all receive rebirth. One version reads "deliver the minister," which is doubtful. The Vast Realm refers to the Northern Yin Fengdu. The kidney division pertains to water, and metal generates water.

Assist and protect the earthly gate within. Guard and support the earthly gate, storing the generative qi in the lower field. As the *Book* says: "Attend to the bright mandate of Heaven." The earthly gate is the life-gate of the lower division. Cherish and protect it; do not corrupt it with lust and desire.

Preserve this King of Longevity. In heaven, there is the Jade Pure Perfected King, the Great Emperor of Longevity, who exclusively holds the power of generation and transformation. Within the human, preserve and guard the King of My Longevity and Deathlessness—this is the indestructible primordial spirit through eons, the root of the sacred embryo.

Turn and enter the Ten Immortal Gates. The Gates of Wondrous Observation—there are ten kinds of immortal gates: the Unobstructed Gate, the Gate of Concentrated Contemplation, the Gate of Myriad Wonders, the Gate of Subtlety and Silence, the Gate of Self-Mastery, the Gate of Longevity, the Gate of Immortal Advancement, the Gate of Flying Immortals, the Gate of Flying Spirits, and the Gate of Perfected Ascent.

The Eight Radiant Spirits unite in the Cavern Yang. The Eight Radiant Spirits and Eight Gates are all portals within the body through which the spirit and qi exit and enter. It is also said: The Three Divisions and Eight Radiant Spirits enter together the Cavern Yang Palace. The Vermilion Mound Fire Mansion refines the essence in the Jade Pupil, and the Yellow Florescence washes the form.

These jade-script celestial seal characters, fifty in number, govern above the Supreme Ultimate Veiled Heaven and command below the Second Rampart of the August Virtue Lord.

The *Mysterious Contract* states: Recite them eight times, and the Eight Radiant Spirits are born. The Eight Mighty Spirit Kings guard and protect the cultivator of the real. The eight heavens in the four directions record the immortal’s name, sever the earthly gate, and forever cut off the roots of evil. The ten thousand qi shine in unison, and one enters the Gate of Flying Spirits.

The Celestial Venerable of Primordial Beginning declares: This is the Ninth Jade Chapter of the Great Cavern of Wenchang. In the ninth month, the Nine Houses open and communicate, and the nine return through seven reversions. Xinmao, Renchen, Heng, Dun. Flaming qi generates evolving qi, its color white, congealing into the southwestern celestial realm called the Heaven of No Thought, No Knots, No Attachment. This heaven’s essence-spirit germinates the yang qi, presiding over the Lower Cinnabar Field Palace. The Imperial Perfected of the Yue Mansion commands the primordial natural mysterious illumination qi to permeate the nine apertures.

The Purple Essence nurtures the Flourishing Forest. The term "Purple Essence" appears four times, all referring to celestial realms, though some versions contain errors; here, all are annotated. In the first chapter of the upper scroll, "Ascending the Purple Clarity in Leisure"; in the first chapter of the lower scroll, "Ascending the Purple Clarity in Ease"—both are heavens where the Primordial Beginning abides. In the sixth chapter of the upper scroll, "Purple Essence within the Great Nonbeing," the Purple Essence Heaven is formed by the congealing of the Three Primes’ qi, governed by a Perfected Lord named the Three Primes Purple Essence Lord. In this ninth chapter, "Purple Essence Nurtures the Flourishing Forest," it refers to the Purple Essence Heaven of the Upper Clarity realm, where there is a Flourishing Forest with leaves like bamboo, flowers like mirrors, and fruit like plums. Heavenly beings who eat of it attain long life without aging and ascend as upper immortals. An ancient poem says: "In the Purple Essence Heaven’s Flourishing Forest, / Crimson fruit and vermilion branches, bamboo leaves deep. / Chewing the lush blossoms, one does not age; / Below, one watches the birds and hares exchange the light of time." Yet this is not a sight the lower realms can behold.

Within the human, the kidney water is black, the heart fire red. When these two qi unite, they transform into pure yang, and the purple golden essence flourishes into a forest. When the fruit ripens, one’s true self may partake of it to cultivate the Dao of longevity. As in the *Chapter on Generating the Spirit*, which speaks of "the jade blossoms and yellow flourishes, the wild and luxuriant branches of the jade forest in the life-gate," and the *Wenchang Scripture*, which says, "The cinnabar forest flourishes with vermilion branches"—all convey this meaning, illustrating what the human should nurture.

Within the Great Void beyond all bounds lies the Long Slumber.
"Slumber" means absolute stillness, unmoving—like one who sleeps without departing. The "Great Void" is the realm of emptiness and quiescence, as when the monk Budai or Chen Tuan slept for months on end, dust gathering upon their bodies—true breath in profound stillness.

From the Jade Chamber, treasure clouds arise.
The Jade Chamber—also called the space between the brows—is the aperture of the viscera and joints. Naturally, it generates clouds of five-colored *qi*; where vital *qi* is born, spirit is born. The scriptures speak of the "Golden Chamber and Jade Abode" and the "Purple Portal and Jade Palace" where spirit is simultaneously generated—all of the same meaning.

Within the nine-gated womb and embryo.
Nine revolutions, nine returns—thus the elixir path is complete. The embryo gestates for nine months, the nine *qi* coalescing, and the human path is perfected. This passage describes the eighth month fulfilled, nearing the ninth, *qi* replete and spirit complete, the sacred embryo whole, awaiting the moment of stirring.

The Imperial Guest presents the Jade Talisman.
Not the Emperor presenting *my* talisman—Chapter Six speaks of the "True Yang Imperial Guest, the Elder." The Imperial Guest is the yang spirit, charged with dispelling yin evil, bearing the Jade Talisman to act, like the Three Elders of the state who uphold the sovereign’s decree to rectify governance.

The Three Lights return beneath the Purple Canopy.
The Three Lights of heaven are the sun, moon, and stars; the Three Lights of the human are the two eyes and the heart. When the sun and moon lose their measure, stars linger or hide, and heaven and earth suffer calamity. When the eyes are beguiled and the heart moved, the body falters. "Return beneath the Purple Canopy" means that when the eyes do not gaze upon evil sights nor the ears hear evil sounds, when one withdraws vision and reverses hearing, spirit is preserved and *qi* congeals. The Purple Canopy covers all without exception. Thus, the two eyes are called the radiant canopy of the nine apertures. As the sun, moon, and stars illuminate heaven and earth, the two eyes and the heart oversee the body, shielding it from external obstructions.

The Azure Jade *Bin* comes to life.
*Wufu* is stone resembling jade, used to counterfeit it—now transformed into true jade. In this passage, the Black *Qi* Lord is named *Binlaisheng*, who governs the inner illumination of human virtue. "Azure" (*cang*) is not written as "granary" (*cang*); it refers to the blue-green jade, signifying the emergence of veined patterns. Jade is compared to virtue: without perfect virtue, the perfect Dao does not coalesce. When inner cultivation is profound, its radiance shines forth externally—like jade within a mountain, where no grass or tree fails to flourish; like a pearl in the depths, where rivers and streams are all clarified; like a treasure held within, where the face glows with luster and the body thrives in health.

Guard this through the Long Night Assembly.
The Long Night Assembly resides in the Crimson Palace, the numinous treasury, the place where blood is generated. When awake, it is ever bright; when unaware, it is ever dark. "Guard" means to correct and rescue from evil. Those who cannot cherish it remain in the endless night—when will dawn come?

The Five Spirits bestow the register of passage.
The Five Spirits are the Azure Spirit, Vermilion Spirit, Luminous Spirit, Mysterious Spirit, and Yellow Spirit. "Bestow" means to confer—the Five Elders grant me the register of longevity. The *Jade Scripture* of Mount Mao omits the following six lines, concluding here.

The Nine Governances unite with the Nine Lights.
The method of the Nine Governances is to gather the talismans of the Emperor’s Nine Lights to assemble the spirits. This is the Dao of returning wind and merging as one. When the number nine is encountered, yang is abundant—this yang is pure and unceasing. The *Great Cavern Scripture* states: "From the One *qi* arises the Two *qi*, from the Two *qi* arises the Nine *qi*." Nine yang is the extreme number, then it transforms into duality, becoming thirty-six. There is the "Empress of the Nine Lights, the Holy Mother of the True One," who presides over matters of birth and nurture. Some say: "The *Original Scripture*—this must be an error." "Governance" (*tong*) means record; in high antiquity, the Nine Sovereigns had nine records, as found in ancient texts.

The Three Mysteries emerge from the Grand Clarity.
The Three Mysteries are the Three Threes, the Nine Mysteries. "Emerge from the Grand Clarity" refers to the Lower Field, externally corresponding to the Northern Capital of Fengdu, internally to the two kidneys. It speaks of the ancestors and progenitors transcending this realm, where the spirit ascends to the Nine Heavens, forever becoming a perfected one.

The Purple Yang gives rise to the myriad beings.
The Jade Treasury of Purple Yang is the palace of life’s generation, whence the roots of all existence across ten thousand generations are activated, and all spirits are complete. Regardless of rank, all humans emerge from the arising of Purple Yang—this principle of ceaseless generation endures forever.

The Mysterious Essence nurtures the Nine Spirits.
The Mysterious Essence nurtures the Nine Souls. Heaven takes the north as mysterious; humans take the heart as mysterious. The Nine Spirits are the nine apertures of the heart. The Nine Mysteries receive life because the Nine Souls are nurtured, enabling the formation of the embryo. Thus, the essence is bathed in the Great Yang.

The Primordial Father forms the Embryo Immortal.
The Primordial Father, as noted earlier, is the heart’s office of thought—also called intention. The "Embryo Immortal" possesses *qi* but no breath. The lower scroll speaks of the "Purple Flower leading the Embryo Immortal," and the *Yellow Court Scripture* says: "The zither heart in triple layers dances with the Embryo Immortal"—both express the same meaning.

---

The above Jade Stanza, in celestial script, comprises seventy characters, and above it governs the Crimson Brightness and Harmonious Yang Heaven, the third celestial governance of the Earth Sovereign of the Cinnabar-Colored Land.

The *Mysterious Contract* states: "Recite it nine times, and the Nine Governances of the Emperor convene, the Nine Light Spirits assemble, the hundred spirits merge as one, and one’s years equal those of heaven. The Eight Assemblies gather in wandering, paying homage to the Nine Heavens. The ten thousand *qi* ascend together as immortals, attaining the Gate of Perfection."

The Primordial Heavenly King says: "This is the tenth Jade Stanza of the *Great Cavern of Wenchang*, the month when form and spirit are firmly consolidated, and the embryo is transformed through spiritual transcendence."

*Gui-si*, *Jia-wu*, *Great Strength*, *Advance*.

The pure radiance of Brahma’s clear luminous *qi*, its colors blue, yellow, and white, congeals to form the Central Heavenly Realm, called the *Boli Dahuo* Heaven. Within this heaven, the *qi* of central yang presides over the Yellow Court Palace of the Middle Prime, where the Imperial True *qi* of Harmonious Balance descends to infuse spirit and distribute *qi*, solidifying form and essence, giving rise to the human path.

The Azure Spirit fans the Eight Extremities.
The Eastern Beginning Elder is the land of arising, thus fanning and stirring the world of the Eight Extremities. The Eight Extremities are the four cardinal and four intermediate directions—the Eight Trigrams: *Qian*, *Kan*, *Gen*, *Zhen*, *Xun*, *Li*, *Kun*, *Dui*; the Eight Gates: Open, Rest, Life, Wound, Barrier, View, Death, Fright.

The Wheel Drums the Three Flowers’ Citadel
The Three Flowers are the *shen*, *qi*, and *jing*; the Citadel is where the Three Flowers reside. The Azure Spirit’s *qi* drums and arouses the intent of arising. The Wheel is the name of the tongue spirit—when one drums the root of the tongue, stirring the Jade Pond’s fluids to irrigate the Three Fields.

Breaking the Knots of the Womb-Cauldron
*Breaking* (alternately *uprooting*): The *Scripture on Generating Spirit* states, “Sever the stagnant roots of the womb-tree.” The meaning is the same—*breaking* means to brush away, to untie, to dissolve the knotted roots of womb-cauldron habits. As the *Scripture on Generating Spirit* says, “When the womb-knots’ roots are untied,” this is precisely the meaning.

The Seven Ancestors Receive Blessings and Rebirth
The Nine Mysteries’ Seven Ancestors receive these blessings and ascend to heaven, enjoying bliss. If one can advance with diligence and unceasing cultivation, one ascends to the Formless Heavens, attains the Stage of Non-Retrogression, and ultimately climbs to the position of attendant minister in the Great Lofty Three Realms of the Supreme Perfected.

Karmic Adversaries Vanish Across the Five Paths
The *Scripture on Generating Spirit* states, “When karmic adversaries exhaust the great cycle of destiny, they are eradicated.” One eliminates the enmity of past lives and extinguishes the malevolent affairs of the Five Paths. The Five Paths are hell, hungry ghosts, animals, *asuras*, and birds and insects—realms from which escape is difficult.

Constantly Guard the Imperial One’s Camp
Maoshan divides this into two sections: the Feminine One, the Masculine One, and the Imperial One are called the Way of the Three Ones. Here, one guards only the Imperial One’s camp, for it is the most revered—the Great Cavern’s Imperial One. The Hidden Teachings include the *Scripture of the Feminine One* and the *Scripture of the Masculine One*.

The Duke’s Son Holds the Five Talismans
The Left Radiant Duke’s Son, styled *Xuanyuan Shu*, aligns the talismans. Riding the *qi* of the Nine Yangs of the East, he grasps the Five Spirits’ talismans, nurturing the myriad beings. He summons the Nine *Hun* Spirits within the liver, dispersing them throughout the world—thus the human path is born.

The Supreme One Dwells in the Purple Chamber
