The Primordial Beginning declared: “This Azure Grain Treasure and the *Sandalwood Fire Lute Tone*—were it not for the Great Mystery, who could seek and receive them? Only your compassion is profound and your vows weighty; thus, the precious scripture may be entrusted to you.”

The Primordial Beginning further admonished the Dao Father: “When gathered, this scripture is the Azure Grain Treasure; when dispersed, it is the *Sandalwood Fire Lute Tone*. It is most noble and weighty. Were it not for you, who would dare to seek it? Only your heart is deeply compassionate toward beings, and your vow to deliver them is most earnest—therefore, the precious scripture may be entrusted to you. Between master and disciple in the transmission of the Three Treasures, the exhortations are most earnest and repeated, and the protection most solemn. How much less could lesser immortals of lower rank easily hear of it? I see that in the world, those who lightly transmit or secretly leak it, or who slander it, will surely face unseen retribution. This is an inner teaching: if one is not of the Great Mystery, even a single point of true yang can form the elixir—thus, the precious scripture may be bestowed.”

The Primordial Heavenly King said: “*The Jade Chapters of the Great Cavern of Wenchang*, Twenty-First Scroll: ‘Heaven One generates water, one mysterious practice.’
*Yi-mao, bing-chen, Travel, Xun.*
The qi of the Nine August Upper Perfected.”

The Nine August Ones exist in Heaven as the Nine August, on Earth as the Nine August, among the stars as the Nine August, and among the perfected immortals as the Nine August. In recent times, figures such as Zhang Pingshu were all Nine August Perfected, who, having erred in calculating the kalpas’ fortunes, were demoted to the mortal realm. The *Scripture of Salvation* states: “Recite it on one’s natal day to attain the Nine Palaces’ Perfected.” All are transformations of the primordial qi of the Mysterious Origin and Supreme Perfected—namely, the nine qi received in the ninth month, as mentioned in the preceding scroll. It also likens the nine palaces of the human head to the Nine Heavens, and the nine orifices of the body to the Nine Lands and Nine Provinces. Some regard them as the nine true qi: the one true within the heart, the two true in the stomach cavity, the three true of essence and blood, the four true in the liver, the five true in the spleen, the six true in the lungs, the seven true in the kidneys, the eight true in the gallbladder, and the nine true in the Mud Pill Palace. These are the nine qi of the Nine Emperor Perfected that generate the spirit, sharing a single origin under different names—the convergence of the thirty-six palaces.

The Four Celestial Governors are the Four Heavenly Kings. On the eight seasonal nodes, they command the Four Emperors of the Three Realms to refine and transform those who cultivate immortality. The Azure Lad presides over the Eastern Florescence Palace, the Upper Primordial Sovereign over the Vermilion Numinous Palace, the Queen Mother over the Western Florescence Palace, and the Jade Clarity Sovereign over the Northern Supreme Palace. They also symbolize the four numina of humanity: metal, wood, water, and fire. Earth has no fixed form but flourishes in the four seasons—represented by the earthly branches *chen*, *xu*, *chou*, and *wei*—while *wu* and *ji* are the true earth of the center, called the Earthly August. The Four Governors are also said to be the Celestial Governors of Fate, Fortune, Wrongdoing, and Peril, while the Terrestrial Governors are those of Fate, Fortune, Merit, and Destruction. The scriptures state: “The earthly immortals of Heaven are the Celestial Four Governors.” For humans, the four governors are the eyes governing sight, the ears governing hearing, the nose governing scent, and the tongue governing taste. Confucian texts call them the five senses, which must all remain upright, unassailed by deviant qi.

The flying rosy clouds scatter the sun of Heaven,
Heaven is mysterious and Earth is yellow.
“Scatter the sun of Heaven” means each displays its true color. For each heaven has its own sun, moon, stars, and celestial perfected, whose flying rosy clouds disperse radiance, outshining the sun of Heaven. This likens the four qi of humanity to clarity and brightness, illuminating the primordial yang.

They congeal and blaze within the Six Harmonies’ chamber.
“Congeal” means to coalesce; “blaze,” to shine. The celestial perfected’s flying rosy clouds disperse radiance, congealing and blazing between Heaven and Earth. This likens the great elixir’s completion to a luminous brilliance within the upper field, called the Six Harmonies’ chamber—namely, the brain palace.

The Supreme Perfected ascend to pay court to the Jade Clarity,
The perfected immortals of the heavens must also compose their dignity and pay court to the Jade Clarity Supreme Emperor. This likens human cultivation to taking the center as its foundation, gathering the qi of the four numina to ascend to the Mud Pill Palace, called “paying court to the origin.” With time, one may govern as a divine immortal.

Riding the radiance within the dawn’s splendor.
“Dawn’s splendor” refers to the realm of the sun and moon—namely, the two eyes in humans. This speaks of riding the chariot of the sun and moon. The perfected, when ascending to court, all ride chariots, their radiance resplendent. The great elixir’s path involves the three chariots—ox, deer, and goat—transporting and refining, ascending to the summit of Kunlun. The celestial perfected possess the chariot of dawn’s splendor and rosy clouds. Later texts speak of “harnessing the radiance to ascend the absolute empyrean,” confirming that “radiance” refers to the chariot and the sun and moon at its sides. “Splendor” denotes brilliant radiance, describing the elixir’s ascent along the Yellow Path. The scriptures say: “The warm leaden crucible’s light pierces the curtains.”

The Five Celestial Bodies are called the Triggering Mechanism,
These are not the Northern Celestial Pole but the Lord of Essence and Spirit, named the Triggering Mechanism—namely, the five qi and five celestial bodies: *ren-zi*, *wu-zi*, *jia-zi*, *bing-zi*, and *geng-zi*. These are called the “Five *zi* Returning to *geng*” or the “Five Elders Opening the Way.” The “mechanism” is the pivotal joint: when the qi of the five viscera’s misty fusion triggers its articulation, they may coalesce into the four numina. “Celestial bodies” also refer to the supreme pole’s celestial cycles—epochs, kalpas, and generations—circulating endlessly between Heaven and Earth. The *Scripture of Salvation* states: “Revolving the Dipper and traversing the Winnowing Basket, cycling through the Five Constants.” The Five Constants are the five celestial bodies and five phases.

Bearing the registers to present to the Vacuous August.
The perfected each hold tablets and registers, recording the merits and transgressions of mortals. The Vacuous August is the Jade Emperor, who exclusively governs the affairs of the upper heavens and realms. This likens the true qi of humanity, gathering from the nine passes and hundred joints into the Mud Pill Palace.

Leisurely ascending the Purple Clarity,
The Purple Clarity Heaven is the sacred realm of the Jade Clarity where the Primordial Origin resides. “Leisurely” refers to the chariot—some say it shares the name *huilu* with the spirit of the nine passes, a term of profound obscurity. Here, *lü* should be read as a color.

The golden tally is inscribed in the Feather Palace.
The golden tally and jade tablets record the names of divine immortals. The Feather Palace is the light, floating abode transformed by Brahman qi, also called the “feather tone” of water. Without metal, the great elixir has no body, for metal is the elixir’s mother that generates water.

Receiving the dark-green barbarian pearls,
The perfected all receive the five-colored dark-green pearls of Cang Jie. This likens the elixir’s completion to the coagulation of the myriad qi, receiving the attendance of the hundred spirits in homage. “Dark-green barbarian” is explained in the middle scroll’s commentary as the lead and mercury of human nature and destiny.

Vastly aiding and ascending the Universal Radiance.
“Vast” means great; “aiding,” to ferry across. All must attain their proper place. In humans, this means vastly propagating beneficence to ascend the Hall of Universal Radiance. The sage’s intent is universally inclusive, ensuring all above and below find their rightful place.

Transporting and delivering the people of the Mysterious Center,
The Supreme Simplicity is the mysterious qi. Those to be delivered are determined by the kalpas’ reckoning without regard to fate. Those who accord with the Dao are to be delivered. The “people of the Mysterious Center” are like those in the *Scripture of Spirit Generation*, which states: “Several tens of thousands are destined to be delivered.” Having attained the Dao, one must emerge into the world to deliver others.

Swallowing and savoring the five sprouts.

Savor, then, is the fluid beneath the tongue, corresponding to Heaven’s Water. When those of the Mysterious Center attain the Dao of rinsing and swallowing to irrigate, they shall generate the Five Sprout Pearls—namely, the quintessence of the five viscera congealing into five flavors, sweet and pungent, fit for swallowing.

Gathering to form the Womb Immortal,
A woman’s gestation occurs in the lower field, opposite the kidneys, called the Womb Field. If a man constantly nurtures womb-breathing and congeals spirit-qi, he shall be free from hunger, thirst, cold, or heat’s disturbances. When the yang-spirit departs and returns, this is called the Womb Immortal.

The Elixir Mother preserves pure yang.
The Great Elixir’s mother is composed of pure yang. Without transmuting yin-qi, the elixir cannot form—this is called the Golden Tripod’s Dragon-Tiger Great Medicine. Kun is the mother, as the Scripture states: “Born in Kun, sown in Qian.” At sixteen, a woman’s celestial menses descend; at fifteen, a man’s celestial essence flows. At birth, humans are of pure yang substance, corresponding to the Qian hexagram. From fifteen, when essence is discharged, to twenty-five, the first line breaks into yin, forming the Gou hexagram. At thirty-five, the second line breaks, forming the Dun hexagram; at forty-five, the third, forming the Pi hexagram; at fifty-five, the fourth, forming the Guan hexagram; at sixty-five, the fifth, forming the Bo hexagram; at seventy-five, the sixth line breaks, forming the Kun hexagram—pure yin. When the yang lines are exhausted, death approaches.

Yin and yang harmonize, inherently possessing the principle of endless generation. Upon reaching middle age, when men and women are fully developed, one may cease desire and refine the Elixir Mother to preserve pure yang and restore original nature.

Host and guest unite in the primordial model.
The Chan gate states: “Guest within host, host within guest,” as when Sudhana visited fifty-three spiritual guides. Here, primordial qi serves as the host, while postnatal qi attends it. *Yuanfan* is the method—following the model, the compass, and the carpenter’s square.

To refine the Golden Elixir, one must guard speech, moderate diet, and reduce sleep—these three come first. Next, spread a thick sitting mat, loosen clothing and belt, align the body, straighten the spine, let lips and teeth meet, press the tongue to the upper palate, slightly open the eyes, and constantly gaze at the tip of the nose. None of these eight may be omitted; this is what it means to unite with the primordial model.

The Supreme Simplicity generates Mysterious Radiance.
The Supreme Simplicity existed at the dawn of primordial chaos. The Limitless stirred into yang, giving birth to Heaven’s First Water and the Supreme Simplicity’s qi—hence called *Tai Xuan*. *Xuan* means black, referring to the water-qi’s initial emergence, black in hue; thus, it is called Mysterious Radiance. This is the primordial spark of numinous clarity, called *nature*. From the formless, numinous life arises—this is called *spirit*. Spirit, then, is that which wondrously fashions the myriad things. Before entering the mortal shell, it flows above and below in unison with Heaven and Earth. Once embodied, it attaches to specific loci. Without this numinous essence, humans would be but inert matter. Spirit resides in the Mud Pill Palace.

The above jade verse in celestial script comprises ninety characters, governing above the Supreme Venerable Elder of the Heavy Floating Heaven and below the Sixth Stratum’s Iron Marsh Earth Sovereign.

The *Mysterious Contract* states: “The Supreme Simplicity’s singular mystery practices the Gate of Breath-Cessation. Qi circulates, first entering the root of nature, beginning at the ground of the heart. Gradually, it grows, flourishing into a forest. This arises from severing doubt and generating faith and understanding—hence called one degree of cultivation, one bend of water and sky. Performing a hundred deeds, one progresses from hearing to seeing. One harmony contains all, originating from initial hearing. Thus, the Heavenly Treasure reveals its radiance, the Black Emperor unblocks the blood, the Northern Dipper casts off death, and the name is fixed in the Mysterious Register.”

The Primordial Heavenly King states: “The twenty-second jade verse of the Great Cavern’s *Wenchang*, ‘Earth’s Second Generates Fire,’ pertains to the second mystery’s practice. Ding-si, Wu-wu, Dui, Huan. The Heavenly Sovereign’s primordial qi.”

As previously stated: the qi of the Nine August Supreme Perfections; now it speaks of the Heavenly August One. For the Heavenly August Great Emperor resides in the Purple Tenuity Enclosure’s Hook-and-Cord Palace, the position revered by all stars—thus called the most exalted among the stars, governing all affairs of the celestial palaces and constellations. Moreover, one *cun* above the Flowing Pearl lies the Heavenly August Palace’s Supreme Perfection qi, all born of the Primordial Beginning. Wang Bi states: “It is the womb-ancestor of the Three Origins, stirring and shaping all things.” This aligns precisely with this discourse, for it arises from the Three Treasures’ true qi of the Primordial Beginning, born of the Primal Chaos Supreme Non-Being Origin, the Vermilion Chaos Supreme Non-Being Origin, and the Dark Serene Mysterious Penetration Origin.

The Three Origins ride the dawn’s return. *Chen* (dawn) is sometimes called *shen* (spirit), but this is incorrect. The Three Origins—Heaven, Earth, and Water—each govern one hundred twenty bureaus, overseeing the transgressions and blessings of mortals. Thrice yearly, they convene to examine the ledgers, as recorded in the *Scripture of the Life-Spirit Chapters*, the *Three Origins Scripture*, and the *Three Officials’ Repentance*. The Three Origins’ scrutiny is no trifling matter, for they ascend to report mortal sins before the Jade Emperor, riding the radiant dawn’s chariot. This illustrates how one nurtures form and spirit with the Three Origins’ qi—what is called the Three Origins’ nurturing, the two images’ life-preservation.

The *Doctrine of the Mean* states: “The virtue of ghosts and spirits—how abundant it is! Though invisible and inaudible, it pervades all things and cannot be escaped. *Yuan heng li zhen*: bending and stretching, advancing and retreating, fortune and misfortune arise from mutual resonance. The retribution of transgressions and blessings lies herein. Though it stems from mortal summoning, ghosts and spirits indeed oversee their allotment.”

The Dharma Enclosure ascends the Vermilion Empyrean. This was explained in Chapter Ten of the middle volume: the Vermilion Empyrean is the Crimson Empyrean, one of the Nine Empyreans. The Great Cinnabar’s luminous qi opens the Great Cinnabar’s heaven, congealing the Crimson Empyrean’s palace in the south. The Dharma Enclosure encompasses the Purple Tenuity, Supreme Tenuity, and Celestial Market heavens.

The Emperor prospers, opening the Jade Gate. The Nine Perfected of the Mud-Pill Palace, the August Emperor of Prosperity, bears the primordial name *Xianlingyuan*. At this time, the Jade Portal opens to receive them. Qi follows spirit’s journey, all returning to the Gate of Myriad Mysteries. As Chan Buddhism says: “Possess another eye to see”—this is precisely it.

Extract the corpse’s qi from within the Gate of Life. Draw forth the corpse’s foul qi, severing it from the Gate of Life. The right kidney is called the Gate of Life, the crux of the body’s vital pulse. Those who fail to honor their qi and secure their root, indulging in lust and desire to agitate the Gate of Life, court death.

Unbind the knots at the Peach Prosperity Stair. Dissolve the obstructions and root-tethers at the Peach Prosperity Stair. Peach Prosperity refers to the true qi’s correct spirit, the kidney spirit named *Heyan*, also called *Xuanming* or *Yuying*—a single spirit with two names, or two spirits with one name.

Gather the spirit to guard the Five Registers. Collect the myriad spirits of the body to safeguard the Five Viscera. Above, they correspond to the Five Stars; at the center, to the Five Qi; below, to the Five Marchmounts. All possess ledgers recording the immortal names of those who attain the Dao.

Ascend through turns into the Supreme Tenuity. The Supreme Tenuity is the Southern Dipper’s enclosure. Only by passing through the Three Realms’ protection and recommendation may one enter the Supreme Tenuity. All proceed from lower to higher, advancing step by step. From the Supreme Tenuity, one ascends to the Three Bounds, becoming a minister in attendance upon the Three Clarities.

Single entry, dual cultivation. Entering the Dao with one body, cultivate both merit and wisdom, benefiting the hidden and the manifest. This illustrates how one preserves the clarity of sincere mindfulness, investigating the subtleties of a single aperture. Thus, the precelestial and postcelestial qi merge into one family, forged into a single whole.

A bend of water and sky heard. Initially, Heaven One generates Water, whence Earth Two generates Fire. Below, it speaks of the Sea Sun. Water’s nature flows downward through the earth, yet its resonance answers to the celestial realm. The unheard hearing—let the noble person fear what they do not hear. Whispers in the human world are heard in heaven like thunder. How much more in the dark chamber’s seclusion, where ten eyes watch and ten hands point—dare one not fear!

The solitary crane cries in the Nine Marshes, its voice heard in heaven. When the cultivator attains utmost stillness, not a single sound in heaven or earth escapes their awareness. All is known, all is heard. Some interpret *heard* as *opened*.

The Sea Sun rises from the east. Earth Two generates Fire, hence the Sea Sun. The sun emerges from the Eastern Sea’s Fusang Mountain. This illustrates how, when one seeks to form the embryo, yin and yang qi coalesce within the self. Only when the six yang are complete—forming the *Qian* hexagram—does the body’s form take shape.

The primordial life ascends to the Great Beginning. *Yuanming* (primordial life) is primordial qi. Heaven’s root lies in Heaven One, extending to Earth Two—the inception of form and qi’s portents. Mortal life’s root lies in the intercourse of essence and qi. Only when true yang congeals does the embryo form, transforming into the Great Beginning’s pre-formative state.

To discourse on nature without qi is incomplete; to discourse on qi without nature is unclear. Nature is spirit, belonging to yin; life is qi, belonging to yang. Cultivating nature without life leaves one’s dwelling prone to decay. Cultivating life without nature, though one may live for millennia, ultimately fails to grasp the wondrous principle. Thus, dual cultivation of nature and life is the supreme immortal fruit.

The above jade verse comprises sixty celestial seal-characters, governing above the Thought-Free River’s Heavenly Flow and commanding below the Sixth Rampart’s Earth Virtue Lord.

The *Mysterious Contract* states: “The Great Beginning’s second origin’s wondrous practice of the Breath-Resting Gate. Contemplate the arising of the nature-mind’s movement to grasp nature’s mechanism. Thoughts of faith must not be forgotten; faith must not be lost in guarding. Act for the sake of faith. When the Five Faiths reside within, the heart harmonizes and sight harmonizes—thus called the second degree, the second spark of Earth’s Fire. Perform five hundred deeds, progressing from seeing to observing. When observation stabilizes, the spirit clarifies; when the spirit clarifies, the qi purifies. Only then is it named correct observation. The two harmonies contain and gather the spirit’s eyes and square pupils. Thereby, the Numinous Treasure opens the long night’s darkness, and the Red Emperor nurtures the qi of thorough harmony.”

The Southern Dipper’s upper register inscribes the cinnabar script.

The Primordial Heavenly King states: “The twenty-third jade verse of the Great Cavern’s *Wenchang*, ‘Heaven Three Generates Wood,’ pertains to the third origin’s wondrous practice.”

On the days *jiwei*, *gengshen*, at the seasonal nodes and during *Zhongfu*. The Supreme Unity’s Upper Primordial Qi—this chapter is absent from the Mao Shan *Jade Canon*. The Supreme Unity was noted earlier; previously, the Upper Perfected Qi appeared twice, and today it is the Upper Primordial Qi. The Mud-Pill Palace is also called the Upper Primordial Palace, governing the affairs of the Celestial Treasury. Some say it is forbidden, though this holds no meaning.

Within the Sun’s center dwells the Youth of the Controller of Destiny. In the Palace of Grand Yang resides the Lord of Destiny Who Receives Life, styled *Daoling*, also called the Numinous Youth of the Controller of Destiny. This metaphor refers to the human heart, which belongs to yang. The Controller of Destiny is the spirit of the heart, also named *Danyuan*, styled *Shouling*. This chapter speaks of the heart as fire, born of wood. The mother conceals the child in the womb—a technique of the Five Phases’ inversion. The dragon emerges from within fire. As the *Yin Fu Jing* states: “Fire is born of wood, and calamity arises to restrain it.” Fire is generated within wood, yet it turns to burn the fuel. In worldly affairs, this brings harm through reversal; in the Dao of the Elixir, wood as three and fire as two make five, containing the mechanism of transformation.

Radiant, the spirit’s light shines bright. The heart is the image of *li* brightness, the mansion of numinous clarity—its divine light blazes resplendent. Cultivating this *Wenchang Great Cavern* is like polishing a pearl from mud, wiping a mirror free of dust, or blowing embers in a cold furnace—only to restore its original luminosity.

Clad in rosy clouds, one ascends the Emperor’s ramparts. The clouds appear in five hues: crimson, cinnabar, deep red, vermilion, and purple—all yang qi. This speaks of the heart-spirit donning these rosy clouds to ascend the ramparts of the Jade Emperor’s palace in the Mud-Pill. As noted earlier, the characters often reveal overlapping meanings.

Arrayed in seats upon the *Zhen* numinous mat. The myriad spirits are seated in ranks upon the mat of *Zhen*, the east’s Wood virtue, the place of burgeoning life qi. “The Emperor emerges from *Zhen*”—this is the Lesser Yang’s position.

Below, the two *Zhen* numina are seen. Here, the trigrams *Kan*, *Li*, and *Zhen* are observed.

Harmonizing within the Five-Day Chamber. Five days make one *hou*. The spirit and essence merge within the Purple Chamber; only after five days do they return to their respective palaces. In the Great Elixir’s Dao, a moment’s effort can ascend one to sagehood. This refers to the firing times, which must be guarded with days and hours—advancing and withdrawing, adding and reducing.

The *Analects* states: “Choosing the Mean, yet unable to hold it for even a month.” Yan Hui, as a person, chose the Mean and, having attained one good, grasped it firmly and never lost it. It also says: “Yan Hui’s heart did not stray from benevolence for three months.” Once one obtains this wondrous aperture, one must guard it with effort—even for a lifetime. Why be bound by a single *hou*? The five days also correspond to the Five Emperors dispersing the essence of the sun, and the sun’s center opening its five radiant beams—these are of the same meaning.

The *Scripture of Numinous Treasure* says: “For seven days and nights, the sun, moon, and stars of all heavens halt their wheels.” All these describe the coagulation of spirit and qi, the blending of yin and yang within the Hollow Cavern. The eyes do not blink, the heart is still and settled—this is the way.

White qi nurtures *Shangsheng*. The One Primordial White Qi Lord within the womb is named *Yushangsheng*, styled *Shengchang*, also called *Xuanguizi*. A later chapter states: “The Right Assistant returns to *Shengchang*.” The *Chapter on Generating the Spirit* says: “Devote yourself to *Xuanyu Shangsheng*,” and also refers to the names of the Jade Emperor of the Brain Palace.

The Azure Lord presses *Yanchang*. The Azure Qi Lord of the Center, *Anyanchang*, styled *Heheying*, rides the qi of Jupiter, the Wood virtue of the east, flowing forth the true qi of life to descend and infuse the human body and the liver regions of all beings, generating the essence of the Three Hun.

On the left, he carries *Jingshangmen*. The Black Qi Lord of the Nodes, *Fulaisheng*, styled *Jingshangmen*, is carried by the Azure Lord to generate the left-eye youth named *Feiling*, which in the head is the sun. The sun has nine-colored rays, brilliant and dazzling, forming the Nine Hun Perfected.

On the right, he embraces *Heheying*. The White Qi Lord embraces the Azure Qi *Heheying*, uniting with the qi of Grand Harmony to generate the right-eye youth *Chenying*, which in the head is the moon. The moon has fourteen luminous essences, clear and lustrous, forming the Seven Po Perfected.

I give birth to the sun and moon’s splendor. The human eyes alternate like the sun and moon, and the heart of heaven and earth is never obscured—how could the world lie beyond me? The Dao of heaven flows and transforms, giving life to the myriad things. All that fills heaven and earth with sound, color, form, and appearance are things. Since things exist, there must be their inherent principles, which cannot be otherwise. This is what heaven bestows, not what humans can fabricate.

The *Book of Songs* says: “Heaven gives birth to the teeming people; there are things, there are principles. The people hold fast to the constant; they love this excellent virtue.” All things under heaven are complete within me. When the two qi are complete in the body, the eyes shine like the sun and moon’s radiance. In the Golden Elixir, this is called the union of sun and moon.

The *Cantong Qi* states: “The two crescents unite their essence; the body of Qian and Kun is thus formed.” It also says: “Between the dark and new moons, chaos and vast obscurity—yin and yang qi are complete. This is the time of the sun and moon’s union.” Lü Dongbin said: “Upon the winding river, the moon’s radiance is pure and bright; a crow flies there.”

The Crimson Qi King, *Youbao*. “Friend” (*you*) takes harmony, “treasure” (*bao*) takes preciousness. The Crimson Qi King is the spirit of the heart, which one must cherish, keeping it tranquil and harmonious. Some say *Youbao* is the style of the Crimson Qi King, signifying the principle of the numinous terrace’s emptiness and clarity.

The Eight Sceneries illuminate the Mud-Pill. The Three Divisions and Eight Sceneries refer to the twenty-four vertebrae of the spine, passing through their joints to shine upon the Mud-Pill. The inner names of the Three Divisions and Eight Sceneries’ spirits are hidden and tabooed—recorded in the middle scroll. Through human concentration, the numinous clarity comes of itself.

Brilliant within the Cavern Chamber. The Cavern Chamber lies within the Brain Palace. The true qi of Primordial Yang ascends from the twenty-four nodes to the Cavern Chamber, brightly illuminating the Eight Chambers. From here, one gazes down upon the Six Poles’ realm as if in the palm of the hand—so-called “the Three Realms are not distant.”

The Infant is the Red Child—the spirit of the Lower Elixir Field is named the Infant, like a newborn babe. Through cultivating this Dao, I return to the state of infancy, and the infant further transforms into Mysterious Qi. As the *Tradition* states: "Cherish the heart of the Red Child; earnestly seek it, and though you may not hit the mark, you shall not be far off."

Commingling gives birth to the Jade Countenance. When Kan and Li unite in intercourse, Water and Fire achieve harmony, Yin and Yang merge, and the Elixir congeals. Nurtured in the Primordial Palace with proper warmth, refined through timely withdrawal and addition, it accumulates within and manifests without—seen upon the face, flourishing upon the back.

The Five Paths bring forth Golden Splendor. The Five Paths are the Five Phases, embodied in Earth yet with qi coursing through Heaven. As the Five Viscera reside within, the Five Qi surge outward—thus do all Five Viscera radiate brilliance. Golden Splendor is the name of a mountain in Heaven.

Ranked as a Lord of Supreme Clarity. One is enfeoffed in the realm of the Upper Clarity, attaining the noble rank of Immortal Lord. The titles Duke, Marquis, Earl, Viscount, and Baron correspond to the five human ranks, just as the Upper Clarity’s Central Cavity is where the myriad qi settle into a single locus to form the Elixir.

The Seven Ancestors sever Mysterious Obstructions. For the Seven Ancestors and Nine Mysteries whose bonds remain unbroken, this practice severs them like a blade, liberating all at once. The gates of darkest night dissolve without hindrance, allowing ascent to the celestial realms in shared flight, where one attains sagehood and becomes a Perfected—joyous and free.

The Body-Spirit rides the Immortal Wind. The spirit of the body soars lightly, like Liezi riding the wind. In the era of the Three Sovereigns, people were often weightless, traversing the void. Later generations, consuming the five grains and rich flavors, grew heavy and lost the power of flight.

Roaming above the Three Clarities. One wanders leisurely above the Three Clarities, dwelling in their realm yet journeying to their heavens. In life, one may roam the spirit through the Three Fields; in death, one may ascend to the Three Clarities’ domain, above the Thirty-Two Heavens in the Great Canopy.

Harmonious joy returns to the Embryonic Infant. The *Book of Changes* states: "The Dao of Qian transforms and changes, each rectifying its nature and destiny, preserving the Great Harmony." Here, in the Great Cavern, one reverts from old age to infancy, harmonious and blissful. Nurturing the harmonious qi, the Infant spontaneously arises within the navel and abdomen, as if in gestation.

The Great Beginning’s Three Qi cycle. The Supreme Simplicity, Supreme Origin, and Supreme Beginning—these are the Great Mystery, Great Origin, and Great Beginning. When the Three Qi of Mystery, Origin, and Beginning are complete, they become the root of Heaven and Earth. At this stage of human life, all boundaries are established; the Elixir, too, reaches this state when the Fire Times are fulfilled.

The True Scriptures inaugurate luminous clarity. The True Scriptures resemble the cloud-seals of the Five Directions. Refined in the Yang Cavern’s hall and smelted in the Flowing Fire’s court, they first take form. The Heavenly Perfected inscribed them to stabilize Heaven and Earth. This *Great Cavern Immortal Scripture* was formed when the Primordial Heavenly King condensed the qi of the Primal Chaos and Supreme Non-Being into a pearl. The pearl’s radiance dispersed into billions, congealing into clouds and unfolding into patterns, evolving into the *Great Cavern Immortal Scripture*. Its True Scripts and precious talismans originate here. When the Five Viscera are fully formed in a person, it is called the "Opening of the Five Scripts," for the Five Spirits each guard the essence of the Five Viscera—hence the term "Script."

The above Jade Stanzas of Heavenly Seal comprise one hundred twenty characters. Above, they govern the Supreme Purity of Ruanle Heaven; below, they command the Lord of Earthly Virtue of the Sixth Stratum.

The *Mysterious Contract* states: "The Three Qi of the Great Beginning wondrously traverse the Gate of Contemplation. Fixed records are inscribed on metal and stone; perfect faith achieves great completion. Those of virtuous faith can cultivate; steadfast faith advances progress—only then is it called true faith. When the Ten Faiths are complete, harmony of intent generates extended qi; harmony of will brings great benefit; harmony of qi perfects the Three Qi. This is called the Three Degrees within the Three Perfected, the celestial reckoning of a thousand great merits. From hearing one enters vision; from vision one enters penetration. Thus is the Spirit Treasure governed, the myriad spirits restrained, the Azure Emperor safeguarding the soul’s clarity. The Eastern Dipper inscribes the tally of longevity; the Lord of Wood records names on the Azure Tablets."

The Primordial Heavenly King said: "This is the twenty-fourth Jade Stanza of the Great Cavern’s Literary Splendor. Earth gives birth to Metal in the Fourfold; the Four Brahmā wondrously traverse. Xin-You, Ren-Xu, Minor Excess, and After Completion."

Within the Yellow Chamber of the Primordial Spirit...

This stanza takes Metal as its governing element, its color yellow, corresponding to the central spleen-viscera. The Yellow Chamber is the Yellow Court, as the *Book of Changes* states: "The noble one, centered in yellow, penetrates the principles and occupies the proper position within the body." This is precisely what is meant here—Primordial Spirit signifies emptiness and luminous clarity. Within it resides the Yellow Serenity Youth.

The Three Perfected Sovereigns of Essence and Blood, the Primordial King of the Yuan, styled Yellow Serenity Master of the Mysterious, dwells in the Yellow Chamber, presiding over the transformation of the water-and-grain repository. Clad in brocade robes and yellow skirts, he sits upon a golden terrace, encircled by walls and ramparts—this is also called the Great Granary.

To his left is the Firm Jade Lord: the Two Perfected of the Stomach Cavity, Firm Jade Lord, styled Congealed Feather Pearl, guarding the left of the stomach cavity. He governs the stomach’s qi and water-grain, nourishing the four limbs, rendering them firm as gold and jade, while his true qi spreads like azure clouds, descending to suffuse the Great Granary.

To his right is the Imperial Prosperity August One: the Nine Perfected of the Mud-Pellet Palace, Imperial Prosperity Supreme August, styled Primordial Spirit of the First, guarding the right of the spleen and stomach. He distributes water-grain, irrigating the five viscera and the flesh, causing them to flourish. Some texts call him the Imperial Prosperity Youth, which is surely an error, for he should not be redundantly termed a "youth."

The floating yellow haze of spirit-qi—spleen qi pertains to Earth, Earth’s color is yellow, and true qi steams and veils, shading the spirit-brilliance of the lower fields. Alchemical classics state: "This is called the Spirit-Qi Cavern, within which lies the essence of Kan and Li." Thus, essence, qi, and spirit all converge here.

Lush and verdant, the Valley of Empty Spirit—thickly luxuriant, it blankets the empty spirit, preserving the complexion. This is the true qi of the Firm Jade Lord and the Imperial Prosperity August One, descending to infuse the spleen and stomach, flourishing like a clump of verdant growth, thereby moistening and enhancing the countenance.

The Bright Wheel Child of the Azure Liver—the Four Perfected of the Liver, Azure Bright Lord, styled Bright Wheel Child, receives stomach qi to render the eyes luminous. The liver pertains to Wood, Wood’s color is azure, hence "azure liver." The Bright Wheel refers to the sun and moon: in the heavens, sun and moon are flying essences; in the grottoes, they are hidden roots; among humans, they are bright wheels. Those who ingest the bright wheel become immortals. Methods exist for absorbing the radiance of sun and moon, which can moisten the five viscera and enhance the complexion. Wood governs the eastern region of Jia and Yi, the gate through which sun and moon emerge. The earthly realm, at dawn and dusk, greets and sends off the spirits of Yu-Yi and Jie-Lin.

Luminous and clear, penetrating the eight windows—the sun and moon emerge, and their brilliance must illuminate. How much more so the eight windows, exquisitely wrought—how could they not be radiant? One version reads "eight faculties," which is surely an error. This refers to the Eight Scenic Illuminations of the Mud-Pellet Nine, their resplendent splendor suffusing the threefold Yellow Path.

The Taiyi’s companion, Qiu Lan—Qiu Lan is the name of the Great Woman in the Dipper, and also the name of the spirit of the lower stomach duct. These are metaphors, like a monk asked about the meaning of the Western advent, who replied, "The cypress tree before the courtyard," or "The grass before Master Lianxi’s window," which are no different from one’s own intent.

Bearing talismans, entering the Jade Palace—obeying the command of Taiyi, they hold talismans and staffs, ascending into the Jade Emperor’s Palace behind the brain. There, they present the merits and transgressions of mortals. On the first and fifteenth days of the lunar month, the days of Geng-Shen and Jia-Zi, and one’s own life-destiny day, they report on the deeds of human souls.

The absolution of seven generations’ sins—delivering the souls of seven ancestral lines, pardoning transgressions and faults. For the hun-souls gather in the Mud-Pill Palace, presenting the good and evil deeds of mortals. First, the seven generations of forebears are liberated; if one lacks good causes, the burden extends to ancestors and fathers, who must bear the punishment.

The Return-to-Origin awaits the Tenfold Permeation. As the *Scripture of Salvation* states: "Ten returns deliver humanity." Ten is also the completion number of earth. "Return-to-Origin" means reverting to the root and restoring the primordial. After ten full cycles, the lingering souls and stagnant po of seven ancestors and ninefold kin may be delivered.

Merging into the Chamber of the Imperial Unity—the revolving wind merges into the chamber of the Imperial Unity. The Chamber of the Imperial Unity lies within the Mysterious Pass. Some say the *Scripture of the Great Cavern* has no fixed sequence, with interwoven references that defy easy tracing. This scripture takes "revolving wind merging" as its theme, hence its shifting structure—front and back, above and below, left and right—interchanging. In truth, this arises from the dazzling interplay of pearl-like radiance, forming its text, which cannot be judged by a single standard.

In former times, Deng Yuzhi, styled Yanda, secluded himself in the Grotto-Spirit Terrace to cultivate the Way of Merging with the Imperial Unity. Each night, he recited the *Scripture of the Great Cavern*. Once, he was visited by the descent of Lady Wei, who told him: "You possess a destiny for immortality, and your tireless recitation has brought me here." One day, three azure birds suddenly arrived, dancing and singing like cranes, lingering for a time before departing. Yuzhi said to his disciples: "The azure birds have come—court assembly is near." He then transcended in a wondrous transformation, becoming an immortal. Was this not a sign of the Imperial Unity?

The Five Elders transform into childlike innocence. The Five Elders, as previously noted, now through the cultivation of the *Great Cavern*’s revolving wind merging Way, all revert to ignorance, becoming unknowing, infantile youths. The Five Elders are the Five Phases; hence, they are called "elders." They are the spirits of the five viscera.

The inception of the Grand Simplicity’s Brahman conduct—when qi, form, and substance are complete yet never separate, it is called the Grand Simplicity. At the initial stage of advancing Brahman conduct, when the fire-timing is insufficient and the golden elixir unformed, the wondrous fruit of Brahman conduct has only reached the fourth level. One must remain reverent and diligent, advancing without slack.

One goodness permeates the Fourfold Gold. "One" is water, which beneficially nurtures all things. As the saying goes: "When the Five Phases do not follow their sequence, the tiger is born in water." The Way of the elixir follows the generative numbers of heaven and earth. Earth’s four generates metal, called the Grand Simplicity. Water generates metal; the child hides in the mother’s womb. Metal is the nature of spirit, residing in the upper cinnabar field, known as the crown gate. People call it the "gate of nature." Nature is most numinous; thus, before the gate of nature closes, one still knows past lives. Once it closes, such knowledge is lost. It lodges in the heart, responding to all affairs. If one can comprehend the gate of nature, one may cultivate the wondrous conduct of the Grand Simplicity’s contemplative gate, transforming into a golden immortal.

---

The above jade verse in celestial script, eighty characters in all, governs above the Boundless Vow-Heaven of Unfathomable Oaths and commands below the Sixth-Tiered Earth Virtue Lord.

The *Mysterious Contract* states: "The contemplative gate of the Grand Simplicity’s Fourfold Brahman conduct first permeates the singular goodness. Essence-water moistens and revives; withered and decayed, it sprouts anew. This is called 'essence-harmony.' When essence harmonizes, spirit harmonizes; when spirit harmonizes, qi clarifies. Clarified qi then harmonizes—hence, 'clarity and harmony.'"

Fourfold completion perfects the Fourfold Gold. The earth number’s five hundred merit-points thus enable the Grand Unity to manifest a divine body before the White Emperor, attending the primordial po. The Western Dipper records names in the *Jade Numinous Jade Chapters*.

The Primordial Heavenly King said: "The twenty-fifth jade verse of the *Great Cavern*’s Wenchang: Heaven’s five generates earth; the Five Spirits’ wondrous conduct."

*Guihai*, *Weiji*, *Qian*.

The Supreme Ultimate presides over the Fourfold True—
The Fourfold True are the Grand Simplicity, Grand Origin, Grand Beginning, and Grand Substance. The Supreme Ultimate presides because only here do the Five Ultimates finally separate, each possessing its own body. As the saying goes: "Each thing has its own Supreme Ultimate, which generates the Two Modes. The Two Modes generate the Four Images"—the Four Images are the Fourfold True. There is also the August Ultimate, governing ruler, minister, people, and things; the qi-movement governing years, months, days, and hours; the numbers governing kalpas, epochs, and generations. Heaven, earth, and humanity all arise therefrom. In heaven, there are the Supreme Ultimate True Person, Supreme Ultimate Immortal Elder, and Supreme Ultimate Immortal Official, who oversee the immortal registers. Xu Laile, Huo Shanyuan Fu, Xiliangzi Wang Zongzhen, An Duming, and Haojing Shechong are all titled Supreme Ultimate True Persons. The Four True Persons in the *Jade Emperor Scripture* and the Fourfold True in the Buddhist *Śūraṅgama Sūtra* are essentially the same. In humanity, they are the heart, liver, lungs, and kidneys—the Fourfold True.

Soaring on feathers, roaming the Upper Clarity—
"Feathers soaring" means swiftly donning feathered robes to roam the heavens of Upper Clarity. An ancient poem says: "The knife’s measure enters the belly, sprouting feathered wings." One who consumes yellow essence and abstains from the five grains will grow fur and feathers, able to fly through empty space and walk the void.

Seven revolutions summon the Director of Destinies—
"Seven revolutions" are the seven returns and nine reversions. At this stage in the elixir Way, the fire-timing is complete, and one may summon the Director of Destinies within the heart, journeying together to Upper Clarity. Upper Clarity is the Crimson Palace of the heart, where all spirits pay court.

The Grand Unity displays its radiant might—
The Grand Unity resides in the head, manifesting its majestic power. In humanity, it fiercely combats worldly toils, preventing sleep-demons and yin-evil from encroaching. Drowsiness scatters spirit and vitality, allowing demons to bully. Thus, martial readiness is employed to restrain and adorn it.

The Recorder safeguards the stored destiny—
The *Scripture of Salvation* speaks of the Director of Destinies, Director of Officials, Extender of Lifespan, Increaser of Years, and Deliverer from Misfortune as honored spirits, all sharing this meaning. The Director of Officials governs the principle of endless generation, thus safeguarding the stored destiny as the great root and foundation.

Threefold elevation ascends the numinous thunder—
Once the Supreme Ultimate divides, heaven and earth are established. The Eastern King and Western Mother are set as the parents of all things. Now, the Recorder Spirit thrice elevates the eldest son to preside over the thunder vessel, ensuring the lineage does not falter. Thus, the Way of establishing heaven and earth is no different from the Way of the August Ultimate. Those who recite this invoke it to celebrate the Eastern August One’s millennial reign.

The Demon Kings come to receive their duties—
Those who attain the Dao cannot transcend the Three Realms without the Demon Kings’ sponsorship. Once they have crossed beyond the Three Realms, they receive the Jade Emperor’s decree to oversee the mechanisms of governance. Thus, the great demons who once obstructed them must now come forward to bow and receive their commissions.

The Immortal Officials restrain the ghostly essences—
As the *Book of Changes* states: “Essence and qi become things.” When essence and qi gather, life is born; when the wandering soul transforms, the hun ascends and the po descends, and death ensues. Once dead, they become ghosts. Confucius said: “Radiant brightness, mournful vapors—these are the essences of the hundred things.” In Fengdu, the Six Cavern Palaces’ Immortal Officials, though they govern demons and ghosts, also hold immortal offices, subordinate to the celestial bureaus. Thus, the Immortal Officials bind the ghostly essences for the practitioner, preventing them from returning to the Way and corrupting virtue. This act of yang restraining yin dissolves the passions and perfects the nature, allowing ascent through the Three Realms to realize true immortality.

The Azure Emperor’s Mother resides in the moon—
Some say “in the sun,” but this is incorrect. The Azure Emperor is yang; the Mother is yin within yang, the hidden yin within the Li Palace’s womb. Later, it speaks of the Moon Mother Ning Sulan, sharing the same meaning: sun as yang, moon as yin, their union generating the myriad things. She is called the Fragrant and Resplendent Infant, the name of the moon’s hun-soul, the goddess of the Feminine One. The Daoist scriptures say: “Within the moon dwells Lord Taokang, resplendent in the Yellow Chamber,” and “The moon’s palace brims with immortal recipes”—all referring to the same principle. Heaven and earth, through the union of yin and yang, fulfill the principle of generation and transformation.

The Supreme Unfolds the Five Talismans—
The Central Primordial Lord of the Yellow Plain, Yuan Hua Huang Ren, bears the style “Supreme Unfolds Above.” He presents the Five Numinous Talismans to pacify and stabilize heaven and earth, just as humans use the five qi to stabilize the five viscera. This chapter corresponds to earth, governing the Four Symbols, hence the term “Five Talismans.”

Peace Comes to Bear the Jade Name—
The Left Primordial Lord of the Purple Plain, Yi Yu Ren, bears the style “Peace Comes Above.” His is the Jade Name—indeed, a name of jade. One version reads “Peace Comes to Life,” a grave error. The Three Primordial Lords’ jade taboos are: White Plain for the Right Primordial Lord, and for the Left Primordial Lord, Qiming Xiao Ren, styled “Golden Gate Above.”

The Chamber of Harmonious Transformation pervades the Six Directions—
“Harmonious Transformation” is one of the Nine Hun-souls’ names. Only by blending and transforming within the Six Directions—what the *Universal Geography* calls the Six Directions and Eight Extremities—can this be achieved. In humans, it is the brain palace, the Mud Pill, where the myriad spirits gather.

The Cavern Palace arrays the Fire Soldiers—
The Cavern Palace is the Crimson Palace. The *Jade Scripture* states: “The Vermilion Emperor of the Red Mound, the Red Rider of the Divine Immortals, the Red Lads of the Demon-Slaying Register, command the Fire Soldiers.” The incantation says: “The Luminous Divine Youth commands the Fire Soldiers. The Jade Controller of the Southern Thearch governs the Terrace of Vermilion Yang, dispatching the fire essence and the Red Soldiers of Bing, wielding the authority of the Supreme Perfected. They employ the spirits of Bing and Ding to enact celestial virtue, and the spirits of Si and Wu to rectify earthly qi.” In truth, this is the fire of the heart. Used rightly, it refines the Golden Crucible’s great elixir; used wrongly, it ignites the fires of ignorance, plunging one into the dark hells.

The Five Numinous Forces surge through the Supreme Ultimate—
When the Five Phases are complete, they harmonize; when incomplete, they clash. Before the Supreme Ultimate divided, the Five Phases were undifferentiated within it. After its division, the Four Symbols each assumed their positions, while the Supreme Ultimate, belonging to earth, resided at the center. Thus, it lends form to the Four Symbols and entrusts its vigor to the four seasons. Now, with the Five Numinous Forces of the Supreme Ultimate in harmonious union, no conflict arises. The Five Numinous Forces are the Five Phases—water, fire, wood, metal, and earth—the Five Elders, the Five Thearchs, the Five Marchmounts. In humans, they are the five viscera. When harmonized, the five qi surge purely, the five flowers naturally bloom, the five bodies thrive in health, and one becomes a true immortal.

The Imperial Son Bin receives the Horizontal Script—
The Imperial Son Bin appears in the previous scroll, where it says: “The Imperial Son Bin presents the Five Talismans,” and “The True Yang Elder, the Imperial Son Bin.” This spirit, residing above the five viscera in humans, can enter the Jade Emperor’s Palace behind the brain to report one’s sins and blessings. The “Horizontal Script” refers to the Five Scripts, which are the Five Phases of the Supreme Ultimate—the fifteen numbers of the Luo and Yellow River diagrams, arranged horizontally and vertically. This is the Hun-soul of the August One, ascending to become the “Imperial Son,” one of the myriad spirits. In heaven, he is the Imperial Son and Guest; in humans, the guest of the heart. He rectifies deviant qi, descends the flow of true qi, and nourishes the myriad spirits, his patterns both horizontal and vertical following principle.

The above is the Jade Stanza of Heavenly Seal Script, eighty characters in all, which above stabilizes the Vast Court of the Azure Empyrean and the Heaven of Rosy Clouds, and below governs the Seventh Tier’s Water-Restraining Marshland and the Earthly Sovereign of the Yellow Soil.

The *Mysterious Contract* states: “In the wondrous practice of contemplating the spirits through the Five Numinous Forces of the Supreme Ultimate, first cultivate the Four Virtues. The Five Numbers reside at the center, corresponding to the spleen-earth and the root of intention. Thus, it is called ‘contemplating the spirits.’ The heart’s palace is the seat of thought; reflection arises from the root of intention—this is the wondrous practice of Dark Purity and Profound Wisdom. Therefore, the Five Degrees of Heaven and the Five Horizontal Scripts are indeed the ‘Script’ that unites the Five Directions, totaling ten. When one hears goodness, the Mysterious Above pierces the glabella, and the Six Dings illuminate with cavernous light—this corresponds to the previous scroll’s ‘piercing the glabella with the ten directions,’ the wondrous practice of the ear root’s cavernous subtlety. When one sees goodness, the Cinnabar Origin’s square pupils and the Eight Scribes radiate cavernous clarity—this corresponds to the previous scroll’s ‘Luminous Pearl,’ the square pupils being the wondrous practice of the eye root’s cavernous vision. When one speaks goodness, the Tongming swallows and rinses, the Five Scripts and Jade Flowers—this corresponds to the previous scroll’s ‘tasting and refining the Five Sprouts Pearl,’ the wondrous practice of the tongue root’s cavernous subtlety. When one walks goodness, strength aids and connects, the Earthly Pass and Life Gate—wielding the spirit and life root of the Heavenly and Earthly Passes, the hands and feet’s strength connects through the wondrous practice of cavernous numinosity. When the original nature first unites with the Five Degrees, it perfects the Five Horizontal Scripts. From the Five Greatnesses of Heaven and the Five Hundred Merits, it completes the Central Qi’s Numinous Imperial Lord. Thereby, the Primordial Life-Form coalesces, the Yellow Emperor of the Center presides, the myriad spirits guard and encamp, and the Great Dipper’s Chief Star oversees the host of spirits.”

Here ends Scroll Eight of the *Jade Purity’s Boundless Supreme Perfected Writ of the Great Cavern and the Numinous Star of Literature*.

(Note: “Wang Wen” should likely read “Yu Wen.”)

● "Wang" should likely read "Yu."
● "Thus it is called Lao" should likely read "Some call it the Five Elders."

**Scroll Nine of the *Jade Purity’s Boundless Supreme Perfected Writ of the Great Cavern and the Numinous Star of Literature***

The Primordial Heavenly King states: The twenty-sixth jade chapter of the *Great Cavern of Wenchang* speaks of Earth’s sixfold completion into water, and the wondrous practice of the six harmonies.

*Jiazi*, *Kun*, *Zhun*—
Heaven and Earth bear no branches or stems.

Within the Dipper dwell the Four Perfected,
scattering flowers upon the Jade Purity Terrace.
The Northern Dipper’s position lies in the Kan Palace,
and Kan is water. The Four Perfected are the Four Symbols previously mentioned.
Formerly called the Upper Purity, now the Jade Purity—
a yet higher tier, corresponding in man to the brain palace.
The Four Perfected govern the Four Perfected Inscriptions within the Great Ultimate.

Burning incense and scattering flowers,
circling in the pacing of emptiness—
such is the joy of the true immortals,
the fragrance and blossoms arising from the true qi within the body.
One must not cling to images or attachments as though they were substantial things.
The Jade Purity Terrace is none other than the upper cinnabar field of the Muddy Pellet Palace within man.

The Imperial Minister of the Central Mystery is born—
the Upper Primordial Imperial Minister of the Muddy Pellet Palace,
whose name is Zhong Xuansheng,
encompasses the host of immortals.
(One version reads "Imperial Homeland’s Zhong Xuanli," which is erroneous.
Another states: "The Three-One Imperial Minister, whose refined essence is named Zhong Xuansheng,
is also called the Second Unity of the One Spirit Perfected.")

At the first advent of Zhong Xuansheng,
the host of perfected beings gathers in full.
Where the mind directs, qi rushes to follow—
not out of reluctance, but because intent commands qi,
and qi obeys its bidding.
When one true being assembles, ten thousand true beings assemble.

Fragrant winds fan the Three Treasures—
gentle breezes waft and stir above the Three Treasures,
serving as offerings.
The Three Treasures are the three treasures within one’s body.
Through refined cultivation and inner alchemy,
the five qi steam forth,
and fragrant winds emanate externally.
This aligns with the *Mysterious Contract*, which states:
"Always offer celestial incense and celestial flowers to the Primordial Beginning."
The *Celestial Youth Sutra* says:
"Golden rice and jade nectar arise from seeking within—
all are found within one’s own body.
Do not seek outwardly."
The Three Treasures are the spirits of the three fields;
the fragrant winds are the steaming of true qi.
The fan symbolizes diligent stirring—
all follow the natural way.

The five viscera reflect the Clear and Level Palace.
The preceding passages speak of celestial matters,
while this line turns to the affairs within the body.
Thus, one draws near from the self and far from things.
This speaks of the Clear and Level Palace in heaven,
which man mirrors with the qi of the five viscera.
Buddhist texts say:
"Offer the fivefold fragrant incense as devotion,
and vow to uphold this resolve in repayment of the Buddha’s grace."
The *Book of Documents* states:
"Millet and sorghum are not truly fragrant—
only bright virtue is fragrant."
All share this principle.
People often burn incense, arrange flowers,
and prepare a hundred delicacies as offerings,
believing they accumulate merit.
Yet if sincerity is lacking,
heaven and earth do not accept it.
Instead, they incur the fault of wastefulness and the transgression of irreverence.
How much better to refine the fivefold true incense within oneself,
offering it to the Three Treasures within the body!
Then the five viscera will naturally radiate clarity,
peace, and harmony—
free from harm by ghosts and spirits,
and blessed with abundant fortune.
Why, then, do people toil in vain, seeking outwardly?

The azure barbarian’s radiant splendor—
only with qi does sound arise.
Sound harmonizes in high and low tones,
forming musical harmony.
When the numinous wind stirs and circulates,
it becomes music—
this single point of numinous light,
unobstructed and luminous,
shines throughout the eight directions.
In man, it is the golden elixir,
accumulated within,
while speech and sound manifest externally.
Thus, the six qi are distinct,
and the six yin demons are subdued.
The *Scripture of Salvation* speaks of the millet-grain pearl,
and the Buddha’s Śākyamuni jewel—
in truth, they are one.
The Great Elixir is called the Dragon-Tiger Great Medicine,
which must be conjoined with true lead and true mercury
to achieve resplendent radiance.

The sandalwood blazes with auspicious harmony—
harmonious qi brings forth blessings.
The sounds uttered by the Primordial Beginning
are called the "Sandalwood Blazing Harmony."
The *Scripture of the Jade Emperor* says:
"The wondrous music of the Celestial Harmony."
When Duke Mu of Qin reached the Heavenly Gate,
he heard the vast music of the Celestial Harmony.
When Emperor Ming of Tang arrived at the Moon Palace,
he heard the *Rainbow Skirt and Feathered Robe* melody—
both were celestial music.
In the mortal world, there are the Yellow Emperor’s *Xianchi*,
Yao’s *Great Elegance*,
Shun’s *Nine Shao*,
Yu’s *Great Xia*,
and Tang’s *Great Huo*—
all are the music of a well-governed age.
Where music reaches, auspiciousness gathers—
the height of harmony.
"Husband and wife live in harmony, like the zither and lute;
brothers unite in joy and delight."
How much more so with celestial music—
would it not bring forth auspicious signs?
Thus, when music harmonizes, spirits harmonize;
when spirits harmonize, heaven and earth harmonize;
when heaven and earth harmonize,
the five grains flourish,
and the people live in peace.
How could the vulgar music of Zheng and Wei ever achieve this?
When the five viscera within man are at peace,
speech becomes clear and resonant—
all who hear it perceive the pure Dharma-sound.

The Great Centrality’s six qi are pure—
beyond the Five Greatnesses lies another Five Greatnesses,
completing the number ten—
the number of the *River Chart*.
This is the one root from which the six qi divide.
In the Great Centrality, the five movements and six breaths are clear and undisturbed,
continuing the preceding theme of harmonious music.
The six qi correspond to Earth’s sixfold completion into water.
The six qi govern the generation and destruction of the myriad things in heaven and earth—
medical texts describe this in detail.
They also respond to human influence:
cold, heat, wind, rain, darkness, and obscurity are called the six atmospheric influences.
If one opposes their qi, illness and epidemics arise,
even leading to death.
Yet practicing the wondrous Way of the Great Cavern’s Great Centrality averts them.

The winding waters embrace the Celestial River—
as previously stated:
"One bend of the water hears the heavens."
The Celestial River flows into the Eastern Well,
circulating between heaven and earth.
The ancients said:
"The waters issue from Kunlun,
flow downward through the tail’s gate,
then rise again—
this is the Celestial River,
the river of heaven and earth."

The human river flows upward from the Tail Gate to Kunlun,
harmonizing with heaven and earth.
The Yellow River’s nine bends mirror the nine coils of the human intestines—
Master Lü said:
*"Above the winding river, the moon’s radiance gleams pure,
a bird takes flight."*
This aligns with *"One bend of the water hears the heavens,"*
both found beneath the preceding *Great Primordial* chapter,
their purport mutually illuminating.

The six perfections’ merit is complete—
the six perfections and ten thousand practices’ merit now perfected,
corresponding to the six waters.
Six perfections, six yin, six unions—
all are numerical completions.
When a person’s cultivation reaches fulfillment,
three thousand merits and eight hundred deeds
may also ascend as an Upper Immortal.

The five demons assail the six yin.
The five demons are:
Green Heaven’s Demon King, Bayuan Choubo;
Red Heaven’s Demon King, Futiandan Shi;
White Heaven’s Demon King, Fanshan Liumu;
Black Heaven’s Demon King, Jianchou Langyu;
Yellow Heaven’s Demon King, Hengtian Danli.
At the center coalesces the Primordial Beginning Lord—
the four cardinals and four corners all become the realm of the Great Yang Dao,
only then does the Primordial Beginning manifest.
As with one who refines away all yin qi,
forging pure yang,
only then does the Great Cavern’s Imperial Honored One appear—
the *Chapter of Spirit Generation* states:
*"Loftily coalesces the Primordial Beginning Lord,"*
of the same meaning.

Loftily behold the sixfold union’s court.
Having coalesced the Primordial Beginning within,
one may gaze upward to perceive all within the six unions—
just as the human spirit may inwardly inspect the viscera.
Master Zhang the Celestial Master cultivated for a thousand days,
able to inwardly inspect the five viscera
and outwardly gather the ten thousand spirits and their kind.

The wondrous practice of the Great Centrality takes qi as its master.
There is the qi of heaven and earth,
and the qi of father and mother,
which mingle to generate a person.
Within the womb, the umbilical cord connects to the mother—
when she exhales, so does the child;
when she inhales, so does the child.
At birth, the umbilical cord is severed,
and each breathes independently.
Qi is stored in the Sea of Qi,
called the life’s origin—
those who cultivate life cultivate this.

The above jade chapter of celestial seal-script comprises seventy characters,
above it governs the Abyssal-Pervading Primordial Cavern Heaven,
below it commands the Seventh Fortress’s Virtue Lord.

The *Mysterious Contract* states:
*"The wondrous observation gate of the Great Centrality’s six unions—
contemplate goodness, practice goodness,
unobstructed and unimpeded,
supreme goodness untransgressed,
abide in goodness, preserve peace,
establish goodness as the foundation,
perfect the ten virtues,
the ten flowers interpenetrate in glory.
Life unites with wisdom,
the winding waters embrace the flow,
the six perfections’ merit is complete.
A thousand merits accomplished,
from the first to the sixth,
three thousand six hundred,
fulfill the great merit,
thereby the Nine Heavens bear you as a Perfected Person,
the Five Emperors for you vanquish the six yin.
Revolving the Dipper, traversing the Winnowing Basket,
you cross the Celestial Pass—
the eight luminaries darkly merge,
and the Mysterious of the Mysterious begins."*

The Primordial Beginning Heavenly King said:
*"The twenty-seventh jade chapter of the Great Cavern’s Wenchang—
heaven’s seven completes fire,
the seven awakening wondrous practices.
Yichou, Bingyin, Meng, Xu.
Within Chen resides the Yellow Radiance qi."*

At *Chen*—the sun—within the sun’s heart dwells the qi of yellow radiance, speaking of the newly risen sun. It figures the hour of the Golden Elixir when the yang qi of the Yellow Court first stirs, and thus the moment of action: when lead meets *gui*, it must be swiftly gathered.

Three blossoms ascend the Empyrean Court.
Three leaps, and only then do they mount the Milky Way, rolling upward on the round axle to the layered heavens—how arduous! The Three Blossoms are a mountain in the midst of heaven; immortals call the magic mushroom the “three-blossom herb.” Riding the qi of yellow radiance, they wander the court of the Great Empyrean.

The Azure Terrace wheels its feathered chariot.
In the Eastern Sea’s Penglai stands a mountain named Canglang, and a terrace also called Canglang. Realized immortals, borne by the qi of yellow radiance, drive feathered chariots in flight to this terrace, enter the Three-Blossom Mountain, return to the Empyrean Court Palace, and there assume office and duty.

The Way of Welcoming and Prolonging is already accomplished.
Perfected immortals and Primordial *Chen* Perfected Ones, wearing the talismans of Welcoming and Prolonging, ride the whirlwind wheels and feathered chariots as carefree immortals—this is the achievement of cultivating the *Wenchang Great Cavern Scripture*, not the rank of lesser immortals.

The Director of Destinies bears the Emperor’s writ.
The spirit who governs the heart receives the imperial decree and proclaims it to the ten directions, ever mindful of preserving the root of life. The Director of Destinies, in golden script, determines the span of human life; all depends on whether the heart is stored and well used, for only then can one be called one who bears the marks of longevity.

He is titled Minister of the Mysterious Measure.
The Central Director of Destinies, the Venerable One who governs the dawn of clarity, is titled Minister of the Mysterious Measure. His sole duty is to guard the Crimson Palace of the heart. Human life is originally a hundred years, but because of the varying degrees of good and evil, the gods and spirits oversee its granting and taking, so that few reach eighty or ninety.

Preserve life in the Palace of Great Radiance.
Preserve life and protect destiny in the Palace of Great Radiance—that is, the Crimson Palace. This chapter corresponds entirely to the number of fire. Humans embody the image of *li* brightness, belonging to fire, their brilliance shining like radiance; thus it is called the Palace of Great Radiance, preserving the root of life.

Array the guest lodges in the Upper Clarity.
The lodges for guests are arrayed in the Palace of Upper Clarity—also the Crimson Palace—for it is the gathering place of the ten thousand qi and the ten thousand spirits. The ancients said: when one aperture opens, all apertures open; when one spirit gathers, all spirits gather.

The Gate of Life conjoins essence and prolongs.
The Gate of Life is the right kidney; its spirit, named Taokang, conjoins essence and prolongs. In sevenfold vision it appears. One tradition says: on the left is Father Ningzai, on the right is Mother Jingyan; it is also called the name of the Great Cavern’s Imperial Unity, Supreme Spirit Lord—both are preserved.

Guard my body’s Yellow Tranquility.
Taokang constantly gazes upward to Yellow Tranquility to receive qi. For the spleen and stomach, having received the water and grain, disperse them to the five viscera and six bowels. Earlier, Yellow Tranquility was noted as having a commentary; it is also the jade taboo of the Three Perfected of essence and blood—these may be cross-referenced.

On the left, escort the Lord of Primordial Simplicity.
“Primordial Simplicity” is another name for Wuying, as previously annotated. He is the master of the Fire Marsh, that is, the Left Primordial Lord of Purple Simplicity, Yiyuren, whose name is Anlaishang. He governs the protection of the liver and the guarding of the hun-soul, corresponding above to the virtue of wood and the Year Star, and below to Mount Tai of the Eastern Marchmount.

On the right, grasp the Vermilion Luxuriance.
The White Primordial Lord who Regulates Yang, named Zhu Jing, whose name is Yulingbiao—also called Xuan Yijuezhong—is the master of the Water Pool. As noted in the previous volume in the annotation on Master Zhu Jing Qiming, he communicates with the qi of the lungs and below presides over Mount Hua of the Western Marchmount.

Great Harmony conveys the Seven Awakenings.
Seven is the completion number of fire, hence the resonance in meaning. The Seven Awakenings are the Seven Primes of the Northern Dipper in heaven and the seven apertures of the heart in humans. When the qi of Great Harmony enters, awareness and perception arise, and the literary brilliance shines forth—hence the following phrase speaks of the true scripture proclaiming humanity. If one can bring centered harmony to the body, then “my body’s heaven and earth are positioned, and the ten thousand things nurtured”; thus, the heaven and earth outside the body are also positioned, and the ten thousand things nurtured. To be ever in perfect enlightenment yet never in perfect enlightenment is the way of the ordinary person. The immortals say: “Why not consume the qi of Great Harmony’s essence?” Mount Wudang calls it the Mountain of Great Harmony. In Buddhism, the Seven Awakenings are, in sequence: mindfulness, discernment of dharmas, diligence, joy, ease, concentration, and equanimity—these are also called the Seven Awakenings. In essence, they are nothing other than the spirit of pre-heaven and pre-earth, the numinous clarity that does not darken—it is simply the one empty, numinous awareness. Master Guifeng Pei’s exposition is most detailed.

Igniting the fire gives rise to the True Writs. Two dots form fire; earth’s two generates fire, heaven’s seven completes it, coalescing into the Vermilion Numinous Fire Mansion’s True Writs of the Southern Elixir—this is what was earlier called the Cloud Scripts of the Five Directions, the crucible’s flowing fire courtyard, where cavernous yang qi glows crimson, hence named the Crimson Writs. The Purple Radiance guides the Embryonic Immortals: only after the jade pupils refine the substance, the Yellow Radiance purges the form, and the Purple Radiance True Person leads the Embryonic Immortals to verify and ascend to immortal fruition—yet it is only through the refinement of Nanchang’s alchemical transformation that one may be reborn in heaven and regenerated in the world, exchanging mortal for immortal. This speaks of the Ten Radiant Immortals.

The Spirit within the Primal Mandate’s Truth: this is the Embryonic Immortal, also called the Primal Mandate True Person. The *Tradition* states: “At fifty, one knows Heaven’s mandate.” Yet if so, Heaven itself would never attain the Dao. The Primal Mandate is the primordial reception of Heaven’s luminous decree; within the truth resides the Spirit of Eternal Life, the Great Lord—this is the spirit enduring through vast kalpas, existing alone before heaven and earth, uncorrupted through eons, perfectly luminous and serenely void, wondrously existent yet truly empty. Such is its essence. Swift without haste, arriving without movement, transforming myriadfold, responding to affairs and engaging with beings—such is its function. Only by nurturing it with harmonious qi does one achieve the wondrous practice of the Seven Awakenings.

The above jade passage of celestial script comprises eighty characters, above governing the exalted literary grace of the wondrously perfected heavens, below presiding over the Virtuous Lords of the Seventh Stratum.

The *Mysterious Concordance* states: “The Tenfold Radiance’s Gate of Contemplation in the Purple Radiance Heaven of the Great Harmony’s Seven Awakenings wondrous practice—
First, the essence pervades the Cinnabar Radiance Earth of Supreme Nonbeing;
Second, the qi pervades the Azure Radiance Heaven of Congealed Mystery;
Third, the spirit pervades the Plain Radiance Earth of Myriad Beings;
Fourth, the purity pervades the Yellow Radiance Heaven of the Ten Directions;
Fifth, the origin pervades the Jade Radiance Earth of Supreme Clarity;
Sixth, the origin pervades the Golden Radiance Heaven of Dark Yin;
Seventh, the origin pervades the Verdant Radiance Earth of Supreme Mystery;
Eighth, the primordial pervades the Jasper Radiance Heaven of Highest Clarity;
Ninth, the primordial pervades the Jade Void’s Luminous Radiance Earth;
Tenth, the mysterious pervades the Jade Clarity’s Chaotic Abyss ●.”

The Tenfold Supreme Nonbeing’s Radiance connects the empty earth dwelling within heaven, a thousand practices commencing. At the first ignition, the Crimson Chaotic Wisdom coalesces with the Primordial Truth—hearing merges with union, seeing merges with union, union with virtue transforms the form—this is called the Supreme August within the Mysterious, the Spirit within the Truth.

The Primordial Heavenly King states: “The twenty-eighth jade passage of the Great Cavern’s Literary Florescence: earth’s eight completes wood, the wondrous practice of the Eight Sceneries.” Dingmao, Wuchen, litigation, and armies. The qi of the Golden Watchtower’s Upper Scenery...

The Golden Watchtower is the palace where the Three Pures preside—one text calls it the Golden Watchtower, which must be an error. The *fan*, *qing*, and *jing* Three Qi are the wondrous qi of the Qingwei Heaven. This scripture, when summoning the Primordial Spirit, the Mountain Perfected, and the Three Officials, first takes the *jing* qi as its foundation.

The Ten Directions glow with purple mist.
This speaks of the *jing* qi suffusing all, the Ten Directions radiant and coalescing into purple-hued clouds of mist. The *Huangting* states: “Purple mist above and below, the Three Pristine Clouds.”

The Three Conjoin the Supreme Unity.
The Supreme Unity, according to the *Records of the Grand Historian*, resides in the Purple Tenuity’s Imperial Throne—see the earlier volume’s annotation on the Supreme Unity as the root of destiny. The Three Conjoining refers to the *xuan*, *yuan*, and *shi* Three Qi uniting in virtue, synonymous with the aforementioned *fan*, *qing*, and *jing* Three Qi.

The Emperor summons the Supreme Primordial Spirit.
The Supreme Primordial Spirit is the name of the essence-soul of the Northern Direction. The Jade Emperor regularly summons it with the True Summoning Talisman to inquire into and examine the matters of merit and transgression under the jurisdiction of the Three Palaces and Five Peaks—this is the indestructible Primordial Spirit of a person through kalpas.

Seven revolutions summon the Mountain Perfected.
The Five Peaks have Five Perfected Persons, Five Perfected Lords, and Five Sage Emperors, with subordinate offices overseeing the registers of life and death. The Seven Revolutions refer to the talisman’s swaying and drawing during the summoning, revolving to the number seven, for seven is the number of generation.

The Jade Talisman notifies the Three Officials.
The Supreme Unity’s honored spirit notifies the Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water with the Jade Talisman. A person’s Primordial Spirit congeals, the Five Qi circulating through the Three Officials to gather at the crown and pay homage to the Primordial. Those who cultivate the Great Cavern’s Dao should remove their names from the Three Officials’ registers.

Extract the registers from the Three Paths below.
Command the Three Officials and Five Peaks to erase the names of the guilty from the registers of the Three Paths and Five Sufferings, pardoning and releasing them. The Three Paths and Five Sufferings together form the Eight Difficulties. Only when one departs from the Eight Difficulties may there be signs of rebirth.

Receive birth in the Lofty Supreme Constellation.
Those who cultivate the *Wenchang Great Cavern*’s Dao, transcending the Five Phases and Eight Trigrams, refine the lead and mercury within the body into the Elixir—when merit and practice are complete, the True Spirit naturally surpasses the Three Realms, receiving birth in the Lofty Supreme Constellation’s ultimate pole.

The Supreme Emperor of the Eight Spirits,
The Supreme Emperor is the essence-soul named Yangtang, styled Baling—“King” denotes reverence. The *Shengshen* states: “The Supreme Emperor is titled Yangtang, styled Baling Lord,” also called the Spirit of the Eight Consciousnesses. The Eight Spirits and Eight Sceneries are the completion numbers of wood.

One transformation returns the Auspicious Clouds.
From this single transformation, the Auspicious Clouds are drawn back to open the Gate of Life. The Elixir Canon states: “The double passes of the spine reach the crown gate—this is the root of the cultivation path.” The fire-timing of the Golden Elixir lies in personal inquiry; it cannot be conjectured.

Peach Health guards the Six Harmonies.
See the middle volume’s annotation on entering the essence of the Six Harmony Chambers. Peach Lord is the name of the kidney spirit. One should curb anger, restrain desire, cherish essence, and treasure qi, making them the master of the body and the root of life and destiny. When thoughts of lust arise, visualize Peach Health in the navel.

Restrain essence to fortify the Mud Pill.
Restraining essence follows a natural principle. If one employs the arts of the bedchamber, it is like cooking sand to make rice—though steamed for a thousand kalpas, it remains only hot sand, never rice. The *Huangting* states: “The brain spirit’s essence-root is the Mud Pill’s root.” The Former Master said: “This essence is not the essence of lust but the Primordial Supreme Essence, the Jade Emperor’s saliva. In seeking a master and inquiring into the Dao, one must fathom its mysteries. Though your wisdom surpasses Yan and Min, without a master’s transmission, do not rashly guess. The Three-One Imperial Ministers first restrain essence—one should visualize this spirit directing true qi into the brain’s Mud Pill and Six Harmonies.”

Observe the Eight Sceneries of the Grand Clarity.
The wondrous practice of the Observation Gate is all read in the falling tone. The internal observation of the Three Fields and Eight Sceneries refers to the Grand Clarity’s Lower Field. The *Scripture of Ascending to Heaven* states: “Draw the True Qi of Grand Harmony and focus the mind’s intent on the Three Fields and Eight Sceneries of the Elixir Field—this lies in a single gaze of the heart and eyes.”

Proclaim the True Writ of Ten Virtues.
The sages looked up and down to draw the Eight Trigrams, thereby communicating with the virtue of the numinous. The Primordial began to expound the Great Cavern’s True Writ to congeal the True Spirit, forming the virtue of humanity—its principle is one.
